# 5.3 PUCCH

**5.3.0-1**  (ID: `11452491`)

PUCCH
Document Owner

Dariusz Kobylarz

Additional support:

Wenjian Li

Sathiaseelan Sundaralingam

---

## 5.3.1 General

### 5.3.1.1 Functional split in 7-2e

#### 5.3.1.1.0-2 Functional split in 7-2e 5G-L1-UL shall follow the same functional split in 7-2e as in 7-2a for PUCCH channel. [CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e [End CB012115-GA] (ID: 12733525)

### 5.3.1.2 Name notation for PUCCH Receive messages.

#### 5.3.1.2.0-1 Name notation for PUCCH Receive messages. In the chapter dedicated to PUCCH when names of messages are used: UlData_PucchReceiveReq UlData_PucchReceiveRespPs UlData_PucchReceiveRespHarqD it means both messages: UlData_PucchReceiveReqL1sw and UlData_PucchReceiveReqLoner UlData_PucchReceiveRespPsL1sw and UlData_PucchReceiveRespPsLoner UlData_PucchReceiveRespHarqDL1sw and UlData_PucchReceiveRespHarqDLoner (ID: 13419888)

## 5.3.2 Start-up configuration

### 5.3.2.1 General

**5.3.2.1.0-2**  (ID: `12727376`)

General
Startup in Loner / Loki / Thor

During the startup, the 5G-L1-UL shall read the R&D parameter tables which holds the configurable parameters needed for PUCCH processing.

[CNI-108168-J] The requirement was refined under CNI-108168  [End CNI-108168-J]

---

### 5.3.2.2 RAD parameters

#### 5.3.2.2.1 Loki and Thor

##### 5.3.2.2.1.1 format0

###### 5.3.2.2.1.1.0-1 format0 rdPucchF0Thresholds4Rx (ID: 11452730)

**5.3.2.2.1.1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11452738`)

format0
rdPucchF0Thresholds4Rx

[From 5G20B]The values are defined in L1 internally in code as defined in 2.4.1.6 of 5Gmax algorithm specification document (5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and rdPucchF0Thresholds4Rx was NOT used as R&D parameter from [End 5G20B].

array of length 12

Value range: 0..3

Default value: {1.072, 1.183, 1.325, 1.462, 1.665, 1.80, 1.954, 2.121, 1.665, 1.80, 1.954, 2.121}

Unit: -

Step Size: 0.001

Specified in: 5G\_L1\_8359\_replaced([11456812](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAn-jfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Here is the definition of the thresholds:

* rdPucchF0Thresholds4Rx[0]: only SR over one OFDM symbol without Frequency Hopping
* rdPucchF0Thresholds4Rx[1]: only 1 bit HARQ-ACK (no SR allowed) over one OFDM symbol without Frequency Hopping
* rdPucchF0Thresholds4Rx[2]: only 2 bit HARQ-ACK (no SR allowed) or 1 bit HARQ-ACK + SR (positive or negative) over one OFDM symbol without Frequency Hopping
* rdPucchF0Thresholds4Rx[3]: 2 bit HARQ-ACK + SR (positive or negative) over one OFDM symbol without Frequency Hopping
* rdPucchF0Thresholds4Rx[4]: only SR over two OFDM symbols without Frequency Hopping
* rdPucchF0Thresholds4Rx[5]: only 1 bit HARQ-ACK (no SR allowed) over two OFDM symbols without Frequency Hopping
* rdPucchF0Thresholds4Rx[6]: only 2 bit HARQ-ACK (no SR allowed) or 1 bit HARQ-ACK + SR  over two OFDM symbols without Frequency Hopping
* rdPucchF0Thresholds4Rx[7]: 2 bit HARQ-ACK + SR over two OFDM symbols without Frequency Hopping
* rdPucchF0Thresholds4Rx[8]: only SR over two OFDM symbols with Frequency Hopping
* rdPucchF0Thresholds4Rx[9]: only 1 bit HARQ-ACK (no SR allowed) over two OFDM symbols with Frequency Hopping
* rdPucchF0Thresholds4Rx[10]: only 2 bit HARQ-ACK (no SR allowed) or 1 bit HARQ-ACK + SR  over two OFDM symbols with Frequency Hopping
* rdPucchF0Thresholds4Rx[11]: 2 bit HARQ-ACK + SR over two OFDM symbols with Frequency Hopping

---

###### 5.3.2.2.1.1.0-2 format0 rdPucchF0Thresholds2Rx (ID: 11452748)

**5.3.2.2.1.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11452758`)

format0
rdPucchF0Thresholds2Rx

[From 5G20B]

The values are defined in L1 internally in code as defined in 2.4.1.6 of 5Gmax algorithm specification document (5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and rdPucchF0Thresholds2Rx  was NOT used as R&D parameter [End 5G20B].

array of length 12

Value range: 0..3

Default value: {0.745, 0.850, 0.969, 1.098, 1.068, 1.205, 1.322, 1.460, 1.068, 1.205, 1.322, 1.460}

Unit: -

Step Size: 0.001

Specified in: 5G\_L1\_8359\_replaced([11456812](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAn-jfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Here is the definition of the thresholds:

* rdPucchF0Thresholds2Rx[0]: only SR over one OFDM symbol without Frequency Hopping
* rdPucchF0Thresholds2Rx[1]: only 1 bit HARQ-ACK (no SR allowed) over one OFDM symbol without Frequency Hopping
* rdPucchF0Thresholds2Rx[2]: only 2 bit HARQ-ACK (no SR allowed) or 1 bit HARQ-ACK + SR (positive or negative) over one OFDM symbol without Frequency Hopping
* rdPucchF0Thresholds2Rx[3]: 2 bit HARQ-ACK + SR (positive or negative) over one OFDM symbol without Frequency Hopping
* rdPucchF0Thresholds2Rx[4]: only SR over two OFDM symbols without Frequency Hopping
* rdPucchF0Thresholds2Rx[5]: only 1 bit HARQ-ACK (no SR allowed) over two OFDM symbols without Frequency Hopping
* rdPucchF0Thresholds2Rx[6]: only 2 bit HARQ-ACK (no SR allowed) or 1 bit HARQ-ACK + SR  over two OFDM symbols without Frequency Hopping
* rdPucchF0Thresholds2Rx[7]: 2 bit HARQ-ACK + SR over two OFDM symbols without Frequency Hopping
* rdPucchF0Thresholds2Rx[8]: only SR over two OFDM symbols with Frequency Hopping
* rdPucchF0Thresholds2Rx[9]: only 1 bit HARQ-ACK (no SR allowed) over two OFDM symbols with Frequency Hopping
* rdPucchF0Thresholds2Rx[10]: only 2 bit HARQ-ACK (no SR allowed) or 1 bit HARQ-ACK + SR  over two OFDM symbols with Frequency Hopping
* rdPucchF0Thresholds2Rx[11]: 2 bit HARQ-ACK + SR over two OFDM symbols with Frequency Hopping

###### 5.3.2.2.1.3.0-9 format2 pucchF2DtxThrFactor (ID: 11452948)

**5.3.2.2.1.3.0-9.0-1**  (ID: `11452956`)

format2
PUCCH F2 DTX threshold adjust factor

Value range: 1:0.05:5

Default value: 1.3 for number of PRB is greater than 1. Otherwise it shall be set to 1.

Unit: -

Online modifiable: Yes

Step Size: 0.05

These parameters are depicted in the following Table:

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Parameter Name |  | Case |  |  |
| pucchF2DtxThrFactorMultiPrbPolar |  | Polar code, numOfPrb > 1 |  |  |
|  | pucchF2DtxThrFactorMultiPrbRM |  | Reed-Muller code, numOfPrb > 1 |  |
|  | pucchF2DtxThrFactorOnePrbPolar |  | Polar code, numOfPrb = 1 |  |
|  | pucchF2DtxThrFactorOnePrbRM |  | Reed-Muller code, numOfPrb = 1 |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |

Here is the definition of the thresholds:

* rdPucchF0Thresholds4Rx[0]: only SR over one OFDM symbol without Frequency Hopping
* rdPucchF0Thresholds4Rx[1]: only 1 bit HARQ-ACK (no SR allowed) over one OFDM symbol without Frequency Hopping
* rdPucchF0Thresholds4Rx[2]: only 2 bit HARQ-ACK (no SR allowed) or 1 bit HARQ-ACK + SR (positive or negative) over one OFDM symbol without Frequency Hopping
* rdPucchF0Thresholds4Rx[3]: 2 bit HARQ-ACK + SR (positive or negative) over one OFDM symbol without Frequency Hopping
* rdPucchF0Thresholds4Rx[4]: only SR over two OFDM symbols without Frequency Hopping
* rdPucchF0Thresholds4Rx[5]: only 1 bit HARQ-ACK (no SR allowed) over two OFDM symbols without Frequency Hopping
* rdPucchF0Thresholds4Rx[6]: only 2 bit HARQ-ACK (no SR allowed) or 1 bit HARQ-ACK + SR  over two OFDM symbols without Frequency Hopping
* rdPucchF0Thresholds4Rx[7]: 2 bit HARQ-ACK + SR over two OFDM symbols without Frequency Hopping
* rdPucchF0Thresholds4Rx[8]: only SR over two OFDM symbols with Frequency Hopping
* rdPucchF0Thresholds4Rx[9]: only 1 bit HARQ-ACK (no SR allowed) over two OFDM symbols with Frequency Hopping
* rdPucchF0Thresholds4Rx[10]: only 2 bit HARQ-ACK (no SR allowed) or 1 bit HARQ-ACK + SR  over two OFDM symbols with Frequency Hopping
* rdPucchF0Thresholds4Rx[11]: 2 bit HARQ-ACK + SR over two OFDM symbols with Frequency Hopping

rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMrc

As defined in 2.4.2.8 of 5Gmax algorithm specification document (5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) DTX detection threshold of PUCCH format 1 (MRC)

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | No multiplexing |  | multiplexing HARQ-ACK/CSI and SR |  |  |
| No frequency hopping | frequency hopping | No frequency hopping for both HARQ-ACK resource and SR resource | frequency hopping for both HARQ-ACK resource and SR resource | One hopping and one without hopping |  |
| threshold | 1400 | 1050 | 1900 | 1250 | 1500 |

array of length 5

Value range: 1000..2000

Default value: {1400, 1050, 1900, 1250, 1500}

## 5.3.3 Cell configuration

### 5.3.3.1 Overview

#### 5.3.3.1.0-1 Overview Cell specific parameters (ID: 11453440)

**5.3.3.1.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `12727602`)

Overview
5G-L1-UL shall support the L1L3 interface and following messages for PUCCH (with cell specific parameters):

-L1L3: UlCell\_SetupReq ([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

-L1L3: UlCell\_SetupResp ([11513515](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRxIyvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

-L1L3: UlCell\_ParameterReconfigurationReq ([11513565](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRxv0vvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

-L1L3: UlCell\_ParameterReconfigurationResp ([11513574](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRxv1PvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

### 5.3.3.2 Group and sequence hopping

**5.3.3.2.0-3**  (ID: `12732125`)

Group and sequence hopping
12732125:
Group and sequence hopping
12732125:
Group and sequence hopping
12732125:
Group and sequence hopping
12732125:
Group and sequence hopping
5G-L1-UL shall support following group and sequence hopping configuration:

According to 3GPP 38.211 section 6.3.2.2

- pucch-GroupHopping = 'neither' is supported

- hoppingId : 5G-L1-UL shall receive via parameter UlCell\_SetupReq->pucchHoppingId  (see: [11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) )

Note:

1. The higher layer parameter hoppingId is configured and set to physical cell ID, which means [image-0][image\_desc]n\_ID = N\_ID^cell[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m4dng\_5G\_UP\_External\_Interfaces\_file\_645.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0].
2. Parameter pucchHoppingId is used to selection of the base sequence to generate [ZC](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_6Dz7YHO5EfCRE7eh4Ndkrw) (Zadoff-Chu) sequence (format 0,1 and 3).

3. Parameter pucch-GroupHopping is not modifiable.

1. Not supported configuration:

- pucch-GroupHopping = ''enabled'

- pucch-GroupHopping = 'disabled'

1. For conformance test:

- pucch-GroupHopping = 'neither'

- hoppingId = 0

1. For reference please see: ([11496456](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tSFqR_v1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

### 5.3.3.3 Robustness

## 5.3.4 Dynamic configuration

### 5.3.4.1 PUCCH messages

#### 5.3.4.1.1 Overview

###### 5.3.4.1.1.1 Loki / Thor / Odin

**5.3.4.1.1.1.0-2**  (ID: `12727452`)

Loki / Thor / Odin
5G-L1-UL shall support the L1L2 interface and following messages for PUCCH :

-L1L2: UlData\_PucchReceiveReqL1sw ([11513979](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MHvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

-L1L2: UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPsL1sw ([11514171](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR1aQ_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

-L1L2: UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqDL1sw ([11514243](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BT_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

#### 5.3.4.1.2 Receive Request from L2PS

##### 5.3.4.1.2.1 Parameter isServingSubcell for supercell

**5.3.4.1.2.1.0-2**  (ID: `13374648`)

Parameter isServingSubcell for supercell
Upon reception of the IE "isServingSubcell" in message UlData\_PucchReceiveReq ([11514105](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR1aNPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)), 5G-L1-UL shall determine whether PUCCH format3 resource should be processing:

* Decode+Measurement (isServingSubcell =true)
* or only selected Measurement for non-serving FDD Supercell subcell (isServingSubcell =false).

For details please find: ([11454745: FDD Supercell](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAe0nfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

Note:

In case of FDD supercell, PUCCH format3 resources allocation parameters are broadcasted to all subcells of the supercell through the UlData\_PucchReceiveReqL1sw messages; but  for a given PUCCH format3 resource, only one subcell may receive parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->isServingSubcell with value "true" (for others subcells parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->isServingSubcell equals "false").

[CNI-108168-J] The requirement was refined under CNI-108168  [End CNI-108168-J]

---

##### 5.3.4.1.2.2 Parameter harqProcessIndex

**5.3.4.1.2.2.0-2**  (ID: `12727501`)

Parameter harqProcessIndex
5G-L1-UL shall support a new value ID = 100 in harqProcessIndex IE in UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message from L2.

The value range to be supported is [0..15,100].

5G-L1-UL supports 16 HARQ processes, indices [ 0 .. 15], defined by 3GPP. In addition, HARQ process index 100 is used to indicate the existence of UL CA for L1.

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

##### 5.3.4.1.2.3 Parameter l2CtxtAnMgt

**5.3.4.1.2.3.0-4**  (ID: `12727498`)

Parameter l2CtxtAnMgt
5G-L1-UL shall support the reception of parameter from L2-PS:

UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->l2CtxtAnMgt

This enabler content is private of 5G-L2-PS, and 5G-L1-UL shall only copy it from the request message UlData\_PucchReceiveReq and send it back in the response message UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD to 5G-L2-PS.

Note:

This parameter is used for supporting enhancement enabler for Inter Band CA between CCs with different numerologies.

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

##### 5.3.4.1.2.4 Configuration of parameters: srBitDetection, nANPucch and numOfBitsOfUciInformation for PUCCH

###### 5.3.4.1.2.4.1 Format0

**5.3.4.1.2.4.1.0-2**  (ID: `13379712`)

Format0
For PUCCH format0 5G-L1-UL shall support following configuration of parameters srBitDetection, nANPucch and numOfBitsOfUciInformation (from UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message).

The srBit is not included in the numOfBitsOfUciInformation.  
The numOfBitsOfUciInformation is set to the same as nANPucch if the UCI is used for HARQ ack report. e.g. in case of 1 bit AN (nANPucch = 1)

There are following cases:

* SR is multiplexed with HARQ feedback (same starting symbol)
* numOfBitsOfUciInformation=1,
* srBitDetection is set to ’true’,
* nANPucch is set to ‘1’
* SR only
* numOfBitsOfUciInformation=0,
* srBitDetection is set to ’true’,
* nANPucch is set to ‘0’
* HARQ A/N only
* numOfBitsOfUciInformation=1,
* srBitDetection is set to ’false’,
* nANPucch is set to ‘1’

Note:

1. For detailed specification of parameters srBitDetection, nANPucch and numOfBitsOfUciInformation please find: ([11513979](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MHvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))
2. For UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message filling for format0 by L2-PS please refer ([11180313: PUCCH format 0](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27Lj7vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

[CNI-108168-J] The requirement was refined under CNI-108168  [End CNI-108168-J]

---

###### 5.3.4.1.2.4.2 Format1

**5.3.4.1.2.4.2.0-3**  (ID: `12730649`)

Format1
For FR1-TDD and FR1-FDD for PUCCH format1 5G-L1-UL shall support following configuration of parameters srBitDetection, nANPucch and numOfBitsOfUciInformation (from UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message).

* 1 SR bit only
* Single PUCCH only:
  + srBitDetection = 1,
  + nANPucch = 0,
  + numOfBitsOfUciInformation = 0

DTX threshold: first column in DTX detection threshold table [14.1]

* 1 bit AN only
* Single PUCCH only:
  + srBitDetection = 0,
  + nANPucch = 1,
  + numOfBitsOfUciInformation = 1

DTX threshold: second column in DTX detection threshold table [15.7]

* 2 bit AN only
* Single PUCCH only:
  + srBitDetection = 0,
  + nANPucch = 2,
  + numOfBitsOfUciInformation = 2

DTX threshold: previous to last column in DTX detection threshold table [17.2]

* 1 bit AN + 1 SR bit
* PUCCH on SR resource:
  + srBitDetection = 1,
  + nANPucch = 1,
  + numOfBitsOfUciInformation = 2
* PUCCH on AN resource:
  + srBitDetection = 0,
  + nANPucch = 1,
  + numOfBitsOfUciInformation = 2

DTX threshold: previous to last column in DTX detection threshold table [17.2]

* 2 bit AN + 1 SR bit
* PUCCH on SR resource:
  + srBitDetection = 1,
  + nANPucch = 2,
  + numOfBitsOfUciInformation = 3
* PUCCH on AN resource:
  + srBitDetection = 0,
  + nANPucch = 2,
  + numOfBitsOfUciInformation = 3

DTX threshold: last column in DTX detection threshold table [18.8]

The IE srBitDetection is set to TRUE if the PUCCH Format1 is related to an SR resource and set to FALSE if the PUCCH Format 1 is related to a HARQ A/N resource or HARQ A/N of Msg4/SRB0.

If nANPucch > 0 then IE numOfBitsOfUciInformation shall be set to nANPucch + number of expected SR bits, else IE numOfBitsOfUciInformation shall be set to zero (SR only).

Note:

1. numOfBitsOfUciInformation is used by 5G-L1-UL to select correct DTX threshold.

Below there is example for part of table with DTX detection threshold of PUCCH format 1 (MLD)  for 2RX w/o [FH](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_81YX4HK4EfCRE7eh4Ndkrw). The thresholds correspond to the above configurations.

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | SR only | 1bit HARQ-ACK | 2 bit HARQ-ACK or multiplexing 1 bit HARQ-ACK and SR | multiplexing 2 bit HARQ-ACK and SR |
| 2Rx no frequency hopping | 14.1 | 15.7 | 17.2 | 18.8 |

1. For detailed specification of parameters srBitDetection, nANPucch and numOfBitsOfUciInformation please find: ([11513979](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MHvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))
2. For complete [DTX](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_e858kHMWEfCRE7eh4Ndkrw) detection threshold table please find section  2.4.2.8  of the 5Gmax algorithm specification.
3. For UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message filling for format1 by L2-PS please refer ([11180342: PUCCH format 1](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27MK8_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

##### 5.3.4.1.2.5 bufferedUlStruct

**5.3.4.1.2.5.0-1**  (ID: `11453828`)

bufferedUlStruct
L1-SW shall receive UlData\_PucchReceiveReq messages containing, per subcell, in the IE bufferedUlStruct which provides the actual time to process PUCCH of this subcell, 3 new IEs,

bufferedUlStruct.processInRealTime which is of type Bool, where True indicates data process in RT (i.e., same as air interface time given by SFN and Slot IEs), and False indicates data process in NRT (for FDD, RT processing is relevant, i.e., processInRealTime is set to True);

bufferedUlStruct.sfnForProcessing which is of type u16 [0..1023], which indicates the SFN to process the data in RT or NRT;

bufferedUlStruct.slotForProcessing which is of type u8 [0..79], which indicates the Slot to process the data in RT or NRT.

Note that as up to 4 C2/D2 type subcells can be scheduled in a slot, up to 4 UlData\_PucchReceiveReq messages can be received by L1-SW.x

---

##### 5.3.4.1.2.6 Robustness

###### 5.3.4.1.2.6.1 Parameter longTermCfoMetricOfBeam

**5.3.4.1.2.6.1.0-3**  (ID: `12727502`)

Parameter longTermCfoMetricOfBeam
To help L2-PS to maintain LT CFO functionality for 2RX, 4RX, 8RX,  5G-L1-UL shall ensure LT CFO protection for reception of 0+j0 from L2-PS:

- For 5G-L1-UL, assume frequency offset equals 0Hz if LT CFO == 0+j0 is received.

- For L2-PS, when using 0+j0 for LT CFO reset, no validity check is performed anymore (i.e., not modify value 0 to 1.0 in purpose).

Note: it is also possible that only some antennas (i.e., two of total four) have LT CFO == 0+j0, while other antennas have non-zero values.

For details see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9896\_replaced([11102750](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_knm7UvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

###### 5.3.4.1.2.6.2 numOfLayers validation

**5.3.4.1.2.6.2.0-1**  (ID: `12729412`)

numOfLayers validation
5G-L1-UL (BB) shall validate that parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->numOfLayers is set to 1

If numOfLayers is not equal to 1, 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall drop the request and log unique error.

Note: this requirement is derived from interface definition [11513990](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_P6U4UPvwEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)

---

###### 5.3.4.1.2.6.3 modulationType validation

**5.3.4.1.2.6.3.0-1**  (ID: `12729516`)

modulationType validation
5G-L1-UL (BB) shall validate that parameter modulationType  is BPSK, if UlData\_PucchReceiveReq was received with:

* UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->pucchFormat = Format3
* UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->dmrsSequenceType = type2

If modulationType is not BPSK, 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall drop the request and log unique error.

Note: this requirement is derived from interface definition [11514084](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_Q5X6gPvwEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)

---

###### 5.3.4.1.2.6.4 startPrb and numOfPrb validation

**5.3.4.1.2.6.4.0-1**  (ID: `12729544`)

startPrb and numOfPrb validation
5G-L1-UL (BB) shall validate that sum of parameters UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->startPrb and UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->numOfPrb in not higher or equal to ulBandwidth

If this sum is higher, 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall drop the request and log unique error.

Note:

1. ulBandwidth is the maximum PRB number in the given bandwidth

2. this requirement is derived from interface definition [11514084](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_Q5X6gPvwEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)

---

###### 5.3.4.1.2.6.5 firstSymbol and numOfsymbols validation

**5.3.4.1.2.6.5.0-1**  (ID: `12729550`)

firstSymbol and numOfsymbols validation
5G-L1-UL (BB) shall validate that sum parameters of UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->firstSymbol and UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->numOfSymbols is not higher than 14

If this sum is higher, 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall drop the request and log unique error.

Note: this requirement is derived from interface definition [11514084](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_Q5X6gPvwEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)

---

###### 5.3.4.1.2.6.6 nANPucch validation

**5.3.4.1.2.6.6.0-1**  (ID: `12729558`)

nANPucch validation
5G-L1-UL (BB) shall validate that parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->nANPucch in not higher than 2, if UlData\_PucchReceiveReq was received with:

* UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->pucchFormat = Format0 or Format1

If nANPucch is higher than 2, 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall drop the request and log unique error.

Note: this requirement is derived from interface definition [11514147](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_RiE5QPvwEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)

---

###### 5.3.4.1.2.6.7 numOfbitsUciinformation validation

###### 5.3.4.1.2.6.7.0-1 numOfbitsUciinformation validation Format0 (ID: 12743547)

**5.3.4.1.2.6.7.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `12729561`)

numOfbitsUciinformation validation
5G-L1-UL (BB) shall validate that parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->numOfBitsOfUciInformation is not higher than 2, if UlData\_PucchReceiveReq was received with:

* UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->pucchFormat = Format0

If numOfbitsUciinformationis higher than 2, 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall drop the request and log unique error.

Note: this requirement is derived from interface definition [11514147](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_RiE5QPvwEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)

---

###### 5.3.4.1.2.6.7.0-2 numOfbitsUciinformation validation Format1 (ID: 12743549)

**5.3.4.1.2.6.7.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `12743525`)

numOfbitsUciinformation validation
5G-L1-UL (BB) shall validate that parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->numOfBitsOfUciInformation is not higher than 3, if UlData\_PucchReceiveReq was received with:

* UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->pucchFormat = Format1

If numOfbitsUciinformationis higher than 3, 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall drop the request and log unique error.

Note: this requirement is derived from interface definition [11514147](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_RiE5QPvwEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)

---

##### 5.3.4.1.2.7 Frozen Requirements

###### 5.3.4.1.2.7.1 Parameter harqProcessIndex (UlData_PucchReceiveRespPs)

###### 5.3.4.1.2.7.1.0-2 Parameter harqProcessIndex (UlData_PucchReceiveRespPs) Loner (ID: 11454166)

**5.3.4.1.2.7.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11454174`)

Parameter harqProcessIndex (UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs)
L1 PHYUL shall support a new value ID = 100 in harqProcessIndex IE in UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs and UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD messages sent to L2. The value range to be supported is [0..15,100]. Even though according to 3GPP only 16 harq processes ([0..15]) are supported, value 100 is not a real harq process index and this value is not communicated to the UE, but rather it is only an indicator between L1 and L2 regarding the existence of UL CA and L1 shall return value 100 to L2.

---

###### 5.3.4.1.2.7.1.0-3 Parameter harqProcessIndex (UlData_PucchReceiveRespPs) Loki (ID: 11454181)

**5.3.4.1.2.7.1.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11454188`)

Parameter harqProcessIndex (UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs)
L1 PHYUL shall support a new value ID = 100 in harqProcessIndex IE in UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs and UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD messages sent to L2. The value range to be supported is [0..15,100]. Even though according to 3GPP only 16 harq processes ([0..15]) are supported, value 100 is not a real harq process index and this value is not communicated to the UE, but rather it is only an indicator between L1 and L2 regarding the existence of UL CA and L1 shall return value 100 to L2.

---

###### 5.3.4.1.2.7.1.0-4 Parameter harqProcessIndex (UlData_PucchReceiveRespPs) Thor (ID: 11454196)

**5.3.4.1.2.7.1.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11454204`)

Parameter harqProcessIndex (UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs)
L1 PHYUL shall support a new value ID = 100 in harqProcessIndex IE in UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs and UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD messages sent to L2. The value range to be supported is [0..15,100]. Even though according to 3GPP only 16 harq processes ([0..15]) are supported, value 100 is not a real harq process index and this value is not communicated to the UE, but rather it is only an indicator between L1 and L2 regarding the existence of UL CA and L1 shall return value 100 to L2.

[CB011178-A] 5G-L1-UL shall also support requirements above for FR1 FDD 7-2a eCPRI for Thor. [End CB011178-A]

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
|  | Thor |
| FR1-FDD-CPRI | Supported |
| FR1-FDD-7-2a-eCPRI | [CB011178-A] Supported [End CB011178-A] |
| FR1-FDD-OBSAI | [CB010969-SR-CB] Supported [End CB010969-SR-CB] |

---

#### 5.3.4.1.3 Receive Response to L2PS

##### 5.3.4.1.3.1 Parameter srBit

**5.3.4.1.3.1.0-2**  (ID: `12731252`)

Parameter srBit
5G-L1-UL shall set parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->srBit as following:

In case of format2 and format3, all information (e.g. including srBit) is included as physical bits, srBit is multiplexed with CSI bits and/or HarqAN bits.

For format2 and format3, the numOfBitsOfUciInformation includes the srBit.

In case of format0 and format1 srBit is not transmitted as a physical bit.

For implementation convenient 5G-L1-UL is expected to follow different representation in case of format1.

Please see the next sections for the details.

srBitDetection [IE](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_2GtM4HMaEfCRE7eh4Ndkrw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) from UlData\_PucchReceiveReq informs whether SR detection shall be performed in the 5G-L1-UL.

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| format | UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->srBitDetection |
| format0 | Can be set either to enabled or disabled |
| format1 | Can be set either to enabled or disabled |
| format2 | Set to invalid. |
| format3 | Can be set either to invalid or disabled |

srBit IE in UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs(7) message depending on PUCCH format is set according to below table:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| format | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->srBit(7) |
| format0 | \* Can be set to invalid when srBitDetection is set to disabled. \* Can have value either 0 or 1 depending on the detection result. |
| format1 | \* when IE nANPucch > 0 and srBitDetection is set to "enabled" (SR+HARQ-AckNack case) {numOfBitsOfUciInformation= nANPucch + number of expected SR bits }, srBit is set to 1. \* when IE nANPucch > 0 and srBitDetection is set to "disabled" (SR+HARQ-AckNack case) {numOfBitsOfUciInformation= nANPucch+ number of expected SR bits }, srBit is set to 0. \* when IE nANPucch = 0 and srBitDetection is set to "enabled"(SR-only case) {numOfBitsOfUciInformation= nANPucch =0}, srBit is set to 1. \* when IE nANPucch > 0 and srBitDetection is set to "disabled" (AckNack case)  {numOfBitsOfUciInformation= nANPucch}, srBit is set to "invalid" |
| format2 | Set to invalid. |
| format3 | Set to invalid. |

Note:

1. For format1 the IE srBit is used to distinguish the PUCCH related to SR and the PUCCH related to PUCCH Resource Set0. For details see ([11187513](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvbamfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))
2. For format2 and format3 when SR bit is multiplexed with the CSI report, regardless the setting of srBitDetection IE, 5G-L1-UL decodes the numOfBitsOfUciInformation and passes them transparently as bit string to L2-PS in UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs . Whether SR is transmitted via  PUCCH or not is transparent to 5G-L1-UL.
3. For detailed specification of parameters srBit please find: ([11513979](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MHvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
4. For UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message filling by L2-PS please refer ([11180309](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27Lj7fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) ).
5. For format0 IE srBitDetection is set to false for MSG4 ACK.
6. For format0 IE srBitDetection is set to false in conformance tests
7. Parameter srBit is also sent in message UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqDL1sw (not for Loner). For specification of srBit parameter in this message see: ([11514255: ULData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqDL1sw](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BUvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))
8. For format0 SR bit is not multiplexed with the CSI report, decoded SR bit (format0) is located in the srBit IE in UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs message.

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e.  [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

##### 5.3.4.1.3.2 Parameter numOfBitsOfUciInformation.

**5.3.4.1.3.2.0-2**  (ID: `12727509`)

Parameter numOfBitsOfUciInformation.
The 5G-L1-UL shall report the number of sent UCI bits in UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->subcells->pucchResources->numOfBitsOfUciInformation.

The value of UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->subcells->pucchResources->numOfBitsOfUciInformation  shall be copied from UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->subcells->pucchResources->numOfBitsOfUCIInformation .

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

##### 5.3.4.1.3.3 Parameter harqProcessIndex

**5.3.4.1.3.3.0-2**  (ID: `12727507`)

Parameter harqProcessIndex
5G-L1-UL shall support a new value ID = 100 in harqProcessIndex IE in UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs  and UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD messages sent to L2.

The value range to be supported is [0..15,100].

5G-L1-UL supports 16 HARQ processes, indices [ 0 .. 15], defined by 3GPP. In addition, HARQ process index 100 is used to indicate the existence of UL CA for L1.

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

##### 5.3.4.1.3.4 BufferedUlResp structure

**5.3.4.1.3.4.0-1**  (ID: `11454222`)

BufferedUlResp structure
L1-SW shall send a single UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs message per subcell (no bundle) to 5G-L2-PS containing, for all subcells receiving PUCCH in the slot, in the IE bufferedUlRespStruct, 3 new IEs,

bufferedUlRespStruct.processInRealTime which is of type Bool, where True indicates PUCCH process was done in RT (i.e., same as air interface time given by SFN and Slot IEs), and False indicates PUCCH process was done in NRT (for FDD, RT processing is relevant, i.e., processInRealTime is set to True);

bufferedUlRespStruct.sfnForProcessing which is of type u16 [0..1023], which indicates the SFN at which PUCCH processing was done;

bufferedUlRespStruct.slotForProcessing which is of type u8 [0..79], which indicates the Slot at which PUCCH processing was done.

SubcellId parameter shall support any value 0 through 7 for Loner. Please refer to ([11375846: subcellId](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueQLIfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) and [11375909: ulSubcellIdMax maximum value](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueQLKvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) ) for detail. Note that this structure is also used in UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD.

---

###### 5.3.4.1.3.5.2 Time Offset Estimation Invalid Values

###### 5.3.4.1.3.5.2.1 General

**5.3.4.1.3.5.2.1.0-2**  (ID: `12732455`)

General
5G-L1-UL shall support Invalid Values for Short Term Time Offset measurements as following:

Invalid value of UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->shortTermTaMetric shall be set to −32768.

Invalid value of UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->shortTermTaPeakAmp shall be set to −1.

5G-L1-UL shall report invalid measurement for ST TA Metric and its associated Peak Amplitude if:

* the estimate is out of the allowed range or,
* in case PUCCH format0 (UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->pucchFormat value equals 0='PUCCH\_FORMAT\_0') or,
* in case PUCCH format1 (UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->pucchFormat value equals 1='PUCCH\_FORMAT\_1') or,
* in case PUCCH format2 with 1 or 2 PRBs (UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->pucchFormat value equals 2='PUCCH\_FORMAT\_2' and UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->numOfPrb value in range [1,2])

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

###### 5.3.4.1.3.5.3 RSSI measurement Invalid Values

###### 5.3.4.1.3.5.3.1 General

**5.3.4.1.3.5.3.1.0-2**  (ID: `12732452`)

General
5G-L1-UL shall support Invalid Values for [RSSI](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_CtgTJmbXEfCwWbD4x7Iu-g) measurement as following:

Invalid value of UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->rssi shall be set to -140dBm .

5G-L1-UL shall report invalid measurement for RSSI if:

* zero-valued samples got from the radio module or (e)CPRI interface for all the receiving antennas (meaning "spatial-stream-wise" as per ([11107886](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koj9lvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), typically the case of broken antenna, or noisy measurements

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

###### 5.3.4.1.3.5.4 Received Power measurement Invalid Values

###### 5.3.4.1.3.5.4.1 General

**5.3.4.1.3.5.4.1.0-2**  (ID: `12732458`)

General
5G-L1-UL shall support Invalid Values for Received Power measurement as following:

Invalid value of UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->rxPower shall be set to -140dBm .

5G-L1-UL shall report invalid measurement for Received Power if:

* zero-valued samples got from the radio module or (e)CPRI interface for all the receiving antennas (meaning "spatial-stream-wise" as per ([11107886](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koj9lvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), typically the case of broken antenna, or noisy measurements

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

###### 5.3.4.1.3.5.5 SINR measurement Invalid Values

###### 5.3.4.1.3.5.5.1 General

**5.3.4.1.3.5.5.1.0-2**  (ID: `12732460`)

General
5G-L1-UL shall support Invalid Values for [SINR](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_qVlYEHPyEfCRE7eh4Ndkrw) measurement as following:

Invalid value of UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->sinr shall be set to -255dB .

5G-L1-UL shall report invalid measurement for SINR if:

* the measurement can't be computed for the current configuration (example: SINR for 2nd layer when all PUCCH formats support only one layer)

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

###### 5.3.4.1.3.5.8 Short Term Frequency Offset Estimation Invalid Values

**5.3.4.1.3.5.8.0-1**  (ID: `13378500`)

Short Term Frequency Offset Estimation Invalid Values
For PUCCH format3 5G-L1-UL shall support Invalid Values for Short Term Frequency Offset Estimation (ST FOE) as following:

Invalid value of UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->shortTermCfoMetric shall be set to (0+0j).

5G-L1-UL shall report invalid measurement ST FOE if:

* the measurement can't be computed for the current configuration (configuration for PUCCH format3 with additional DMRS, when the number of PUCCH symbols is lower than 10 (i.e. < 10))

Refer to ([11109726](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ko7J_PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and ([11109794](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ko8YGPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Message detail is defined in ([11514200: PucchRespPsMeas structure](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BRfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).

---

###### 5.3.4.1.3.5.9 Antenna-wise ST Frequency Offset Estimation Invalid Values

**5.3.4.1.3.5.9.0-1**  (ID: `13378499`)

Antenna-wise ST Frequency Offset Estimation Invalid Values
For PUCCH format3 5G-L1-UL shall support Invalid Values for Antenna-wise ST Frequency Offset Estimation (antenna-wise FOE) as following:

Invalid value of UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->extendedParameters->shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt shall be set to (0+0j).

5G-L1-UL shall report invalid measurement for antenna-wise ST FOE if:

* zero-valued samples got from the radio module or (e)CPRI interface for all the receiving antennas (meaning "spatial-stream-wise" as per ([11107886](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koj9lvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), typically the case of broken antenna, or noisy measurements).

Refer to ([11109726](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ko7J_PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and ([11109794](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ko8YGPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Message detail is described in ([11514174: PUCCH Receive Response PS message content](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BQPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).

---

###### 5.3.4.1.3.5.10 Parameters for non-serving subcell in FDD supercell

**5.3.4.1.3.5.10.0-2**  (ID: `12709940`)

Parameters for non-serving subcell in FDD supercell
5G-L1-UL shall report following values for following measurements when UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->isServingSubcell value equals 'false' :

Values for parameters for non-serving subcell in FDD supercell:

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Report / Measurement | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs parameter | value |
| UCI bits | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->uciBits | (0) |
| DTX state | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->dtx | {NON\_DTX=0} |
| DTX metric | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->dtxMetric | {NON\_DTX=0} |
| DTX threshold | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->dtxThreshold | {NON\_DTX=0} |
| CRC state | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->crc | {NOK=1} |
| Noise Power per PRB | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->noisePerPrb | (-140) |
| ST TA metric | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->shortTermTaMetric | (-32768) |
| ST TA peak amplitude | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->shortTermTaPeakAmp | (-1) |
| RSSI | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->rssi | (-140) |
| ST FO metric | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->shortTermCfoMetric | (0+0j) |
| antenna-wise  ST FO | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->extendedParameters->shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt | (0+0j) |

[CNI-108168-J] The requirement was refined under CNI-108168  [End CNI-108168-J]

##### 5.3.4.1.3.6 Robustness

###### 5.3.4.1.3.6.1 Parameter sinr

###### 5.3.4.1.3.6.1.1 Loki / Thor / Odin

**5.3.4.1.3.6.1.1.0-2**  (ID: `13105309`)

Loki / Thor / Odin
For PUCCH format2 and PUCCH format3 5G-L1-UL shall ensure that the value of result of sinr measurement reported via parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->sinr does not exceed the range [-20..+40] dB.

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

###### 5.3.4.1.3.6.1.2 Recalculation of SINR (Loner)

**5.3.4.1.3.6.1.2.0-2**  (ID: `13390849`)

Recalculation of SINR (Loner)
To avoid unrealistic SINR values (e.g. SINR = -150 dB)in the L1L2 interface (in the UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs message) for PUCCH format0 and format1, the 5G-L1-UL shall do the following check:

if (final\_rxPower\_pucchF0F1 after conversion to dBm < -140) {

set the final rxPower\_pucchF0F1 after conversion to dBm as -140 dBm.

recalculate the SINR as SINR = final\_rxPower\_pucchF0F1 - noisePower\_dBm;

}

Where final\_rxPower\_pucchF0F1 refers to rxPower reported to L1L2 in the UlData\_PucchReceivRespPs message.

[CNI-108168-J] The requirement was refined under CNI-108168  [End CNI-108168-J]

---

##### 5.3.4.1.3.7 Frozen Requirements

###### 5.3.4.1.3.7.0-1 Frozen Requirements Parameter harqProcessIndex (UlData_PucchReceiveReq) (ID: 11453639)

**5.3.4.1.3.7.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11453866`)

Frozen Requirements
Loner

---

**5.3.4.1.3.7.0-1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11453875`)

Frozen Requirements
L1 PHYUL shall support a new value ID = 100 in harqProcessIndex IE in UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message from L2. The value range to be supported is [0..15,100]. Even though according to 3GPP only 16 harq processes ([0..15]) are supported, value 100 is not a real harq process index and this value is not communicated to the UE, but rather it is only an indicator to L1 regarding the existence of UL CA.

---

**5.3.4.1.3.7.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11453882`)

Frozen Requirements
Loki

---

**5.3.4.1.3.7.0-1.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11453891`)

Frozen Requirements
L1 PHYUL shall support a new value ID = 100 in harqProcessIndex IE in UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message from L2. The value range to be supported is [0..15,100]. Even though according to 3GPP only 16 harq processes ([0..15]) are supported, value 100 is not a real harq process index and this value is not communicated to the UE, but rather it is only an indicator to L1 regarding the existence of UL CA.

Frozen Requirements
Thor

Frozen Requirements
L1 PHYUL shall support a new value ID = 100 in harqProcessIndex IE in UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message from L2. The value range to be supported is [0..15,100]. Even though according to 3GPP only 16 harq processes ([0..15]) are supported, value 100 is not a real harq process index and this value is not communicated to the UE, but rather it is only an indicator to L1 regarding the existence of UL CA.

###### 5.3.4.1.3.7.0-2.2 Frequency Offset Estimation Invalid Values Frequency Offset Estimation Invalid Values Frequency Offset Estimation Invalid Values (ID: 13378498)

**5.3.4.1.3.7.0-2.2.1.0-1**  (ID: `11454103`)

Case of additional DMRS for format3
Loki

---

**5.3.4.1.3.7.0-2.2.1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11454110`)

Case of additional DMRS for format3
For PUCCH format 3 with additional DMRS, when the number of PUCCH symbols is lower than 10 (i.e. < 10), 5G-L1-UL shall report invalid FOE result (i.e. 0+j0).

Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29003\_replaced([11109726](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ko7J_PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29002\_replaced([11109794](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ko8YGPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Case of additional DMRS for format3
For Thor

---

**5.3.4.1.3.7.0-2.2.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11454125`)

Case of additional DMRS for format3
For PUCCH format 3 with additional DMRS, when the number of PUCCH symbols is lower than 10 (i.e. < 10), 5G-L1-UL shall report invalid FOE result (i.e. 0+j0).

Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29003\_replaced([11109726](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ko7J_PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29002\_replaced([11109794](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ko8YGPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**5.3.4.1.3.7.0-2.2.2.0-1**  (ID: `11458181`)

Case of Broken Rx
Loki

---

**5.3.4.1.3.7.0-2.2.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11458191`)

Case of Broken Rx
For each scheduled UE on PUCCH, 5G-L1-UL estimates a short term (ST) antenna-wise FOE metric on PUCCH Format3. 5G-L1-UL shall report invalid measurement for antenna-wise FOE(shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt) with message UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs when the Rx is failed (typically the case of RU lost or fiber broken or Rx failure).

Message detail is defined in 5G\_L1\_IF\_221\_replaced([11514182](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BQvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Invalid value of shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt shall be set to 0+0j (both real and imaginary parts set to zero).

---

**5.3.4.1.3.7.0-2.2.2.0-2**  (ID: `11458201`)

Case of Broken Rx
Thor

---

**5.3.4.1.3.7.0-2.2.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11458209`)

Case of Broken Rx
For each scheduled UE on PUCCH, 5G-L1-UL estimates a short term (ST) antenna-wise FOE metric on PUCCH Format3. 5G-L1-UL shall report invalid measurement for antenna-wise FOE(shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt) with message UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs when the Rx is failed (typically the case of RU lost or fiber broken or Rx failure).

Message detail is defined in 5G\_L1\_IF\_221\_replaced([11514182](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BQvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Invalid value of shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt shall be set to 0+0j (both real and imaginary parts set to zero).

[CB010575-D] The requirement is also applicable for L1 Thor for FR1-TDD-CPRI [End CB010575-D]

[CB009514-F] The requirement is also applicable for Thor(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e [End CB009514-F]

#### 5.3.4.1.4 Receive Response for HARQ to L2PS

##### 5.3.4.1.4.1 srBit

**5.3.4.1.4.1.0-2**  (ID: `13390891`)

srBit
5G-L1-UL shall send to 5G-L2-PS parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqDL1sw->Subcells->PucchResources->srBit as copy of parameter: UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPsL1sw->Subcells->PucchResources->srBit

The scheme of setting of srBit parameter is described in: ([11453947: Parameter srBit](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAbKM_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

For specification of parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqDL1sw->Subcells->PucchResources->srBit see: ([11514255: ULData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqDL1sw](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BUvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

##### 5.3.4.1.4.2 Robustness

### 5.3.4.2 Specific PUCCH configuration

#### 5.3.4.2.1 L1 call

##### 5.3.4.2.1.1 FR1-TDD

###### 5.3.4.2.1.1.1 L1/L3 call for FR1-TDD-eCPRI-7.2a for Odin

**5.3.4.2.1.1.1.0-1**  (ID: `12732468`)

L1/L3 call for FR1-TDD-eCPRI-7.2a for Odin
5G-L1-UL on Odin BB shall process PUCCH with the following configuration for L1/L3 call under CB012115-I for FR1-TDD-eCPRI-7.2a:

Format: long: format1 and format3

PUCCH start symbol = 0

PUCCH number of symbols = 14

OCC for format1 : {0}

Number of PRBs = 1 - for format1; 1..5  - for format3

PUCCH UCI bits: {1, 2} - for format1; [3..50]  - for format3

Bandwidth = 100MHz

Capacity: 8 resource per subcell for format1,  4 resources per subcell for format3

DMRS: Low-PAPR Type1, no additional DMRS for format3

PUCCH intra-slot FH = enabled, disabled

Receiver: 2Rx/4Rx MLD w/o pre-whitennig for format1, 2Rx/4Rx MMSE MRC for format3

DTX detection method: IFFT for format3

Supported Compensation: TOC, FOC

Supported Estimation and Measurements: TOE, RSSI, Recived Power, Noise Power, Noise Power per PRB, SINR

---

###### 5.3.4.2.1.1.2 L1/L3 call for FR1-TDD-eCPRI-7.2e for Odin

**5.3.4.2.1.1.2.0-1**  (ID: `12979050`)

L1/L3 call for FR1-TDD-eCPRI-7.2e for Odin
5G-L1-UL on Odin BB shall process PUCCH with the following configuration for L1/L3 call under CB012115-G for FR1-TDD-eCPRI-7.2e:

Format: long: format1 and format3

PUCCH start symbol = 0

PUCCH number of symbols = 14

OCC for format1 : {0}

Number of PRBs = 1 - for format1; 1..5  - for format3

PUCCH UCI bits: {1, 2} - for format1; [3..50]  - for format3

Bandwidth = 100MHz

Capacity: 8 resource per subcell for format1,  4 resources per subcell for format3

DMRS: Low-PAPR Type1, no additional DMRS for format3

PUCCH intra-slot FH = enabled, disabled

Receiver: 8Rx MLD with pre-whitennig for format1, 8Rx MMSE IRC for format3

DTX detection method: IFFT for format3

Supported Compensation: TOC, FOC

Supported Estimation and Measurements: TOE, RSSI, Recived Power, Noise Power, Noise Power per PRB, SINR

---

##### 5.3.4.2.1.2 FR1-FDD

###### 5.3.4.2.1.2.1 L1/L3 call for FR1-FDD-eCPRI-7.2a for Odin

**5.3.4.2.1.2.1.0-1**  (ID: `12979052`)

L1/L3 call for FR1-FDD-eCPRI-7.2a for Odin
5G-L1-UL on Odin BB shall process PUCCH with the following configuration for L1/L3 call under CB012115-L for FR1-FDD-eCPRI-7.2a:

Format: long: format1 and format3

PUCCH start symbol = 0

PUCCH number of symbols = 14

OCC for format1 : {0}

Number of PRBs = 1 - for format1; 1..2  - for format3

PUCCH UCI bits: {1} - for format1; [3..50]  - for format3

Bandwidth = 100MHz

Capacity: 8 resource per subcell for format1,  4 resources per subcell for format3

DMRS: Low-PAPR Type1, no additional DMRS for format3

PUCCH intra-slot FH = enabled, disabled

Receiver: 2Rx/4Rx MLD w/o pre-whitennig for format1, 2Rx/4Rx MMSE MRC for format3

DTX detection method: IFFT for format3

Supported Compensation: TOC, FOC

Supported Estimation and Measurements: TOE, RSSI, Recived Power, Noise Power, Noise Power per PRB, SINR

---

###### 5.3.4.2.1.2.2 L1/L3 call for FR1-FDD-CPRI for Odin

Format: long: format1 and format3

PUCCH number of symbols = 14

OCC for format1 : {0}

Number of PRBs = 1 - for format1; 1..2  - for format3

Supported Compensation: TOC, FOC

Supported Estimation and Measurements: TOE, RSSI, Recived Power, Noise Power, Noise Power per PRB, SINR

Bandwidth = 100MHz

###### 5.3.4.2.4.1.0-1 Overview Supported cell and dynamic configuration for PUCCH (specified in PUCCH chapter in 5G L1 Entity Level module) shall allow to execute test cases described as Conformance Test in 5G UP System Level in chapter: ( 11366926: Conformance Testing ). (ID: 13384242)

##### 5.3.4.2.4.2 Frozen Requirements

###### 5.3.4.2.4.2.0-1 Frozen Requirements L1 shall execute test cases described as performances requirements for PUCCH (Format F1 and F3) with 8RX TDD cell configuration in compliance with the 3GPP specification 38.141-1, please see clause 8.3, with supported cell bandwidth from 20MHz to 100MHz for TDD-eCPRI in Thor for ABIP and ABIQ HW. (ID: 11454510)

#### 5.3.4.2.5 Carrier Aggregation

##### 5.3.4.2.5.1 Overview

**5.3.4.2.5.1.0-1**  (ID: `13383061`)

Overview
The Carrier Aggregation functionality allows for aggregation of multiple carriers in DL and UL and with that increased aggregated bandwidth and higher peak and mean DL and UL user datarates.

In case of Carrier Aggregation, PUCCH on the PSCell is use for periodic CSI (CSI Acquisition and Beam Management) and HARQ reporting for each configured and active carrier. CSI reporting is done via dedicated PUCCH resource occasion.

For detailed information please find:

Carrier Aggregation Description: ([11596065: Carrier Aggregation](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Y2u3BvwOEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

UCI bit sequence: ([11508450: (38.212, 6.3.1.1) UCI bit sequence generation](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tTIzI_v1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

Overview for Max UCI Payload with Periodic CSI (P-CSI): ([12763238: Overview for Max UCI Payload with Periodic CSI (P-CSI)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_6rUdo4PbEfCOGMMH109ICw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

CSI Acquisition Max UCI Payload with Periodic CSI (P-CSI): ([12764792: CSI Acquisition Max UCI Payload with Periodic CSI (P-CSI)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_08wlAISvEfCOGMMH109ICw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

Beam Management Max UCI Payload with Periodic CSI (P-CSI): ([12764792: CSI Acquisition Max UCI Payload with Periodic CSI (P-CSI)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_08wlAISvEfCOGMMH109ICw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

Determine the number of UCI bits required for Channel Acquisition Reporting: ([11312227: Determine the number of UCI bits required for Channel Acquisition Reporting](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TrgbDPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

Determine the number of UCI bits required for Beam Reporting: ([11312249: Determine the number of UCI bits required for Beam Reporting](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TrhCEfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

Determine the maximum number of UCI bits for HARQ A/N: ([11312258: Determine the maximum number of UCI bits for HARQ A/N](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TrhCE_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

Determine the maximum number of UCI bits for pCSI report: ( [11312326: Determine the maximum number of UCI bits for pCSI report](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TrhCG_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

##### 5.3.4.2.5.2 Frozen Requirements

###### 5.3.4.2.5.2.1 FR1-TDD

###### 5.3.4.2.5.2.1.0-1 FR1-TDD Before 23R2 (ID: 11454531)

**5.3.4.2.5.2.1.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11454558`)

FR1-TDD
L1 shall support carrier aggregation up to 4 CCs in DL and no UL CA with TDD as PCell for the following cases:

* 1 CC TDD + 2 CCs FDD
* 2 CCs TDD + 1 CC FDD
* 2 CCs TDD  + 2 CCs FDD
* 1 CC TDD  + 3 CCs FDD

L1 shall support up to 55 bits UCI information in F3 format in order to support the above CA with the following details:

* Up to 19 bits of CSI report for channel acquisition
* Up to 21 bits of CSI report for Beam management
* Up to 14 bits of HARQ A/N
* 1 bit of SR

Note:

The CSI report is done per CC per UE; in other words, no P-CSI bundling for CCs.

[CB008827-5G-A] Parity from CB008532:

L1 shall support requirements above on Thor for FR1 TDD.

[End CB008827-5G-A]

HW-Technology Map (with FR1 TDD as PCell):

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Technology / HW | Loner | Loki | Thor |
| FR1-TDD-CPRI | Supported | Supported | [CB010575-D] Supported [End CB010575-D] |
| FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI | Supported | Supported | Supported |

---

###### 5.3.4.2.5.2.1.0-2 FR1-TDD From 23R2 (ID: 11454566)

**5.3.4.2.5.2.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11454575`)

FR1-TDD
Loner

---

**5.3.4.2.5.2.1.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11454582`)

FR1-TDD
L1 shall support carrier aggregation up to 4 CCs in DL and up to 2 CCs in UL with TDD or FDD cell as PCell for the following cases:

* 3 CCs TDD + 1 CC FDD
* 1 CC FDD + 3 CCs TDD

[CB008053-A]

L1 shall support:

up to 38 bits UCI information in F3 format for TDD eCPRI in order to support the above CA with the following details:

* Up to 21 bits of CSI report for Beam management
* Up to 16 bits of HARQ A/N
* 1 bit of SR

up to 36 bits UCI information in F3 format for TDD CPRI in order to support the above CA with the following details:

* Up to 19 bits of CSI report for Channel acquisition
* Up to 16 bits of HARQ A/N
* 1 bit of SR

[End CB008053-A]

[CB008053-C]

L1 shall support:

up to 39 bits UCI information in F3 format for TDD eCPRI in order to support the above CA with the following details:

* Up to 21 bits of CSI report for Beam management
* Up to 17 bits of HARQ A/N
* 1 bit of SR

up to 37 bits UCI information in F3 format for TDD CPRI in order to support the above CA with the following details:

* Up to 19 bits of CSI report for Channel acquisition
* Up to 17 bits of HARQ A/N
* 1 bit of SR

[End CB008053-C]

Note:

The CSI report is done per CC per UE; in other words, no P-CSI bundling for CCs.

The difference above is justified by the fact that TDD CPRI with BF is not supported in this feature.

---

**5.3.4.2.5.2.1.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11454590`)

FR1-TDD
Loki and Thor

---

**5.3.4.2.5.2.1.0-2.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `11454622`)

FR1-TDD
L1 shall support carrier aggregation up to 6 CCs in DL and up to 2 CCs in UL(1 TDD or 1 TDD+1 FDD) with TDD cell as PCell for the following cases:

* 3 CCs TDD + 3 CCs FDD
* 2 CCs TDD + 4 CCs FDD

L1 shall support up to 64 bits UCI information in PUCCH F3 format in order to support the above CA with the following details:

* Up to 19 bits of CSI report for channel acquisition
* Up to 21 bits of CSI report for beam management
* Up to 23 bits of HARQ A/N(23 bits are needed with 3 CCs TDD + 3 CCs FDD and 21 bits are needed with 2 CCs TDD + 4 CCs FDD)
* 1 bit of SR

Supported L1 HW and technology is as below:

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | Loner | Loki | Thor |
| FR1-TDD-CPRI | Not supported | [CB011080-A] Supported [End CB011080-A] | [CB011080-A] Supported [End CB011080-A] |
| FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI | Not supported | [CB011080-A] Supported [End CB011080-A] | [CB011080-A] Supported [End CB011080-A] |
| FR1-TDD-7-2e-eCPRI | Not supported | Not supported | [CB009936-H] Supported [End CB009936-H] |

Note:

1) The total number of the UCI bits can be reached as long as UCI bundling is supported per CB007827.

2) pCSI bundling means that CSI report for channel acquisition and beam management can be carried with same PUCCH resource. So it is needed to sum maximum bit of CSI report for channel acquisition and maximum bit of CSI report for beam management when calculating maximum bit nubmer of UCI information.

3) No pCSI bundling means that CSI report for channel acquisition and beam management are carried with separate PUCCH resource.So it is needed to maximize(maximum bit number of CSI report for channel acquisition, maximum bit number of CSI report for beam management) when calculating maximum bit number of UCI information.

4) The CSI report is done per CC per UE; in other words, no pCSI bundling for CCs.

---

###### 5.3.4.2.5.2.2 FR1-TDD-7-2e

**5.3.4.2.5.2.2.0-1**  (ID: `11454638`)

FR1-TDD-7-2e
L1 shall support carrier aggregation up to 4 CCs in DL and no UL CA with TDD as PCell for the following cases:

* 1 CC TDD + 2 CCs FDD
* 2 CCs TDD + 1 CC FDD
* 2 CCs TDD  + 2 CCs FDD
* 1 CC TDD  + 3 CCs FDD

L1 shall support up to 55 bits UCI information in F3 format in order to support the above CA with the following details:

* Up to 19 bits of CSI report for channel acquisition
* Up to 21 bits of CSI report for Beam management
* Up to 14 bits of HARQ A/N
* 1 bit of SR

Note:

The CSI report is done per CC per UE; in other words, no P-CSI bundling for CCs.

---

###### 5.3.4.2.5.2.3 FR1-FDD

###### 5.3.4.2.5.2.3.0-1 FR1-FDD Loner (ID: 11454655)

**5.3.4.2.5.2.3.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11454673`)

FR1-FDD
L1 shall support carrier aggregation up to 6 CCs in DL and up to 2 CCs in UL(2 FDD or 1 FDD+1 TDD) with FDD cell as PCell for the following cases:

* 3 CCs FDD + 3 CCs TDD
* 4 CCs FDD + 2 CCs TDD

[CB011081-A]

No pCSI bundling, L1 shall support up to 31 bits UCI information in PUCCH F3 format in order to support the above CA with the following details:

* Up to 19 bits of CSI report for channel acquisition
* Up to 21 bits of CSI report for beam management
* Up to 9 bits of HARQ A/N(9 bits are needed with 3 CCs FDD + 3 CCs TDD and 8 bits are needed with 4 CCs FDD + 2 CCs TDD)
* 1 bit of SR

[End CB011081-A]

[CB011081-A]

With pCSI bundling, L1 shall support up to 50 bits UCI information in F3 format in order to support the above CA with the following details:

* Up to 19 bits of CSI report for channel acquisition
* Up to 21 bits of CSI report for beam management
* Up to 9 bits of HARQ A/N(9 bits are needed with 3 CCs FDD + 3 CCs TDD and 8 bits are needed with 4 CCs FDD + 2 CCs TDD)
* 1 bit of SR

[End CB011081-A]

Note:

1) The total number of the UCI bits can be reached as long as UCI bundling is supported per CB007827.

2) pCSI bundling means that CSI report for channel acquisition and beam management can be carried with same PUCCH resource. So it is needed to sum maximum bit of CSI report for channel acquisition and maximum bit of CSI report for beam management when calculating maximum bit number of UCI information.

3) No pCSI bundling means that CSI report for channel acquisition and beam management are carried with separate PUCCH resource.So it is needed to maximize(maximum bit number of CSI report for channel acquisition, maximum bit number of CSI report for beam management) when calculating maximum bit number of UCI information.

4) The CSI report is done per CC per UE; in other words, no pCSI bundling for CCs.

---

[End CB011081-A]

* Up to 19 bits of CSI report for channel acquisition
* Up to 21 bits of CSI report for beam management
* Up to 9 bits of HARQ A/N(9 bits are needed with 3 CCs FDD + 3 CCs TDD and 8 bits are needed with 4 CCs FDD + 2 CCs TDD)

[End CB011081-A]

So it is needed to sum maximum bit of CSI report for channel acquisition and maximum bit of CSI report for beam management when calculating maximum bit number of UCI information.

3) No pCSI bundling means that CSI report for channel acquisition and beam management are carried with separate PUCCH resource.So it is needed to maximize(maximum bit number of CSI report for channel acquisition, maximum bit number of CSI report for beam management) when calculating maximum bit number of UCI information.

#### 5.3.4.2.6 Supercell

##### 5.3.4.2.6.1 FDD Supercell

###### 5.3.4.2.6.1.1 General

**5.3.4.2.6.1.1.0-2**  (ID: `13374650`)

General
For FR1-FDD 5G-L1-UL shall receive PUCCH transmission for all UL subcells belongs to FDD Supercell.

The number of FDD supercell subcells is in the range of [2 .. 6] (1 serving subcell plus 1~5 non-serving subcells) in one FDD Supercell per L1 Pool for Loki and Thor.

For details please find: ([11353530: Supercell Mode for FDD](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucAIa_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

Note:

1. There is possible to mix one or more FDD Supercell with one or more regular subcell within one L1 Pool for Loki or Thor.
2. The FDD Supercell is a 3GPP “cell” with a unique cellId (all FDD Supercell subcells have the same physCellId).

[CNI-108168-J] The requirement was refined under CNI-108168  [End CNI-108168-J]

---

###### 5.3.4.2.6.1.2 PUCCH format3 processing for FDD Supercell subcell

**5.3.4.2.6.1.2.0-2**  (ID: `13374649`)

PUCCH format3 processing for FDD Supercell subcell
For PUCCH format3 for FDD Supercell subcells 5G-L1-UL shall support different PUCCH processing depending on the type of FDD Supercell subcell:

* serving subcell   
  (indicated via value "true" of parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->isServingSubcell)  
  PUCCH format3 processing is regular (related to other parameters from PucchReceiveRequest and UlCellSetup)
* non-serving subcell  
   (indicated via value "false" of parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->isServingSubcell)  
  PUCCH format3 processing is reduced to processed measurement for Power Noise, rxPower and SINR.

For details please find: ( [11104965: PUCCH Format 3 Receiver in non-serving subcell of FDD supercell](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koEOVvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)), ( [11105105: FDD FR1 - PUCCH Format 3](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koGDivvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

Note:

1. For FR1-TDD and for subcells not belonged to FDD Supercell 5G-L1-UL shall expect value "false" of parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->isServingSubcell) from L2-PS

[CNI-108168-J] The requirement was refined under CNI-108168  [End CNI-108168-J]

---

#### 5.3.4.2.7 Interworking with other channels

##### 5.3.4.2.7.1 Multiplexing with PUSCH and PRACH

###### 5.3.4.2.7.1.1 Long PUCCH (format1 and format3)

**5.3.4.2.7.1.1.0-2**  (ID: `13391496`)

Long PUCCH (format1 and format3)
For long PUCCH formats 5G-L1-UL shall support Frequency Domain Multiplexing of PUCCH and other UL channels on the same subcells within same slot for:

a) FDM PUSCH + Long PUCCH

b) FDM PUSCH + PRACH + Long PUCCH

c) FDM SRS + Long PUCCH

For details please find: ([11109907: FDM Configurations](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ko-NRfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

Note:

Long PUCCH formats are: PUCCH format1 and PUCCH format3.

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

###### 5.3.4.2.7.1.2 Short PUCCH (format0 and format2)

**5.3.4.2.7.1.2.0-2**  (ID: `13371508`)

Short PUCCH (format0 and format2)
For short PUCCH formats 5G-L1-UL shall support multiplexing of PUCCH and other UL channels on the same subcells within same slot for:

Multiplexing Configurations:

a) PRACH FDM with PUSCH;

b) PRACH FDM/TDM with short PUCCH;

c) combination of the a and b;

For details please find: ([11109907: FDM Configurations](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ko-NRfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

Note:

Short PUCCH formats are: PUCCH format0 and PUCCH format2.

[CNI-108168-J] The requirement was refined under CNI-108168  [End CNI-108168-J]

---

**5.3.4.3.1.0-1**  (ID: `12659711`)

Overview
The reference for PUCCH Formats is 3GPP TS38.211.

Information about supported configuration (5G L1 Entity Level module) are in:

Supported values for startPrb and numOfPrb are specified in: [11455494: Frequency domain resource allocation](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAjGAfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

Supported values for firstSymbol and numOfSymbols are specified in: [11455229: Time domain resource allocation](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAhQ4vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

Supported numbers of UCI bits are specified in: [11453947: Parameter srBit](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAbKM_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) , [11457186: Handling AN and SR bits](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fApzvvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

OCC and CS configuration are specified in: [11455460: Time domain orthogonal cover codes (OCC)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAie_PvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

Configuration of SR bit is described in: [11456442: Uplink control information](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAmJXPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

DMRS configurations are described in: [11455553: DMRS](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAjGCPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

Frequency hopping configuration is described in: [11455971: Frequency Hopping](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAk7OvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

#### 5.3.4.3.6 Frozen Requirements

##### 5.3.4.3.6.0-1 Frozen Requirements Loner and Loki (ID: 11454962)

**5.3.4.3.6.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11454977`)

Frozen Requirements
Format 0

---

**5.3.4.3.6.0-1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11457966`)

Frozen Requirements
**Loner and Loki**

---

**5.3.4.3.6.0-1.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11454984`)

Frozen Requirements
Content of this requirement is frozen and valid until 26R1 release, For later releases please refer to the objects below in chapters : [11454954](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAgCuvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

**Format 0**

For each combination of HARQ-ACK (1 or 2) and SR (negative or positive), UCI bits are transmitted with different sequences (different Cyclic Shift values) with the initial cyclic shift (*initialCyclicShift) presented in UlData\_PucchReceiveReq. Please refer, 5G\_L1\_17222\_replaced([11455460](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAie_PvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L1\_17228\_replaced([11455971](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAk7OvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the supported values.*

For each combination of HARQ-ACK (1 or 2) and SR (negative or positive), UCI bits are transmitted with different sequences (different Cyclic Shift values), ~~as defined in 5G\_RAN\_UP\_13291~~ **[Before PR542948] with the initial cyclic shift (initialCyclicShift in UlData\_PucchReceiveReq) is set to 0.** [End PR542948][PR542948] with the initial cyclic shift (initialCyclicShift in UlData\_PucchReceiveReq) is in the range of ~~[0..11]~~ {0,3} (see 5G\_UP\_IF\_1637). **[End PR542948]**\*\*\*\*

**5.3.4.3.6.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11454992`)

Frozen Requirements
Format 1

---

**5.3.4.3.6.0-1.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11454999`)

Frozen Requirements
Content of this requirement is frozen and valid until 26R1 release, For later releases please refer to the objects below in chapters : [11454954](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAgCuvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

**Format 1**

PUCCH format 1 is scheduled over 1 PRB, a variable number of OFDM symbols in the range [4...14] , an initial cyclic shift in the range of [0...11] and time domain orthogonal cover code is in the range [0...6]. These characteristics are available in the field numPrb, numOfSymbols, initialCyclicShift and timeDomainOcc of the UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message (5G\_L1\_IF\_216\_replaced([11513990](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MIfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Following modulation types (modulationType) are supported:

* BPSK -> modulationType is set to BPSK.
* QPSK -> modulationType is set to QPSK.

Time domain and frequency domain allocations are performed in a contiguous manner. Supported values for the number of OFDM symbols are defined in 5G\_L1\_17221\_replaced([11455229](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAhQ4vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**[5GC00885-A]: FDD support for Loner in 5G20B** [End 5GC00885-A]\*\*\*\*

**[5GC002481-AA]: FDD support for Loki in 5G21A** [End 5GC002481-AA]\*\*\*\*

**[CBC006064-A]: TDD FR1 support for Loner in 5G21A** [End CBC006064-A]\*\*\*\*

**[CB007950-A]: TDD FR1 support for Loki in 5G21B** [End CB007950-A]\*\*\*\*

**[CB008205-B, CB008205-C] 5G-L1-UL shall support only 14 OFDM symbols in ABIO for O-RAN compliant FR1 FDD eCPRI.**[End CB008205-B, CB008205-C]\*\*\*\*

**[Before-CNI-122313-A]**

**[CB009443-C] This requirement shall be supported in RINLINE1 HW for FR1-TDD-eCPRI.**[End CB009443-C]\*\*\*\*

**[CB009444-I] This requirement shall be supported in RINLINE1 HW for FR1-FDD-eCPRI.**[End CB009444-I]\*\*\*\*

**[CNI-122313-A]**

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

**[End CNI-122313-A]**
