### 5.3.4.7 Modulation

#### 5.3.4.7.1 Format1

**5.3.4.7.1.0-2**  (ID: `13254738`)

Format1
5G-L1-UL for PUCCH format1 shall use BPSK and QPSK types of modulation.

BPSK type of modulation is used when 1-bit HARQ AN or SR-only is transmitted over PUCCH format1, QPSK type of modulation is used when 2-bit HARQ is sent.

Note:

Parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->modulationType is ignored, modulation is derived from number of HARQ bits (1: BPSK, 2: QPSK)).

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

#### 5.3.4.7.2 Format2

**5.3.4.7.2.0-1**  (ID: `13241430`)

Format2
5G-L1-UL for PUCCH format2 shall use QPSK type of modulation.

Note:

Type of modulation is indicated by parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->modulationType, but according to 3GPP TS 38.211 (v17.3.0): ch. 6.3.2.5.2 QPSK is only type of modulation for format2.

---

#### 5.3.4.7.3 Format3

**5.3.4.7.3.0-2**  (ID: `13254739`)

Format3
5G-L1-UL for PUCCH format3 shall use π/2-BPSK and QPSK types of modulation.

Note:

Type of modulation is indicated by parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->modulationType.

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

### 5.3.4.8 Spatial streams configuration

#### 5.3.4.8.1 Number of supported spatial streams for PUCCH

##### 5.3.4.8.1.1 FR1-TDD

**5.3.4.8.1.1.0-2**  (ID: `12632604`)

FR1-TDD
For FR1-TDD 5G-L1-UL shall support following numbers of spatial stream (ce)Axc depending on type of subcell (UlCell\_SetupReq->ulSubcellType):

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| SubcellType (L1 BB) | Number of spatial streams (ce)AxC |  |  |  | First feature |
| Loner (CPRI/  eCPRI-7.2a) | Loki (CPRI/  eCPRI-7.2a) | Thor (CPRI/  eCPRI-7.2a/ eCPRI-7.2e) | Odin (eCPRI-7.2a/ eCPRI-7.2e) |  |  |
| C2 (CPRI/  eCPRI-7.2a) | 2 | 2 | 2 | [CB012115-IA] 2 for eCPRI-7.2a [End CB012115-IA] | legacy |
| C4 (CPRI/  eCPRI-7.2a) | 4 | 4 | 4 | [CB012115-IA] 4 for eCPRI-7.2a [End CB012115-IA] | legacy |
| C8 (eCPRI-7.2a) | - | - | 4, 8\* | - | CB009363 |
| C8'2 (eCPRI-7.2e) | - | - | 8 | [CB012115-GA] 8 [End CB012115-GA] | CB010708 |
| C8'4 (eCPRI-7.2e) | - | - | 8 | [CB012115-GA] 8 [End CB012115-GA] | CB010708 |
| C8'8 (eCPRI-7.2e) | - | - | 8 | - | CB008235 |

Note:

* The number of spatial streams ceAxc for C8 for Thor could be 4 or 8 and it is indicated by UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->numCeAxCIndex . See also:  [11456427: 4Rx mode for C8 subcell](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAmJWvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

For eCPRI two consecutive spatial streams (UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->  
Subcells->PucchResources->ceAxCIndex) are mapped to one individual beam patternId (UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->patternId)

For supported types of subcell please refer: [11381236](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uero9fvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

---

##### 5.3.4.8.1.2 FR2-TDD

**5.3.4.8.1.2.0-1**  (ID: `12633908`)

FR2-TDD
For FR2-TDD for PUCCH 5G-L1-UL shall support following numbers of spatial stream (ce)Axc depending on type of subcell (UlCell\_SetupReq->ulSubcellType):

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| SubcellType (L1 BB) | Number of spatial streams (ce)AxC |  |  |  | First feature |
| Loner (CPRI/  eCPRI-7.2a) | Loki (eCPRI-7.2a) | Thor (eCPRI-7.2a) | Odin |  |  |
| D2 (CPRI/  eCPRI-7.2a) | 2 | 2 | 2 | - | legacy |

Note:

For eCPRI two consecutive spatial streams (UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->  
Subcells->PucchResources->ceAxCIndex) are mapped to one individual beam patternId (UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->patternId)

From system perspective, TDD FR2 is supported only for eCPRI

For supported types of subcell please refer: [11381236](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uero9fvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

##### 5.3.4.8.1.3 FR1-FDD

**5.3.4.8.1.3.0-2**  (ID: `13391511`)

FR1-FDD
For FR1-FDD for PUCCH 5G-L1-UL shall support following numbers of spatial stream (ce)Axc depending on type of subcell (UlCell\_SetupReq->ulSubcellType):

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| SubcellType (L1 BB) | Number of spatial streams (ce)AxC |  |  |  | First feature |
| Loner (CPRI) | Loki (CPRI/  eCPRI-7.2a) | Thor (CPRI/  eCPRI-7.2a) | Odin (CPRI/  eCPRI-7.2a) |  |  |
| A2 (CPRI/  eCPRI-7.2a) | 2 | 2 | 2 | [CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] 2 CPRI /eCPRII-7.2a [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] | 5GC000998 |
| A4 (CPRI/  eCPRI-7.2a) | 4 | 4 | 4 | [CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] 4 CPRI /eCPRII-7.2a [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] | 5GC000836 |
| A8 (eCPRI-7.2a) | - | - | 8 | - | CB013442 |

Note:

For eCPRI two consecutive spatial streams (UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->  
Subcells->PucchResources->ceAxCIndex) are mapped to one individual beam patternId (UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->patternId)

For supported types of subcell please refer: [11381236](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uero9fvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

---

#### 5.3.4.8.2 4Rx mode for C8 subcell

**5.3.4.8.2.0-1**  (ID: `11456434`)

4Rx mode for C8 subcell
5G-L1-UL shall support 4Rx PUCCH reception from first 4 streams when C8 subcell is configured.

Note:

In this case, only the first two elements of longTermCfoMetricOfBeam in UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message (5G\_L1\_IF\_216\_replaced([11513990](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MIfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) are valid. 5G-L1-UL shall duplicate each of these two elements for first 4 eAxC streams. The last two elements are invalid value. The size of shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt in UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs (5G\_L1\_IF\_221\_replaced([11514182](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BQvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is 4 instead of 8.

---

### 5.3.4.9 Uplink Control Information

#### 5.3.4.9.1 Overview

**5.3.4.9.1.0-1**  (ID: `13383214`)

Overview
PUCCH is used for UCI reporting.

For detailed information about configuration of UCI payloads please find:

Overview for Max UCI Payload with Periodic CSI (P-CSI): ([12763238: Overview for Max UCI Payload with Periodic CSI (P-CSI)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_6rUdo4PbEfCOGMMH109ICw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

CSI Acquisition Max UCI Payload with Periodic CSI (P-CSI): ([12764792: CSI Acquisition Max UCI Payload with Periodic CSI (P-CSI)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_08wlAISvEfCOGMMH109ICw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

Beam Management Max UCI Payload with Periodic CSI (P-CSI): ([12764792: CSI Acquisition Max UCI Payload with Periodic CSI (P-CSI)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_08wlAISvEfCOGMMH109ICw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

UCI bit sequence: ([11508450: (38.212, 6.3.1.1) UCI bit sequence generation](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tTIzI_v1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

#### 5.3.4.9.2 Format 0

##### 5.3.4.9.2.0-1 Format 0 FR1-TDD (ID: 12683113)

**5.3.4.9.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `12687008`)

Format 0
For FR1-TDD for PUCCH format0 5G-L1-UL shall support following numbers of UCI bits:

The number of UCI bits per PUCCH resource are specified in the table below:

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | number of UCI bits for PUCCH format0 resource for FR1-TDD |  |  |  |  |
|  | Technology | Information type | A/N bits | Total UCI bits[1] | First Feature |
| L1 HW | Loner (CPRI/ eCPRI 7.2a) | A/N + SR SR only A/N only | [0..2] | [0..2] | CB008053 |
| Loki (CPRI/ eCPRI 7.2a) | [0..2] | [0..2] | CB007950 |  |  |

The SR bit detection is requested by parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->nANPucch by value 1='SRBIT\_DETECTION\_ENABLED'

The number of A/N bits is indicated by parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->nANPucch

Note:

[1] Total UCI bits refers to the effective bits for HARQ-AN. Decoded SR bit is indicated via parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->srBit .

#### 5.3.4.9.4 Format 2

##### 5.3.4.9.4.0-1 Format 2 FR1-TDD (ID: 12683127)

**5.3.4.9.4.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `12687010`)

Format 2
For FR1-TDD for PUCCH format2 5G-L1-UL shall support following numbers of UCI bits:

The number of UCI bits per PUCCH resource are specified in the table below:

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | number of UCI bits for PUCCH format2 resource for FR1-TDD |  |  |  |  |
|  | Technology | Information type | A/N bits | Total UCI bits[1] | First Feature |
| L1 HW | Loner (CPRI/ eCPRI 7.2a) | A/N + SR SR + CSI A/N + SR + CSI | [0..50] | [3..50] | legacy |
| Loki (CPRI/ eCPRI 7.2a) | [0..numOfUCInfoInBit] | [3..50][2][4] | legacy |  |  |

The number of A/N bits is indicated by parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->nANPucch

The total number of UCI bits is indicated by parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->numOfBitsOfUciInformation

Note:

[1] For conformance test: {4}

[2] For conformance test: {4, 22}

1. When SR is present, the SR information is provided combined with the CSI report in uciBits.  5G-L1-UL decodes SR + CSI report combined and provides the combined decoding result in uciBits. Whether SR is included in PUCCH format2 or not is transparent to 5G-L1-UL.

[4] When L2 parameter rdUsePucchF2OnlyForHarqonly is true, L2-PS increments the number of A/N bits (UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->nANPucch) by 2 (the UE will report at least 3 bits, but first two bits are not used).

---

##### 5.3.4.9.4.0-2 Format 2 FR2-TDD (ID: 12683148)

**5.3.4.9.4.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `12683304`)

Format 2
theFor FR2-TDD for PUCCH format2 5G-L1-UL shall support following numbers of UCI bits:

The number of UCI bits per PUCCH resource are specified in the table below:

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | number of UCI bits for PUCCH format2 resource for FR2-TDD |  |  |  |  |
|  | Technology | Information type | A/N bits | Total UCI bits[1] | First Feature |
| L1 HW | Loner (CPRI/ eCPRI 7.2a) | A/N + SR SR + CSI | [0..50] | [3..50] | legacy |
| Loki (eCPRI 7.2a) | [0..50] | [3..78][3] | legacy |  |  |
| Thor (eCPRI 7.2a) | [0..50] | [3..78][3] | CB010576 |  |  |
| Odin |  |  |  |  |  |

The number of A/N bits is indicated by parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->nANPucch

The total number of UCI bits is indicated by parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->numOfBitsOfUciInformation

Note:

[1]  When is scheduled PUCCH format2 resource with one symbol, 5G-L1-UL could support two symbols per slot for PUCCH format2. Each symbol could carry a maximum  'Total UCI bits' bits.

1. When SR is present, the SR information is provided combined with the CSI report in uciBits.  5G-L1-UL decodes SR + CSI report combined and provides the combined decoding result in uciBits. Whether SR is included in PUCCH format2 or not is transparent to 5G-L1-UL.

[3] When L2 parameter rdUsePucchF2OnlyForHarqonly is true, L2-PS increments the number of A/N bits (UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->nANPucch) by 2 (the UE will report at least 3 bits, but first two bits are not used).

1. When SR is present, the SR information is provided combined with the CSI report in uciBits.  5G-L1-UL decodes SR + CSI report combined and provides the combined decoding result in uciBits. Whether SR is included in PUCCH format2 or not is transparent to 5G-L1-UL.

#### 5.3.4.9.5 Format 3

##### 5.3.4.9.5.0-1 Format 3 FR1-TDD (ID: 12683124)

**5.3.4.9.5.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `12727594`)

Format 3
For FR1-TDD for PUCCH format3 5G-L1-UL shall support following numbers of UCI bits:

The number of UCI bits per PUCCH resource are specified in the table below:

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | number of UCI bits for PUCCH format3 resource for FR1-TDD |  |  |  |  |
|  | Technology | Information type | A/N bits | Total UCI bits | First Feature |
| L1 HW | Loner (CPRI/ eCPRI 7.2a) | A/N only CSI only SR + CSI A/N + CSI A/N + SR + CSI | [0..17] | [3..39] | CB008053 |
| Loki (CPRI/ eCPRI 7.2a) | [0..23] | [3..64] | CB007950 |  |  |
| Thor (CPRI/ eCPRI 7.2a/ eCPRI 7.2e) | [0..23] | [3..64] | CB007487 |  |  |
| Odin (eCPRI 7.2a/ eCPRI 7.2e) | [CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] [0..11] [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] | [CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] [3..50] [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] | CB012115 |  |  |

The number of A/N bits is indicated by parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->nANPucch

The total number of UCI bits is indicated by parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->numOfBitsOfUciInformation

Note:

HARQ A/N, SR and CSI are concatenated one after the other, respectively.

When SR bit is present, it is multiplexed with the CSI, decoded bit is prepended to the bits of the CSI report. It is transparent to 5G-L1-UL whether SR bit is present.

For the supported configuration of UCI from E2E perspective for CA and different numbers of CC please find: [11104749](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koBLC_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

HARQ A/N, SR and CSI are concatenated one after the other, respectively.

#### 5.3.4.9.6 Frozen Requirements

##### 5.3.4.9.6.0-1 Frozen Requirements Loner (ID: 11456450)

**5.3.4.9.6.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11456470`)

Frozen Requirements
For L1 Loner HW,

supported PUCCH formats, information type and number of information bits are summarized in the table below.

pucchFormat, srBitDetection, nANPucch and numOfBitsOfUciInformation are received from the UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message.

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| PUCCH format (pucchFormat) | TDD  FR1 |  |  | FDD/SUL/DSS |  |  |
| Information type | A/N bits (nANPucch) | Total UCI bits (numOfBitsOfUciInformation) | Information type | A/N bits (nANPucch) | Total UCI bits (numOfBitsOfUciInformation) |  |
| Format 0 |  A/N + SR  SR only [5GC001037-E] [5GC001981-A]  A/N only | [0..2] | [0..2] | [5GC000836-B]  A/N [5GC000836-I]  A/N+SR  SR only | [5GC000836-B] [1..2] [5GC000836-I] [0..2] | [5GC000836-B] [1..2] [5GC000836-H] [0..2] |
| [Before 5GC001981-A] The SR bit is not included in the numOfBitsOfUciInformation. [before 5GC001037-E] 5G-L1-UL shall perform SR detection in each PUCCH reception. [5GC001037-E] When srBitDetection is set to False then HARQ-ACK bit without SR (A/N only) shall be detected. |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| Format 1 | [CB006064-A]  SR only  A/N only  A/N+SR[end CB006064-A] | [CB006064-A] [0..2][end CB006064-A] | [CB006064-A] [0..2][end CB006064-A] | [5GC000885-A]  SR only  A/N only [end 5GC000885-A] [5GC000885-E]  A/N+SR [end 5GC000885-E] | [5GC000885-A] [0..1][end 5GC000885-A]// | [5GC000885-A] [0..1] [end 5GC000885-A] |
| Format 2 |  A/N + SR  A/N + SR + CSI  SR + CSI | [0..8] [5GC001127-C] [0..50] | [3..50] |  A/N + SR  A/N + SR + CSI  SR + CSI | [5GC000836-I] [0..2] [5GC001037-E] [0..4] | [5GC000836-I] [3..11] [5GC001037-E] [3..22] [5GC000920-AA] [3..13] |
| Note: Channel coding is for small block length is used when number of UCI bits <= 11. Polar coding is used when number of UCI bits > 11 |  |  |  |  |  |  |

[CB009854-D] FDD FR1 CPRI: With pCSI bundling, for UCI on PUCCH F3 at most 8 A/N + 19 PCSI for channel acquisition + 21 PCSI for beamforming + 1SR bits are needed. [End CB009854-D]

FDD: HARQ A/N, SR and CSI are concatenated one after the other, respectively. (38.212 6.3.1.1.3 )

Note: When SR bit is multiplexed with the CSI, decoded bit is prepended to the bits of the CSI report (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3617\_replaced([11160013](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktNNC_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3603\_replaced([11159969](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktNNA_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

From end to end point of view, for UCI on PUCCH F3 at most 1 A/N + 11 PCSI + 1SR bits are needed for Loner and Loki L1 HWs

Note:

Channel coding is for small block length is used when number of UCI bits <= 11. Polar coding is used when number of UCI bits > 11.

L1 supports two PUCCH format2 symbols per slot with up to 50 bits for each one

[CB007326-A] ASOE support only FR1-TDD part. [End CB007326-A]

[RP003187-A, RP003187-H] This requirement is valid for L1 Thor [End RP003187-A, RP003187-H]

[CB008205-B] 5G-L1-UL shall support requirements above for FDD FR1 Format 1 and 3 in ABIO for O-RAN compliant FR1 FDD eCPRI. [End CB008205-B]

[CB008325-5G-BA]

Note: From end to end point of view, for Thor HW, up to 27 bits of UCI on F3 are needed with 3CCs (1CC FDD PCell + 2CC TDD SCells) as follow:

* 21 bits of CSI report for beam management
* 5 bits HARQ A/N bits
* 1 bit SR

Note: There is no P-CSI bundling for multiple CCs; CSI report is done for each CC for one UE.

[End CB008325-5G-BA]

[CB008827-5G-A] Parity from CB008532

L1 shall support 27 bits of UCI on F3 with 3CCs (1CC FDD PCell + 2CC TDD SCells) in ABIP.

[End CB008827-5G-A]

[Before-CNI-122313-A]

[CB009443-C] This requirement for format 1 and 3 shall be supported in RINLINE1 HW for FR1-TDD-eCPRI.[End CB009443-C]

[CB009444-I] This requirement for format 1 and 3 shall be supported in RINLINE1 HW for FR1-FDD-eCPRI.[End CB009444-I]

[CNI-122313-A]

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

[End CNI-122313-A]

[CB009029-5G-A] Parity from CB008053:

L1 shall support up to 17 A/N bits and up to 58 bits of UCI on F3 with 4CCs' combination as below in ABIP:

* 3 CCs TDD + 1 CC FDD
* 1 CC FDD + 3 CCs TDD

[End CB009029-5G-A]

[CB010776-5G-A] Parity from CB009854:

L1 shall support for FR1 FDD up to 8 HARQ A/N bits and up to 49 bits of UCI on PUCCH F3 with 5CCs combination as below in ABIP:

* 2 CC FDD + 3 CCs TDD DL CA(FDD as PSell).

[End CB010776-5G-A]

[CB010575-A] For L1 Thor for FR1-TDD-CPRI:

for F1 parity from  RP003187 (CB007487) : up to 2 A/N bits and up to 2 bits of UCI,

for F3 up to 4 A/N bits and up to 16 bits of UCI  [End CB010575-A]

[CB010575-D] For L1 Thor for FR1-TDD-CPRI for F3 parity from CB009029 (CB008053) : up to 17 A/N bits and up to 58 bits of UCI [End CB010575-D]

[CB007595-B] The requirement is also applicable for L1 Thor for FR1-TDD-7-2e-eCPRI within F1 and F3 [End CB007595-B]

[CB010969-SR-CB] This requirement shall be supported by L1 Thor in FR1-FDD-OBSAI for F1 and F3. [End CB010969-SR-CB]

[CB009514-F,H] For L1 Thor for FR1-TDD-7.2e-eCPRI: for F3 up to 14 A/N bits and up to 55 bits of UCI  [End CB009514-F,H]

---

## 5.3.5 PUCCH processing

##### 5.3.5.1.1.1 Signal processing path

MLSE Receiver

#### 5.3.5.1.2 Demapping

**5.3.5.1.2.0-1**  (ID: `13343051`)

Demapping
For PUCCH format0 5G-L1-UL shall pack frequency domain IQ samples from PRBs allocated to PUCCH resource in the buffer. According to list of PUCCH resources, received in the receive request, FD IQ samples from symbols carrying PUCCH are written in buffer.

For more details, please find sections 2.1 and 2.4.1 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification.

Note:

For format0 within one PRB there is possibility to multiplex several PUCCH format0 resources.

The Demapping is a part of common Front End operations.

---

#### 5.3.5.1.3 Time offset compensation

**5.3.5.1.3.0-2**  (ID: `11456551`)

Time offset compensation
[CNI-108168]

For common requirements (for different formats) for Time offet compensation please find chapter 5G\_L1\_17241\_replaced([11457734](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAs3CPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) in chapter "PUCCH processing\ Format 3"

[END CNI-108168]

---

#### 5.3.5.1.4 UE specific processing

##### 5.3.5.1.4.1 ZC Sequence Removal

**5.3.5.1.4.1.0-1**  (ID: `13343052`)

ZC Sequence Removal
For PUCCH format0 5G-L1-UL shall support ZC sequence removal.

For each symbol there is removed ZC sequence by multiply received signal by conjugation of reference sequence (ZC sequence).

For more details, please find sections  2.4.1.1.3 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification.

---

##### 5.3.5.1.4.2 Cyclic Shift Correlation

**5.3.5.1.4.2.0-1**  (ID: `13343053`)

Cyclic Shift Correlation
For PUCCH format0 5G-L1-UL shall apply cyclic shift correlation operation.

The purpose of this step is to provide correlation with the 12 possible cyclic shifts. This is done using a DFT for each symbol.

For more details, please find sections  2.4.1.1.4 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification.

---

##### 5.3.5.1.4.3 Soft Demodulation

**5.3.5.1.4.3.0-1**  (ID: `13343054`)

Soft Demodulation
For PUCCH format0 5G-L1-UL shall execute soft demodulation to calculate soft information of each cyclic shift correlation.

In result of this operation, it is calculated the power of each cyclic shift correlation.

For more details, please find sections  2.4.1.1.4 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification.

---

##### 5.3.5.1.4.4 ML detection

**5.3.5.1.4.4.0-1**  (ID: `13343055`)

ML detection
For PUCCH format0 5G-L1-UL shall support MLSE (Maximum Likelihood Sequence Estimation) algorithm.

During this operation it is calculated the maximum likelihood metric for each possible cyclic shift considering the Rx spatial stream and symbol.

Supported receiver modes are specified in: ([12576671: Receiver modes](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_QfMWsDA3EfCRMdP0Nuo3Hg?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

For more details, please find sections  2.4.1.3 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification.

Note:

For 2 symbols configuration (with and without FH), non-coherent combine method is used in soft detection.

---

##### 5.3.5.1.4.5 Frozen Requirements

###### 5.3.5.1.4.5.1 Decoding

###### 5.3.5.1.4.5.1-1 Decoding

###### 5.3.5.1.4.5.1-1.0-1 Decoding L1 shall now use the same non-coherent method for FH and non-FH processing for PUCCH format 0, in order to reduce the processing latency. The same DTX thresholds could be used for both FH and non-FH processing. (ID: 11456731)

###### 5.3.5.1.4.5.1-2 Decoding

**5.3.5.1.4.5.1-2.0-1**  (ID: `11456715`)

Decoding
If PUCCH F0 is transmitted in 2 OFDM symbols and frequency hopping is disabled, non-coherent combine method is used in soft detection.

If PUCCH is transmitted in 2 OFDM symbols and frequency hopping is disabled, linear interpolation is performed per OFDM symbols.

For PUCCH format 2, the search window length for time offset estimation is changed to 2/3 CP length, and the search window range is also changed to be symmetric.

---

**5.3.5.1.4.5.1.0-1**  (ID: `11456748`)

Decoding
PUCCH Format 0

[Before 5GC002006-B] If PUCCH F0 is transmitted in 2 OFDM symbols and frequency hopping is disabled, coherent combine method is used in soft detection. [End 5GC002006-B]

[5GC002006-B,CB007326-A] [CB007403-C] [CB007403-E]If PUCCH F0 is transmitted in 2 OFDM symbols and frequency hopping is disabled, non-coherent combine method is used in soft detection. [End 5GC002006-B,CB007326-A] [End CB007403-C] [End CB007403-E]

Reference to section “2.4.1.9 Soft Detection” of 5GMax algorithm specification (see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_916 5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[5GC001972-A]  5G-L1-UL shall also support PUCCH F0 reception in vDU L1 HW. Description of the receiver alghoritm was presented in chapter 4.2 FlexRAN L1 Alghoritm Description (see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_915) [End 5GC001972-A]

[5GC002056-AA,5GC002481-AA,CB007326-A] For L1 Loki HW, PUCCH F0 with 2 OFDM symbols and frequency hopping is disabled, non-coherent combine method is used in soft detection. [End 5GC002056-AA,5GC002481-AA,CB007326-A]

---

##### 5.3.5.1.4.6 Parameter estimation and measurement

###### 5.3.5.1.4.6.1 Noise power

###### 5.3.5.1.4.6.1.1 General

**5.3.5.1.4.6.1.1.0-2**  (ID: `13340075`)

General
For PUCCH format0 5G-L1-UL shall perform the Noise Power Estimation ([NPE](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_hle2YGenEfCk8v_SG2h2xg)) per symbol and per Rx spatial stream.

The noise is the average energy on all other cyclic shifts than:

* the cyclic shift which is used by UEs to send data signal
* the two adjacent cyclic shifts to cyclic shift which is used by UE to send data signal.

NPE is specified in section 2.4.1.1.5 of the 5GMax algorithm specification.

[CNI-108168-J] The requirement was refined under CNI-108168  [End CNI-108168-J]

---

###### 5.3.5.1.4.6.1.1.1 Noise Power Processing

###### 5.3.5.1.4.6.1.1.1.0-1 Noise Power Processing For PUCCH format0 5G-L1-UL shall calculate Noise Power per spatial stream. Noise Power per spatial stream calculation is proceed based on Noise Power estimation. (ID: 13343975)

###### 5.3.5.1.4.6.1.2 Noise Power measurement

**5.3.5.1.4.6.1.2.0-1**  (ID: `13340077`)

Noise Power measurement
For PUCCH format0 for each scheduled resource 5G-L1-UL shall calculate the noise power (interference + thermal noise) and reports this estimate to 5G-L2-PS.

This estimate is derived while considering only the allocated PRBs for a given resource. This estimate is normalized to one PRB and aggregating over all Rx spatial streams. The unit of this estimate is dBm.

5G-L1-UL shall report estimate via L1-L2 IF parameters: UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->noisePower

Noise Power estimation algorithm is specified in section 2.8.3.3 and 2.4.1.1.5 of the 5GMax algorithm specification.

Noise Power measurement for PUCCH format0 is supported for following L1 variants:

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | Technology | FR1-TDD (CPRI/ eCPRI-7.2a/) | FR2-TDD (CPRI/ eCPRI-7.2a) | FR1-FDD (CPRI) | First Feature |
| L1 HW | Loner | supported | supported for CPRI | supported | Legacy |
| Loki | supported | supported for eCPRI-7.2a | - | Legacy |  |
| Thor | - | supported for eCPRI-7.2a | - | CB010576 |  |
| Odin |  |  |  |  |  |

1. For invalid values for Noise Power measurements please find: ([12733068](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_mMhiRXRFEfCRE7eh4Ndkrw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

---

###### 5.3.5.1.4.6.1.3 Noise power per PRB measurement

**5.3.5.1.4.6.1.3.0-1**  (ID: `12714975`)

Noise power per PRB measurement
For all PUCCH transmission for each configured subcell for each slot 5G-L1-UL shall calculate the noise power per PRB estimation (interference + thermal noise) and reports this estimation to 5G-L2-PS.

There are following computations in 2 steps:

Step 1: 5G-L1-UL shall compute noise estimate per PUCCH format and per PRB, while considering all the PUCCH resources scheduled within the same PUCCH format and in the same PRB in the slot.

For PUCCH format0 transmission 5G-L1-UL shall estimate power noise per symbol. This estimate is based on cyclic shifts other than the cyclic shifts used for signal and two adjacent to them another cyclic shifts. It is described in section 2.4.1.1.5 of the 5Gmax algorithm specifications.

All calculated power noise for each symbol per PRB are averaged for a given PRB.

In case of inter-slot frequency hopping where 2 PRBs are used for a PUCCH format0 transmission 5G-L1-UL shall average Noise Power separately for each PRB.

Then, calculated noise power estimations 5G-L1-UL shall average over all the receiving antennas (spatial streams) for each PRB.

Step 2: In case of more than one PUCCH transmission in PRB (also in case of different formats) 5G-L1-UL shall compute one noise estimate per PRB averaged over all PUCCH transmission in the same PRB in the slot.

5G-L1-UL shall convert these estimated noise values to logarithmic scale in dBm unit. Power scaling and conversion to dBm unit shall be done as specified in [11458486](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAv6WPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) for Loki and [11458486](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAv6WPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) for Thor-BB.

5G-L1-UL shall report noise power per PRB measurement via L1-L2 IF parameter: UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->noisePerPrb . Type of parameter is array of float32, where array indices are selected according to PRB positions.

Noise Power per PRB estimation algorithm is specified in section 2.8.3.4 of the 5GMax algorithm specification.

Noise Power per PRB measurement for PUCCH format0 is supported for following L1 variants:

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | Technology | FR1-TDD | FR2-TDD | First Feature |
| L1 HW | Loner | not supported | not supported | - |
| Loki | supported | supported | CB008021 |  |
| Thor | not supported | supported | CB009027 |  |
| Odin |  |  |  |  |

Note:

1. When only zero-valued samples are got from the radio module or (e)CPRI interface for all the receiving antennas (spatial streams) (e.g. broken antenna scenario or protection switching in TSN), in case of noisy measurement, or for non-scheduled PRBs, 5G-L1-UL shall report INVALID value.
2. For invalid values for Noise Power per PRB measurements please find details in: [12714973](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_lIqIEGjtEfC_xcanjXaboQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

---

###### 5.3.5.1.4.6.1.4 Frozen Requirement

**5.3.5.1.4.6.1.4.0-1**  (ID: `11456575`)

Frozen Requirement
[CNI-108168]

For common requirements (for different formats) for Noise Power measurement please find chapter 5G\_L1\_17243\_replaced([11458250](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAvTSfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) in chapter "PUCCH processing\ Format 3"

[END CNI-108168]

---

###### 5.3.5.1.4.6.2 Signal power

###### 5.3.5.1.4.6.2.1 General

**5.3.5.1.4.6.2.1.0-1**  (ID: `13340026`)

General
For PUCCH format0 5G-L1-UL shall estimate Signal Power per symbol and per Rx spatial stream.

5G-L1-UL shall calculate the power of each cyclic shift correlation per symbol per Rx spatial stream.

Signal Power estimation is specified in sections 2.4.1.1.6 and 2.4.1.5 of the 5GMax algorithm specification.

Note:

The signal power is estimated after cyclic shift detection.

---

###### 5.3.5.1.4.6.2.2 Signal Power Selection

###### 5.3.5.1.4.6.2.2.0-1 Signal Power Selection For PUCCH format0 5G-L1-UL shall select Signal Power regarding to cyclic shift with maximal likelihood metric. The maximum likelihood value of used cyclic shift (CSmax) is got from MLSE detection. (ID: 13343070)

###### 5.3.5.1.4.6.2.3 Signal Power Processing

###### 5.3.5.1.4.6.2.3.0-1 Signal Power Processing For PUCCH format0 5G-L1-UL shall calculate Signal Power per spatial stream. Signal Power per spatial stream calculation is proceed based on on Signal Power estimation. (ID: 13343977)

###### 5.3.5.1.4.6.2.4 Received power

###### 5.3.5.1.4.6.2.4-1 Received power

**5.3.5.1.4.6.2.4.0-1**  (ID: `13340028`)

Received power
For PUCCH format0 for each scheduled resource 5G-L1-UL shall estimate one measurement for the UL received power and report it to 5G-L2-PS.

Each UL received power measurement shall be averaged over all the allocated RE and aggregated over all the receiving antennas. Then, one measurement normalized to one PRB shall be reported to L2 .

The scaling factor applied at the radio module to reach a target noise bitwidth shall be compensated at 5G-L1-UL for all the UL power measurements using the IE  UlCell\_SetupReq->rxScalingFactor  (for details see: [11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ), [11418478](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-ZJ5_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

5G-L1-UL shall report estimation via L1-L2 IF parameter: UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->rxPower .

The rxPower parameter is defined in dBm unit as illustrated in [11514200](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BRfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).

The UL received power estimation algorithm on PUCCH is described in section 2.8.4.2 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification: [11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) .

Note:

1. rxScalingFactor value is set as described in [11288559](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tp7ttPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)
2. When only zero-valued samples are received from the radio module or (e)CPRI interface for all the receiving antennas (eg. broken antenna scenario), 5G-L1-UL shall set the rxPower parameter sent in UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs message to invalid value  (-140dBm).
3. For invalid values for Received Power measurements please find: [12717252](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_AV0d4GmnEfC_xcanjXaboQ)
4. The measurement for the UL received power can be used as a level indicator for the UL power control.

---

###### 5.3.5.1.4.6.3 RSSI

**5.3.5.1.4.6.3.0-2**  (ID: `11456632`)

RSSI
[CNI-108168]

For common requirements (for different formats) for RSSI  measurement please find chapter 5G\_L1\_17245\_replaced([11458526](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAv6XfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))  in chapter "PUCCH processing\ Format 3"

[END CNI-108168]

---

###### 5.3.5.1.4.6.4 SINR

**5.3.5.1.4.6.4.0-2**  (ID: `11456648`)

SINR
[CNI-108168]

For common requirements (for different formats) for SINR  measurement please find chapter 5G\_L1\_17246\_replaced([11458550](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAwhYfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))  in chapter "PUCCH processing\ Format 3"

[END CNI-108168]

---

###### 5.3.5.1.4.6.5 DTX Metric

**5.3.5.1.4.6.5.0-1**  (ID: `13340135`)

DTX Metric
For PUCCH format0 5G-L1-UL shall calculate DTX metric which is used to indicate whether a PUCCH signal was transmitted and received as expected.

For Format0, since SR is reported in the same resource as for HARQ-AN (see 38.213 section 9.2.5.1), then only one DTX metric is computed for all UCI on PUCCH format0.

The DTX metric is calculated based on the maximum likelihood metric estimated for each possible cyclic shift.

The DTX metrics for PUCCH format0 are described in section  2.4.1.6  of the 5Gmax algorithm specification.

For DTX detection for PUCCH format0 details see: ([11456795: DTX Detection](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAn-i_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

---

###### 5.3.5.1.4.6.6 Power Adjustment and Scaling

**5.3.5.1.4.6.6.0-1**  (ID: `11456665`)

Power Adjustment and Scaling
[CNI-108168]

Requirements defining power scaling are stored in chapter 6 (see 5G\_L1\_4204\_replaced([11421346](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-hFsvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for Loki and 5G\_L1\_8907\_replaced([11422159](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-hswfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for Thor)

[END CNI-108168]

---

##### 5.3.5.1.4.7 UCI Decoding

###### 5.3.5.1.4.7.1 Hard Decision

**5.3.5.1.4.7.1.0-1**  (ID: `13343072`)

Hard Decision
For PUCCH format0 5G-L1-UL shall decode UCI bits.

The UCI bits are decoded on the maximum likelihood value of used cyclic shift (CSmax).

Hard decision is applied for cyclic shift to actual UCI information bits demapping.

Information of configured SR and HARQ-ACK bits are got from the UlData\_PucchReceiveReq .

For more information about Hard Decision see section 2.4.1.4 of the 5GMax algorithm specification.

---

###### 5.3.5.1.4.7.2 Decoding results

###### 5.3.5.1.4.7.2.1 Loki / Thor

**5.3.5.1.4.7.2.1.0-1**  (ID: `13332652`)

Loki / Thor
For PUCCH format0 5G-L1-UL shall report decoded UCI bits.

All necessary information to decode each signal received on PUCCH format0 (i.e., scheduled resource, number of UCI bits, etc.) are got from the UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message ([11513990](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MIfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For each decoded data on PUCCH (whatever the DTX decision: 'DTX' or 'nonDTX'), 5G-L1-UL shall provide to 5G-L2-PS the respective information in different messages described in ([11513958](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MGfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) as follows:

* The decoded UCI bits (HARQ-ACK bits without SR bit): the numOfBitsOfUciInformation UCI bits shall be reported in the field uciBits of the UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs message.
* The decoded HARQ-ACK bits: 5G-L1-UL shall report nANPucch decoded bits in the UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD message, with nANPucch standing for the number of HARQ-ACK bits which is got from message UlData\_PucchReceiveReq.
* The decoded SR bit: 5G-L1-UL shall report the decoded SR bit through the parameter srBit in the UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs message [PR864105, CB013151-A] and UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD message [End PR864105, CB013151-A], negative (0) or positive (1).

[CNI-108168-I] The requirement was refined under CNI-108168  [End CNI-108168-I]

---

###### 5.3.5.1.4.7.2.2 Loner

**5.3.5.1.4.7.2.2.0-1**  (ID: `13332941`)

Loner
For PUCCH format0 5G-L1-UL shall report decoded UCI bits.

All necessary information to decode each signal received on PUCCH format0 (i.e., scheduled resource, number of UCI bits, etc.) are got from the UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message ([11513990](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MIfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For each decoded data on PUCCH (whatever the DTX decision: 'DTX' or 'nonDTX'), 5G-L1-UL shall provide to 5G-L2-PS the respective information in different messages described in ([11513958](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MGfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) as follows:

* The decoded UCI bits (HARQ-ACK bits without SR bit): the numOfBitsOfUciInformation UCI bits shall be reported in the field uciBits of the UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs message.
* The decoded HARQ-ACK bits: 5G-L1-UL shall report nANPucch decoded bits in the UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD message, with nANPucch standing for the number of HARQ-ACK bits which is got from message UlData\_PucchReceiveReq.
* The decoded SR bit: 5G-L1-UL shall report the decoded SR bit through the parameter srBit in the UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs message negative (0) or positive (1).

[CNI-108168-J] The requirement was refined under CNI-108168  [End CNI-108168-J]

---

##### 5.3.5.1.4.8 DTX Detection

###### 5.3.5.1.4.8.1 General

**5.3.5.1.4.8.1.0-1**  (ID: `13343049`)

General
For PUCCH format0 5G-L1-UL shall use DTX metric to indicate whether an PUCCH signal was transmitted and received as expected.

The ACK missed detection probability shall be lower than 1% to meet 3GPP minimum requirements in TS 38.104

The DTX detection methods, metrics and thresholds for PUCCH format0 are described in section  2.4.1.6  of the 5Gmax algorithm specification.

The two terms used for PUCCH DTX decision (i.e. the metric and the threshold in the fixed-point representation) as well as the decision (i.e. DTX or nonDTX) should then be provided to 5G-L2-PS via parameters:

* UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->dtxMetric  
  and (when value of parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources-> nANPucch > 0) via:  
  UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->dtxMetric
* UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->dtxThreshold  
  and (when value of parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources-> nANPucch > 0) via:  
  UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->dtxThreshold

The results of DTX detection are sent to 5G-L2-PS via parameters:

UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->dtx  
and (when value of parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources-> nANPucch > 0) via:  
UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->dtx

Note:

1. 5G-L2-PS could use the DTX indication to filter reliable measurements performed on PUCCH (e.g. TO), to handle DL retransmission, etc.
2. The false alarm is defined as the probability to detect UCI reporting whereas nothing was sent on PUCCH

---

###### 5.3.5.1.4.8.2 Threshold for DTX decision

###### 5.3.5.1.4.8.2.1 Loki / Thor

**5.3.5.1.4.8.2.1.0-1**  (ID: `13343050`)

Loki / Thor
For PUCCH format0 5G-L1-UL shall use threshold for DTX decision.

Depending on:  
  - the number of scheduled symbols dedicated to PUCCH,  
  - the number of HarqAck bits,  
  - scheduled or not Send Request (SR bit),  
  - number of Rx spatial streams  
5G-L1-UL shall select the appropriate threshold for DTX decision. This selection shall be performed for each NR-slot where resources are scheduled for PUCCH transmission.

5G-L1-UL shall get information about the number of scheduled symbols, the number of HarqAck bits and SR bit flag from parameters:

UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->numOfSymbols

UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->nANPucch

UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->srBitDetection

5G-L1-UL shall infer the number of symbols dedicated to DMRS from the parameters:

UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->numCeAxCIndex

UlCell\_SetupReq->ulSubcellType

The corresponding values of threshold are defined internally in L1 software code as defined in section 2.4.1.6 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification in form of table.

Then, 5G-L1-UL shall use the DTX metric value ( [13340134: DTX Metric](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_M_fF0NvyEfCmxLW1M7HMrQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) to compare with dtxThreshold .

The thresholds and formulas for DTX decision are specified in  5GMAX algorithm spec chapter 2.4.1.6

Note:

1. The DTX indication shall be provided to 5G-L2-PS as described in ([12721868](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_mXk1EW2JEfCmnYHxzZN44w?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).

---

###### 5.3.5.1.4.8.2.2 Loner

**5.3.5.1.4.8.2.2.0-1**  (ID: `13343970`)

Loner
For PUCCH format0 5G-L1-UL shall use threshold for DTX decision.

Depending on:  
  - the number of scheduled symbols dedicated to PUCCH,  
  - the number of HarqAck bits,  
  - scheduled or not Send Request (SR bit),  
  - number of Rx spatial streams  
5G-L1-UL shall select the appropriate threshold for DTX decision. This selection shall be performed for each NR-slot where resources are scheduled for PUCCH transmission.

5G-L1-UL shall get information about the number of scheduled symbols, the number of HarqAck bits and SR bit from parameters:

UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->numOfSymbols

UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->nANPucch

UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->srBitDetection

5G-L1-UL shall infer the number of symbols dedicated to DMRS from the parameters:

UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->numCeAxCIndex

UlCell\_SetupReq->ulSubcellType

The corresponding values of thresholds are delivered from RAD parameters. There are two thresholds respectively for 2Rx and 4Rx spatial streams receivers. For details please see: ([11453048: RAD parameters for Loner](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAW4wfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).

Then, 5G-L1-UL shall use the DTX metric value ( [13340134: DTX Metric](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_M_fF0NvyEfCmxLW1M7HMrQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) to compare with dtxThreshold .

The thresholds and formulas for DTX decision are specified in  5GMAX algorithm spec chapter 2.4.1.6

Note:

1. The DTX indication shall be provided to 5G-L2-PS as described in ([12721868](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_mXk1EW2JEfCmnYHxzZN44w?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).

---

###### 5.3.5.1.4.8.3 Frozen requirements

###### 5.3.5.1.4.8.3.1 DTX threshold for PUCCH Format 0

**5.3.5.1.4.8.3.1.0-1**  (ID: `11456812`)

DTX threshold for PUCCH Format 0
**[CNI-59405]: CP2 part moved**

**DTX threshold for PUCCH Format 0**

Depending on several parameters related to PUCCH format 0 decoding (see below), 5G-L1-UL shall select the appropriate threshold for DTX decision. This selection shall be performed for each NR-slot where resources are scheduled for PUCCH transmission as follows:

1. From *UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message (see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_215), 5G-L1-UL gets the parameters:*
2. *nANPucch*
3. *numOfSymbols*
4. *srBitDetection*
5. *frequencyHopping*
6. **[Before 5GC000836-P] For 2Rx configuration, 5G-L1-UL uses the R&D parameter*rdPucchF0Thresholds2Rx (see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_1470) to derive the *dtxThreshold as illustrated in the Table 1 (see below). Then, 5G-L1-UL shall consider this threshold* to compute the DTX value (see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_1427). The DTX indication shall be provided to 5G-L2-PS as described in 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_1427.***\*\*
7. **[5GC000836-P] Depending on the number of RX antenna (see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_919), 5G-L1-UL uses the appropriate R&D parameter (see below bullets) to derive the *dtxThreshold as illustrated in the respective table. Then, 5G-L1-UL shall consider this threshold \*to compute the DTX value (see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_1427). The DTX indication shall be provided to 5G-L2-PS as described in 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_1427.***\*
8. For 2RX configuration, use the R&D parameter*rdPucchF0Thresholds2Rx (see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_1470) and derive* dtxThreshold according to Table 1 (see below)\*\*
9. **[Before 5GC001848-A] For FDD only** [5GC001848-A] For FDD and TDD FR1 [End 5GC001848-A] and for 4Rx configuration, use the R&D parameter*rdPucchF0Thresholds4Rx (see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_1471) and derive* dtxThreshold according to Table 2 (see below)**\***\*

***\*[End 5GC000836-P]***\*

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| *nANPucch* | *numOfSymbols* | *srBitDetection* | *frequencyHopping* | *dtxThreshold* |
| 0 | 1 | True | disabled | *rdPucchF0Thresholds2Rx[0]* |
| 1 | 1 | False | disabled | *rdPucchF0Thresholds2Rx[1]* |
| 2 | 1 | False | disabled | *rdPucchF0Thresholds2Rx[2]* |
| 1 | 1 | True | disabled | *rdPucchF0Thresholds2Rx[2]* |
| 2 | 1 | True | disabled | *rdPucchF0Thresholds2Rx[3]* |
| 0 | 2 | True | disabled | *rdPucchF0Thresholds2Rx[4]* |
| 1 | 2 | False | disabled | *rdPucchF0Thresholds2Rx[5]* |
| 2 | 2 | False | disabled | *rdPucchF0Thresholds2Rx[6]* |
| 1 | 2 | True | disabled | *rdPucchF0Thresholds2Rx[6]* |
| 2 | 2 | True | disabled | *rdPucchF0Thresholds2Rx[7]* |
| 0 | 2 | True | enabled | *rdPucchF0Thresholds2Rx[8]* |
| 1 | 2 | False | enabled | *rdPucchF0Thresholds2Rx[9]* |
| 2 | 2 | False | enabled | *rdPucchF0Thresholds2Rx[10]* |
| 1 | 2 | True | enabled | *rdPucchF0Thresholds2Rx[10]* |
| 2 | 2 | True | enabled | *rdPucchF0Thresholds2Rx[11]* |

**Table 1: DTX threshold computation for PUCCH format 0 and 2RX configuration**

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| *nANPucch* | *numOfSymbols* | *srBitDetection* | *frequencyHopping* | *dtxThreshold* |
| 0 | 1 | True | disabled | *rdPucchF0Thresholds4Rx[0]* |
| 1 | 1 | False | disabled | *rdPucchF0Thresholds4Rx[1]* |
| 2 | 1 | False | disabled | *rdPucchF0Thresholds4Rx[2]* |
| 1 | 1 | True | disabled | *rdPucchF0Thresholds4Rx[2]* |
| 2 | 1 | True | disabled | *rdPucchF0Thresholds4Rx[3]* |
| 0 | 2 | True | disabled | *rdPucchF0Thresholds4Rx[4]* |
| 1 | 2 | False | disabled | *rdPucchF0Thresholds4Rx[5]* |
| 2 | 2 | False | disabled | *rdPucchF0Thresholds4Rx[6]* |
| 1 | 2 | True | disabled | *rdPucchF0Thresholds4Rx[6]* |
| 2 | 2 | True | disabled | *rdPucchF0Thresholds4Rx[7]* |
| 0 | 2 | True | enabled | *rdPucchF0Thresholds4Rx[8]* |
| 1 | 2 | False | enabled | *rdPucchF0Thresholds4Rx[9]* |
| 2 | 2 | False | enabled | *rdPucchF0Thresholds4Rx[10]* |
| 1 | 2 | True | enabled | *rdPucchF0Thresholds4Rx[10]* |
| 2 | 2 | True | enabled | *rdPucchF0Thresholds4Rx[11]* |

**Table 2: DTX threshold computation for PUCCH format 0 and 4RX configuration**

NOTE: For TDD, PUCCH format 0 is supported for 1 or 2 HARQ-ACK bits and SR. For FDD, SR on PUCCH Format0 is not supported.

**[5GC001868-A] For TDD,** 5G-L1-UL shall support DTX thresholds for format0 with 2RX, nANPucch=1~2, numberOfSymbols=1 and srBitDetection=false in Loki L1 HW **[End 5GC001868-A]**\*\*\*\*

**[5GC001868-C] In addition, 5G-L1-UL shall support DTX thresholds for format0 with 2RX, nANPucch=1~2, numberOfSymbols=2, frequencyHopping=enabled and srBitDetection=false in Loki L1 HW** [End 5GC001868-C]\*\*\*\*

**[5GC002056-AA] For TDD FR1, 5G-L1-UL shall support DTX thresholds for format0 with 4RX in Loki L1 HW** [End 5GC002056-AA]\*\*\*\*

**[5GC001868-D] For FDD, 5G-L1-UL shall support DTX thresholds for format0 with 4RX, nANPucch=1~2, {numberOfSymbols, frequencyHopping}={1, disabled}, {2, enabled} and srBitDetection=false in Loki L1 HW** [End 5GC001868-D]\*\*\*\*

**[5GC002481-AA] For FDD FR1, 5G-L1-UL shall support DTX thresholds for format0 with 4RX in Loki L1 HW** [End 5GC002481-AA]\*\*\*\*

**[End CNI-59405]**

###### 5.3.5.1.4.8.3.2 AN only mode

###### 5.3.5.1.4.8.3.2.0-1 AN only mode L1 shall also support ‘AN only’ PUCCH format 0 detection, and use a different DTX thresholds accordingly. To explicitly indicate the existence of SR could reduce the miss detection and the probability of error decoding. To have a flexible L1 support, L2 shall indicate a SR occasion bit in PUCCH receive request, L1 then use this bit to choose correct DTX thresholds. (ID: 11456774)

#### 5.3.5.1.5 Receive Response and HARQ report preparation

##### 5.3.5.1.5.1 UCI and measurements report

**5.3.5.1.5.1.0-1**  (ID: `13339260`)

UCI and measurements report
For PUCCH format0 for each scheduled resource after decoding control data received on PUCCH and estimating measurements 5G-L1-UL shall return the UCI bits and a set of measurement metrics to the L2-PS via the message UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs.

Following L1L2 [IF](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_eam28HJJEfCRE7eh4Ndkrw) parameters 5G-L1-UL shall use to report UCI bits, measurements, DTX state, DTX metrics, DTX thresholds and CRC state:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs |  |
| Report / Measurement | L1L2 IF Parameter |
| UCI bits | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->uciBits |
| SR bit | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->srBit |
| DTX state | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->dtx |
| DTX metric | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->dtxMetric |
| DTX threshold | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->dtxThreshold |
| CRC state(4) | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->crc |
| Noise Power per PRB(5) | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->noisePerPrb |
| ST TA metric(4) | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->shortTermTaMetric |
| ST TA peak amplitude(4) | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->shortTermTaPeakAmp |
| Noise Power | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->noisePower |
| Received Power | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->rxPower |
| RSSI | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->rssi |
| SINR | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->sinr |
| ST FO metric(4) | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->shortTermCfoMetric |
| antenna-wise  ST FO(4) | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->extendedParameters->shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt |

Note:

1. For detailed L1L2 IF specification please find: ([11513962](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MGvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) and ([11514171](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR1aQ_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))
2. The endpoint address for UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs is defined via parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->addrPucchReceiveRespPs
3. In specific configuration parameters in above table 5G-L1-UL shall set to "invalid values". For details see: ([11454049](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAbxQPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) and ([11514171](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR1aQ_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))
4. Measurements not estimated for PUCCH format0 (related to measurements parameters values are meaningless).

5. For Loner this parameter is not estimated. For details see ([11514171](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR1aQ_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

[CNI-108168-J] The requirement was refined under CNI-108168  [End CNI-108168-J]

---

##### 5.3.5.1.5.2 HARQ report

###### 5.3.5.1.5.2.1 Loki / Thor

**5.3.5.1.5.2.1.0-1**  (ID: `13332237`)

Loki / Thor
For PUCCH format0 when parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->nANPucch is not equal "0", 5G-L1-UL shall send HARQ feedback, SR bit and set of DTX data (DTX state, DTX metric and its threshold) to the 5G-L2-PS via the message UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD.

Following L1L2 [IF](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_eam28HJJEfCRE7eh4Ndkrw) parameters 5G-L1-UL shall use to report HARQ feedback, DTX state, DTX metric and its threshold:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD |  |
| Report / Measurement | L1L2 IF Parameter |
| AN bits | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->ackNack |
| DTX decision | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->dtx |
| DTX metric | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->dtxMetric |
| DTX threshold | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->dtxThreshold |
| SR bit | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->srBit |
| CRC state(4) | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->crc |

Note:

1. For detailed L1L2 IF specification please find: ([11513962](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MGvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) and ([11514243](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BT_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))
2. The endpoint address for UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs is defined via parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->addrPucchReceiveRespHarqD
3. In specific configuration parameters in above table 5G-L1-UL shall set to "invalid values". For details see: ([11454049](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAbxQPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) and ([11514243](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BT_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))
4. Measurements not estimated for PUCCH format0 (related to measurements parameters values are meaningless).

[PR864105, CB013151-A]

Added parameter srBit to message UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqDL1sw.

[End PR864105, CB013151-A]

[CNI-108168-I] The requirement was refined under CNI-108168  [End CNI-108168-I]

---

###### 5.3.5.1.5.2.2 Loner

**5.3.5.1.5.2.2.0-1**  (ID: `13333068`)

Loner
For PUCCH format0 when parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->nANPucch is not equal "0", 5G-L1-UL shall send HARQ feedback and set of DTX data (DTX state, DTX metric and its threshold) to the 5G-L2-PS via the message UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD.

Following L1L2 [IF](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_eam28HJJEfCRE7eh4Ndkrw) parameters 5G-L1-UL shall use to report HARQ feedback, DTX state, DTX metric and its threshold:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD |  |
| Report / Measurement | L1L2 IF Parameter |
| AN bits | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->ackNack |
| DTX decision | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->dtx |
| DTX metric | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->dtxMetric |
| DTX threshold | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->dtxThreshold |
| CRC state(4) | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->crc |

Note:

1. For detailed L1L2 IF specification please find: ([11513962](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MGvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) and ([11514243](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BT_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))
2. The endpoint address for UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs is defined via parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->addrPucchReceiveRespHarqD
3. In specific configuration parameters in above table 5G-L1-UL shall set to "invalid values". For details see: ([11454049](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAbxQPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) and ([11514243](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BT_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))
4. Measurements not estimated for PUCCH format0 (related to measurements parameters values are meaningless).

[CNI-108168-J] The requirement was refined under CNI-108168  [End CNI-108168-J]

##### 5.3.5.2.1.2 Receiver modes

###### 5.3.5.2.1.2.1 FR1-TDD

###### 5.3.5.2.1.2.1.1 FR1-TDD CPRI

**5.3.5.2.1.2.1.1.0-1**  (ID: `12648879`)

FR1-TDD CPRI
For FR1-TDD CPRI for PUCCH format1, 5G-L1-UL shall use receivers with 2 and 4 antenna streams as below table.

Use of 2Rx or 4Rx is configurable per cell during cell setup phase (with parameter UlCell\_SetupReq->ulSubcellType).

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | mode | 2Rx MLD | 4Rx MLD | First Feature |
|  | ulSubcellType | C2 | C4 |  |
| L1  HW | Loner | Supported without pre-whitening | Supported without pre-whitening | legacy |
| Loki | Supported without pre-whitening | Supported without pre-whitening | legacy |  |
| Thor | Supported without pre-whitening | Supported without pre-whitening | CB010575 |  |

Notes:

References for signal processing path diagram for PUCCH format1 MLD receiver (without pre-whitening) are in: [12576682](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_YPMLcDA7EfCRMdP0Nuo3Hg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

For supported types of subcell please refer: [11381236](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uero9fvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

Abbreviations:

MLD: Maximum Likelihood Detection

---

###### 5.3.5.2.1.2.1.2 FR1-TDD eCPRI 7.2a

**5.3.5.2.1.2.1.2.0-2**  (ID: `12723290`)

FR1-TDD eCPRI 7.2a
For FR1-TDD eCPRI 7.2a, for PUCCH format1, 5G-L1-UL shall use receivers with 2,4 and 8 antenna streams as below table.

Use of 2Rx or 4Rx or 8Rx is configurable per cell during cell setup phase (with parameter UlCell\_SetupReq->ulSubcellType).

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | mode | 2Rx MLD | 4Rx MLD | 4Rx MLD | 8Rx MLD | First Feature |
|  | ulSubcellType | C2 | C4 | C8 | C8 |  |
| L1  HW | Loner | Supported without pre-whitening | Supported without pre-whitening | - | - | legacy |
| Loki | Supported\* without or with  pre-whitening | Supported\* without or with  pre-whitening | - | - | CB007950 |  |
| Thor | Supported\* without or with  pre-whitening | Supported\* without or with  pre-whitening | Supported *,*\* without or with  pre-whitening | Supported \*\*  with  pre-whitening | CB007487 |  |
| Odin | [CB012115-IA] Supported without pre-whitening [End CB012115-IA] | [CB012115-IA] Supported without pre-whitening [End CB012115-IA] |  |  | CB012115 |  |

Notes:

* For 2Rx and 4Rx receiver:
* when actPucchF1InterfEnhancement = 'true', pre-whitening is used for Data and DMRS
* when actPucchF1InterfEnhancement = 'false', pre-whitening is NOT used for Data and DMRS

5G-L1-UL shall receive initial parameter value for actPucchF1InterfEnhancement during cell setup via UlCell\_SetupReq->actPucchF1InterfEnhancement IE.  
5G-L1-UL shall receive reconfigured parameter value for actPucchF1InterfEnhancement via UlCell\_ParameterReconfigurationReq->actPucchF1InterfEnhancement IE.

For 8Rx receiver:

* Pre-whitening is always used for Data and DMRS without separate configuration or re-configuration.

\*\* For C8 for Thor, receiver mode can be 4Rx or 8Rx and it is indicated by UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcell->PucchResources->numCeAxCIndex.

References for signal processing path diagram for PUCCH format1 MLD receiver (w/o pre-whitening) are in: [12576682](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_YPMLcDA7EfCRMdP0Nuo3Hg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

References for signal processing path diagram for PUCCH format1 MLD receiver (with pre-whitening) are in: [12576683](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_jL-CEDA7EfCRMdP0Nuo3Hg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

For supported types of subcell please refer: [11381236](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uero9fvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

Abbreviations:

MLD: Maximum Likelihood Detection

\*\*\* pre-whitening is as a method to remove the antenna correlation of interference/noise. It can improve the performance of BER/BLER, miss detection and false alarm for color noise/interference cases. refer to '5GMax-5G New Radio Algorithm Specification' section 2.4.2.5 for algorithm implementation steps.

Abbreviations:

MLD: Maximum Likelihood Detection

\*\*pre-whitening is as a method to remove the antenna correlation of interference/noise. It can improve the performance of BER/BLER, miss detection and false alarm for color noise/interference cases. refer to '5GMax-5G New Radio Algorithm Specification' section 2.4.2.5 for algorithm implementation steps.

#### 5.3.5.2.2 Demapping

**5.3.5.2.2.0-2**  (ID: `13373043`)

Demapping
For PUCCH format1 5G-L1-UL shall pack frequency domain IQ samples from PRBs allocated to PUCCH resource in the buffer. According to list of PUCCH resources, received in the receive request, FD IQ samples from symbols carrying PUCCH are written in buffer.

For more details, please find section 2.1 and 2.4.2 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification.

Note:

For format1 within one PRB there is possibility to multiplex several PUCCH format1 resources.

Demapping is a part of common Front-End operations.

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

#### 5.3.5.2.3 Time offset compensation

**5.3.5.2.3.0-2**  (ID: `12723293`)

Time offset compensation
For FR1-TDD and FR1-FDD for PUCCH format1 5G-L1-UL shall support time offset compensation (TOC).

TOC is performed before channel estimation as specified in section 2.4.2.2 of the 5GMax algorithm specification.

TOC is applied to all received PUCCH format1 DMRS and data symbols.

Note:

The target time offset is used in TOC and it depends on actual FFT size.

The TOC is a part of common Front-End operations.

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

##### 5.3.5.2.3.1 Frozen Requirements

**5.3.5.2.3.1.0-1**  (ID: `11456869`)

Frozen Requirements
**[CNI-108168]**

For common frozen requirements (for different formats) for Time offet compensation please find chapter 5G\_L1\_17241\_replaced([11457734](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAs3CPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) in chapter "PUCCH processing**\ Format 3"**

**[END CNI-108168]**

#### 5.3.5.2.4 ZC Sequence Removal

##### 5.3.5.2.4.1 General

**5.3.5.2.4.1.0-2**  (ID: `12723295`)

General
For FR1-TDD and FR1-FDD for PUCCH format1 5G-L1-UL shall support ZC sequence removal as specified in section 2.4.2.3 of the 5GMax algorithm specification:[11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

##### 5.3.5.2.4.2 Frozen Requirement

###### 5.3.5.2.4.2.0-1 Frozen Requirement Thor (ID: 11456902)

**5.3.5.2.4.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11456910`)

Frozen Requirement
**PUCCH Format 1**

For Thor L1, ZC sequence removal is performed as specified in section 2.4.2.3 of the 5GMax algorithm specification (see 5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

**[RP003187-D] This requirement is applicable for L1** Thor FR1-TDD-eCPRI **[End RP003187-D]**\*\*\*\*

**[CB010575-A] The requirement is also applicable for L1** Thor for FR1-TDD-CPRI **[End CB010575-A]**\*\*\*\*
