#### 5.3.5.2.5 Cyclic Shift Correlation

**5.3.5.2.5.0-2**  (ID: `13373042`)

Cyclic Shift Correlation
For PUCCH format1 5G-L1-UL shall apply cyclic shift correlation operation.

This operation provide signal correlation with the 12 possible cyclic shifts. This is done with DFT of each symbol.

For more details, please find sections  2.4.2.4 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification.

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

##### 5.3.5.2.6 Data/DMRS extraction

**5.3.5.2.6.0-2**  (ID: `13373045`)

Data/DMRS extraction
For PUCCH format1 5G-L1-UL shall separate DMRS and DATA IQ samples for next processing.

For more details, please find 3GPP TS 38.211 (v17.3.0): chapter 6.3.2.4.2, 6.4.1.3.1.2 .

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

#### 5.3.5.2.7 Parameter estimation and measurement

##### 5.3.5.2.7.1 OCC Removal

**5.3.5.2.7.1.0-2**  (ID: `13373046`)

OCC Removal
For PUCCH format1 5G-L1-UL shall apply de-OCC operation.

The DMRS and data symbols of the UE specific cyclic shifts are separated from input signals. The output data is calculated separately for DMRS and data, for all resources (CS, OCC couple), antennas and hops.

For more details, please find sections  2.4.2.4 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification.

Note:

The operation is provided for UE used (scheduled) and unused resources. While Signal Power estimation and MLD are processing related to used resources, Noise Power estimation is based on unused resources in next operations.

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

##### 5.3.5.2.7.2 Noise power

###### 5.3.5.2.7.2.1 General

**5.3.5.2.7.2.1.0-4**  (ID: `12717201`)

General
For FR1-TDD and FR1-FDD for PUCCH format1 5G-L1-UL shall perform the Noise Power Estimation ([NPE](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_hle2YGenEfCk8v_SG2h2xg)).

Noise power estimation algorithm for PUCCH format 1 is described in section "2.4.2.5 Noise power and signal power estimation" of 5GMax algorithm specification: [11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).

Noise power estimation on a given PRB is computed over a set of unused resources determined by their cyclic shift (cs) and orthogonal cover code index (occ).

Noise power estimation is computed using so-called 'AllFreeRes' method described in section 2.4.2.5 of 5GMax algorithm specification: [1396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ). In this method, all unused resources (cs,occ) are considered. This method provides a more reliable estimator and is aligned with noise estimation in LTE PUCCH.

PUCCH F1 resources with different symbol lengths which are multiplexed in the same PRB need to be processed separately (de-OCC, NPE), due to different lengths of OCC sequence.

For NPE all possible OCCs corresponding to the CSs occupied by UEs with other symbol length should be excluded from unused resources.

UEs with different symbol length can't be multiplexed by OCC with same CS.

For details, please refer chapter 2.4.2.5 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification: [11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).

NOTE: For Format1, the noise is estimated on unused cs and occ within one PRB. This estimate includes both thermal noise + intra-cell interference since no orthogonality between the received signals associated with different cyclic shifts, in particular for adjacent cyclic shifts.

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

###### 5.3.5.2.7.2.2 Noise Power measurement

**5.3.5.2.7.2.2.0-2**  (ID: `12723327`)

Noise Power measurement
For FR1-TDD and FR1-FDD for PUCCH format1 for each scheduled resource 5G-L1-UL shall calculate the noise power (interference + thermal noise) on unused cyclic shifts within one PRB and reports this estimate to 5G-L2-PS.

This estimation is aggregating all receiving antennas. The unit of this estimate is dBm.

5G-L1-UL shall report estimate via L1-L2 IF parameters: UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->noisePower

Noise Power estimation algorithm is specified in section 2.8.3.3 of the 5GMax algorithm specification.

Noise Power measurement PUCCH format1 is supported for following L1 variants:

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | Technology | FR1-TDD (CPRI/ eCPRI-7.2a/ eCPRI-7.2e) | FR1-FDD (OBSAI/ CPRI/ eCPRI-7.2a) | First Feature |
| L1 HW | Loner | supported | supported | Legacy |
| Loki | supported | supported | Legacy |  |
| Thor | supported | supported | CB007487 |  |
| Odin | [CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] Supported for  FR1-TDD eCPRI-7.2a / FR1-TDD eCPRI-7.2e [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] | [CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] Supported for FR1-FDD CPRI / FR1-FDD eCPRI-7.2a [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] | CB012115 |  |

1. For invalid values for Noise Power measurements please find: ([12733068](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_mMhiRXRFEfCRE7eh4Ndkrw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

---

###### 5.3.5.2.7.2.3 Noise Power per PRB measurement

**5.3.5.2.7.2.3.0-2**  (ID: `12723335`)

Noise Power per PRB measurement
For all PUCCH transmission for each configured subcell for each slot 5G-L1-UL shall calculate the noise power per PRB estimation (interference + thermal noise) and reports this estimation to 5G-L2-PS.

There are following computations in 2 steps:

Step 1: 5G-L1-UL shall compute noise estimate per PUCCH format and per PRB, while considering all the PUCCH resources scheduled within the same PUCCH format and in the same PRB in the slot.

For PUCCH format1 transmission 5G-L1-UL shall estimate Noise Power as described in section 2.4.2.5 of the 5Gmax algorithm specifications.

5G-L1-UL shall average estimates over all the Rx spatial streams.

In case of intra-slot frequency hopping 5G-L1-UL shall estimate Noise Power as first part-hop and the second part-hop separately as two PUCCH transmissions with the same format with less symbol's quantity for each part. If intra-slot frequency hopping is enabled PUCCH format1 transmission could occupy 2 PRBs.

Noise Power for PUCCH format1 estimation must be achieved separately for PUCCH resources with different symbol length multiplexed in the same PRB.

Step 2: In case of more than one PUCCH transmission in PRB (also in case of different formats) 5G-L1-UL shall compute one noise estimate per PRB averaged over all PUCCH transmission in the same PRB in the slot.

5G-L1-UL shall convert these estimated noise values to logarithmic scale in dBm unit. Power scaling and conversion to dBm unit shall be done as specified in [11458486](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAv6WPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) for Loki and [11458486](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAv6WPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) for Thor-BB.

5G-L1-UL shall report noise power per PRB measurement via L1-L2 IF parameter: UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->noisePerPrb . Type of parameter is array of float32, where array indices are selected according to PRB positions.

Noise Power per PRB estimation algorithm is specified in section 2.8.3.4 of the 5GMax algorithm specification.

Noise Power per PRB measurement for PUCCH format1 is supported for following L1 variants:

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | Technology | FR1-TDD (CPRI/ eCPRI-7.2a/ eCPRI-7.2e) | FR1-FDD (OBSAI/ CPRI/ eCPRI-7.2a) | First Feature |
| L1 HW | Loner | not supported | not supported | - |
| Loki | supported | supported | CB008021 |  |
| Thor | supported | supported | CB009027 |  |
| Odin | [CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] Supported for  FR1-TDD eCPRI-7.2a / FR1-TDD eCPRI-7.2e [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] | [CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] Supported for FR1-FDD CPRI / FR1-FDD eCPRI-7.2a [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] | CB012115 |  |

Note:

1. When only zero-valued samples are got from the radio module or (e)CPRI interface for all the receiving antennas (spatial streams) (e.g. broken antenna scenario or protection switching in TSN), in case of noisy measurement, or for nonscheduled PRBs, 5G-L1-UL shall report INVALID value.
2. For invalid values for Noise Power per PRB measurements please find details in: [12714973](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_lIqIEGjtEfC_xcanjXaboQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

---

##### 5.3.5.2.7.3 Interference CoMa Estimation (Rdd)

**5.3.5.2.7.3.0-2**  (ID: `13373048`)

Interference CoMa Estimation (Rdd)
For PUCCH format1, if interference rejection (pre-whitening) is considered for interference scenarios, 5G-L1-UL shall calculate covariance matrix (Rdd) of interference plus noise in cyclic shift and OCC domain.

Disturbance estimation is proceeded for each Rx stream and each frequency hop.

For more details, please find sections  2.4.2.5 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification.

Note:

The interference rejection (pre-whitening) functionality is specified in:  [11457163: Pre-Whitened](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fApzu_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

[CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e [End CB012115-GA]

---

##### 5.3.5.2.7.4 Signal Power

###### 5.3.5.2.7.4.1 General

**5.3.5.2.7.4.1.0-2**  (ID: `12723349`)

General
For FR1-TDD and FR1-FDD for PUCCH format1 5G-L1-UL shall estimate Signal Power per Rx antenna (spatial stream).

Signal Power estimation is performed after ZC (Zadoff-Chu) sequence removal, the de-Orthogonal Cover Code (OCC), the DFT operations and the FOC operation.

Data Power and DMRS Power are both computed. The Signal Power estimation is performed subtracting Noise Power to the average of Data Power and DMRS Power. To keep the power unchanged after de-OCC and DFT operations, the Signal Power needs to be normalized.

Signal Power estimation is specified in section 2.4.2.5 of the 5GMax algorithm specification.

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

###### 5.3.5.2.7.4.2 Received Power

**5.3.5.2.7.4.2.0-2**  (ID: `12723358`)

Received Power
For FR1-TDD and FR1-FDD for PUCCH format1 for each scheduled resource 5G-L1-UL shall estimate one measurement for the UL received power and report it to 5G-L2-PS.

Each UL received power measurement shall be averaged over all the allocated REs and aggregated over all the receiving antennas. Then, one measurement normalized to one PRB shall be reported to L2 .

The scaling factor applied at the radio module to reach a target noise bitwidth shall be compensated at 5G-L1-UL for all the UL power measurements using the IE  UlCell\_SetupReq->rxScalingFactor  (for details see: [11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ), [11418478](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-ZJ5_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).

5G-L1-UL shall report estimation via L1-L2 IF parameter: UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->rxPower .

The rxPower parameter is defined in dBm unit as illustrated in [11514200](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BRfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

The UL received power estimation algorithm on PUCCH is described in section 2.8.4.2 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification: [11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) .

Note:

1. rxScalingFactor value is set as described in [11288559](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tp7ttPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)
2. When only zero-valued samples are received from the radio module or (e)CPRI interface for all the receiving antennas (eg. broken antenna scenario), 5G-L1-UL shall set the rxPower parameter sent in UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs message to invalid value  (-140dBm).
3. For invalid values for Received Power measurements please find: [12717252](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_AV0d4GmnEfC_xcanjXaboQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)
4. The measurement for the UL received power can be used as a level indicator for the UL power control.

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

##### 5.3.5.2.7.5 RSSI

**5.3.5.2.7.5.0-2**  (ID: `12723373`)

RSSI
For FR1-TDD and FR1-FDD for PUCCH format1 for each scheduled resource in slot 5G-L1-UL shall estimate one [RSSI](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_CtgTJmbXEfCwWbD4x7Iu-g) and report it to 5G-L2-PS.

For each scheduled resource 5G-L1-UL shall estimate one measurement. Each RSSI measurement shall be averaged by over all the allocated REs and aggregated over all the receiving antennas. Then, one measurement normalized to one PRB shall be reported to L2 for long term (LT) averaging.

The scaling factor applied at the radio module to reach a target noise bitwidth shall be compensated at 5G-L1-UL for all the RSSI measurements ([11404480](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e9UL0PvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) using the IE UlCell\_SetupReq->rxScalingFactor (see: [11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The rssi parameter is defined in dBm unit as illustrated in: [11514200](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BRfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

5G-L1-UL shall report estimation via L1-L2 IF parameter: UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->rssi

The RSSI estimation algorithm on PUCCH is described in section  "2.8.2.2 PUCCH" of the 5Gmax algorithm specification (see: [11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note:

1. rxScalingFactor value is set as described in [11288559](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tp7ttPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)
2. When only zero-valued samples are received from the radio module or (e)CPRI interface for all the receiving antennas (eg. broken antenna scenario), 5G-L1-UL shall set the rssi parameter sent in UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs message to invalid value  (-140dBm).
3. For invalid values for RSSI measurements please find: [12717253](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_MIieAGmnEfC_xcanjXaboQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)
4. The RSSI measurement can be used as a level indicator for the UL power control.

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

##### 5.3.5.2.7.6 SINR

**5.3.5.2.7.6.0-2**  (ID: `12723383`)

SINR
For FR1-TDD and FR1-FDD for PUCCH format1 for each scheduled resource 5G-L1-UL shall compute one SINR measurement.

For PUCCH format1, one estimate shall be then provided to 5G-L2-PS.

For format1 no equalization is performed. The SINR on PUCCH is computed as a ratio for RX power ([11457023](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fApMqPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) and noise power ([11456945](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAolnfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

The sinr parameter is defined in dB unit as illustrated in:[11514200](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BRfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

5G-L1-UL shall report estimation via L1-L2 IF parameter: UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->sinr .

The SINR estimation algorithm on PUCCH is described in section  "2.8.5.2 PUCCH" of the 5Gmax algorithm specification (see:[11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note:

1. The thermal noise and the interference will be measured together, i.e., they won't be resolved independently.
2. Since PUCCH format1 is mapped to single logical antenna port (no layer mapping as per 38.211 section 6.3.2), 5G-L1-UL shall report invalid value for the SINR measurement associated to the layer index > 1
3. In the case of invalid measurements for SINR 5G-L1-UL shall report to 5G-L2-PS the value: -255 dB.
4. For invalid values for SINR measurements please find: [12717254](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Ow_uAGmnEfC_xcanjXaboQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

##### 5.3.5.2.7.7 DTX Metric

**5.3.5.2.7.7.0-2**  (ID: `13373052`)

DTX Metric
For FR1-TDD and FR1-FDD for PUCCH format1 5G-L1-UL shall estimate metric which is use to indicate whether an PUCCH signal was transmitted and received as expected.

The DTX metric is calculated based on MLD detection results.

The DTX metric for PUCCH format1 are described in section  2.4.2.7  of the 5Gmax algorithm specification.

For DTX detection for PUCCH format1 details see: ([11457227: DTX Detection](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAqaxPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

##### 5.3.5.2.7.8 Power Adjustment and Scaling

**5.3.5.2.7.8.0-1**  (ID: `11457095`)

Power Adjustment and Scaling
[CNI-108168]

Requirements defining power scaling are stored in chapter 6 (see 5G\_L1\_4204\_replaced([11421346](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-hFsvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for Loki and 5G\_L1\_8907\_replaced([11422159](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-hswfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for Thor)

[END CNI-108168]

---

#### 5.3.5.2.8 Rdd Processing

##### 5.3.5.2.8.1 Shrinkage procedure

**5.3.5.2.8.1.0-2**  (ID: `13373061`)

Shrinkage procedure
For PUCCH format1, if interference rejection (pre-whitening) is considered for interference scenarios, 5G-L1-UL shall apply shrinkage algorithm to covariance matrix (Rdd) to improve estimation.

Shrinkage algorithm is performed for each Rx stream and each frequency hop.

For more details, please find sections  2.4.2.5 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification.

Note:

The interference rejection (pre-whitening) functionality is specified in:  [11457163: Pre-Whitened](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fApzu_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

[CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e [End CB012115-GA]

---

##### 5.3.5.2.8.2 Cholesky Decomposition and Rdd Inversion

**5.3.5.2.8.2.0-2**  (ID: `13373062`)

Cholesky Decomposition and Rdd Inversion
For PUCCH format1, if interference rejection (pre-whitening) is considered for interference scenarios, for calculation of pre-whitening matrix, 5G-L1-UL shall apply Cholesky decomposition and inversion for Rdd matrix (after shrinkage).

Then the matrix is scaled by Noise Power.

For more details, please find sections  2.4.2.5 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification.

Note:

The interference rejection (pre-whitening) functionality is specified in:  [11457163: Pre-Whitened](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fApzu_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

[CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e [End CB012115-GA]

---

#### 5.3.5.2.9 UE specific processing

##### 5.3.5.2.9.1 Frequency Offset Compensation

###### 5.3.5.2.9.1.1 General

###### 5.3.5.2.9.1.1.1 FR1-TDD

**5.3.5.2.9.1.1.1.0-2**  (ID: `12723386`)

FR1-TDD
For FR1-TDD for PUCCH format1 5G-L1-UL shall support frequency offset compensation (FOC).

For each Rx antenna stream 5G-L1-UL shall perform compensation of the Frequency Offset (FO) for Inter-symbol DMRS and DATA symbols.

For FOC 5G-L1-UL shall use Long Term Carrier Frequency Offset metric which 5G-L1-UL received via parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->longTermCfoMetricOfBeam .

The FOC algorithm is specified in section 2.4.2.1 of the 5GMax algorithm specification.

FOC is supported in following HWs:

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | Technology | FR1-TDD-CPRI | FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a | FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e | First Feature |
| L1 HW | Loner | not supported |  | - | Legacy |
| Loki | supported |  | - | CB007449 |  |
| Thor | supported |  |  | CB007487 |  |
| Odin |  | [CB012115-IA] Supported [End CB012115-IA] | [CB012115-GA] Supported [End CB012115-GA] | CB012115 |  |

The mapping between LT FOC and spatial stream is defined in: [12580627:](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_idMawTGfEfCRMdP0Nuo3Hg?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

Note:

1. Before FOC 5G-L1-UL shall perform “LT CFO validation for value 0” for each Rx antenna stream, see [12580643](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_qjrkQDGgEfCRMdP0Nuo3Hg?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) for details. 5G-L1-UL shall assume frequency offset equals 0Hz (no compensation) if LT CFO == 0+j0 is received.

---

###### 5.3.5.2.9.1.1.2 FR1-FDD

**5.3.5.2.9.1.1.2.0-2**  (ID: `13391524`)

FR1-FDD
For FR1-FDD for PUCCH format1 5G-L1-UL shall support frequency offset compensation (FOC).

For each Rx antenna stream 5G-L1-UL shall perform compensation of the Frequency Offset (FO) for Inter-symbol DMRS and DATA symbols.

For FOC 5G-L1-UL shall use Long Term Carrier Frequency Offset metric which 5G-L1-UL received via parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->longTermCfoMetricOfBeam .

The FOC algorithm is specified in section 2.4.2.1 of the 5GMax algorithm specification.

FOC is supported in following HWs:

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | Technology | FR1-FDD-OBSAI | FR1-FDD-CPRI | FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a | First Feature |
| L1 HW | Loner | - | supported(2) | - | CB009107 |
| Loki | supported |  |  | CB007449 |  |
| Thor | supported |  |  | CB007487 |  |
| Odin |  | [CB012115-JA] Supported [End CB012115-JA] | [CB012115-LA] Supported [End CB012115-LA] |  |  |

The mapping between LT FOC and spatial stream is defined in: [12580627:](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_idMawTGfEfCRMdP0Nuo3Hg?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

Note:

1. Before FOC 5G-L1-UL shall perform “LT CFO validation for value 0” for each Rx antenna stream, see [12580643](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_qjrkQDGgEfCRMdP0Nuo3Hg?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) for details. 5G-L1-UL shall assume frequency offset equals 0Hz (no compensation) if LT CFO == 0+j0 is received.
2. From E2E for Loner, FOC is supported when NRBTS.NRCELL.actSupercellSingleSSB = True

---

###### 5.3.5.2.9.1.2 Long Term CFO mapping to spatial streams

**5.3.5.2.9.1.2.0-2**  (ID: `12723390`)

Long Term CFO mapping to spatial streams
5G-L1-UL shall perform antenna-wise FOC using antenna-wise LT-FOE longTermCfoMetricOfBeam received in the UlData\_PucchReceiveReq for PUCCH fomat1 as described in section 2.4.2.1 of the 5GMax New Radio Algorithm Specification document. Where mapping between LT FOE and spatial stream is defined as follows:

A2 or C2:

-longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[0]: (ce)AxC [0]

-longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[1]: (ce)AxC [1]

A4 or C4:

-longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[0]: (ce)AxC [0]

-longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[1]: (ce)AxC [1]

-longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[2]: (ce)AxC [2]

-longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[3]: (ce)AxC [3]

C8 or C8'2 or C8'4 or C8'8  or A8 :

-longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[0]: ceAxC [0]

-longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[0]: ceAxC [1]

-longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[1]: ceAxC [2]

-longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[1]: ceAxC [3]

-longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[2]: ceAxC [4]

-longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[2]: ceAxC [5]

-longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[3]: ceAxC [6]

-longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[3]: ceAxC [7]

Note:

1. For C8, C8'2, C8'4, C8'8 and A8 each element of longTermCfoMetricOfBeam corresponds to two continuous ceAxC streams. 5G\_L1\_UL shall duplicate longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[i] for ceAxC [2i+1] where i = 0,1,2,3.

2. For C8, C8'2, C8'4, C8'8  if 4Rx receiver is configured, only the first two elements of longTermCfoMetricOfBeam are valid and they correspond to ceAxC[0-3]. 5G-L1-UL shall expect the last two elements as invalid value.

1. For C2, C4, A2, A4 Long term CFO metric is sent for each Rx stream. Each value corresponds to one Rx antenna stream.

4. For eCPRI case, the order eAxC spatial stream values of the LT-FOE (longTermCfoMetricOfBeam) in the array and their mapping to beam patternId shall follow the same mapping order of EcpriConfig struct in 5G\_L1\_IF\_15453\_replaced([11514119](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR1aN_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).

1. The parameter longTermCfoMetricOfAnt is changed to longTermCfoMetricOfBeam in MULTI and L1SW in 23R4, refer to 5G\_L1\_13041\_replaced([11396378](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8r5xPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

###### 5.3.5.2.9.1.3 Frozen Requirement

###### 5.3.5.2.9.1.3.0-2 Frozen Requirement Loner (ID: 11456877)

**5.3.5.2.9.1.3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11456886`)

Frozen Requirement
For PUCCH format 1, frequency offset estimation (FOE) is not supported as additional DMRS is not supported.

Inter-symbol FOC is supported for F1 and F3 format based on long-term CFO metric computed at 5g-L2-PS for each Rx antenna stream for a given UE. For calculation of antenna-wise CFO, L1-SW shall conduct CFO compensation per Rx antenna stream for both data and DMRS as specified in 5GMax algorithm specification (section 2.4.2.1).

L1 shall calculate FOC for PUCCH F1 acording to instruction in 5GMax. Pilot distance shall be considered as 4 and first pilot shall be 0.

---

##### 5.3.5.2.9.2 Pre-Whitened

###### 5.3.5.2.9.2.1 2RX and 4RX

###### 5.3.5.2.9.2.1.0-2 2RX and 4RX 5G-L1-UL shall be support pre-whitening for 4RX PUCCH F1 receiver when actPucchF1InterfEnhancement in the cell setup or cell parameter reconfiguration message is set to true in TDD FR1 related cell types; this is valid for Loki. [CB014386-B] Support for pre-whitening is further extended to Loki 2RX; and Thor 2RX and 4RX when actPucchF1InterfEnhancement in the cell setup or cell parameter reconfiguration message is set to true in TDD FR1[End CB014386-B]  . (ID: 12490742)

###### 5.3.5.2.9.2.2 8RX

**5.3.5.2.9.2.2.0-3**  (ID: `12723412`)

8RX
For FR1-TDD eCPRI-7.2a and FR1-TDD eCPRI-7.2e and FR1-FDD eCPRI-7.2a 5G-L1-UL shall support 8Rx pre-whitening for PUCCH F1 when 8Rx receiver mode is configured.

Supported receiver modes are specified in: [12576664](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_0LHvADA0EfCRMdP0Nuo3Hg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

##### 5.3.5.2.9.3 Demodulation and Signal Detection

###### 5.3.5.2.9.3.1 MLD

**5.3.5.2.9.3.1.0-2**  (ID: `12977672`)

MLD
5G-L1-UL shall support MLD (Maximum Likelihood Detection) algorithm for PUCCH format1.

Supported receiver modes are specified in:  [12576664: Receiver modes for F1](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_0LHvADA0EfCRMdP0Nuo3Hg?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

For more details, please find section 2.4.2.7  of the 5Gmax algorithm specification.

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

###### 5.3.5.2.9.3.2 Decoding results

**5.3.5.2.9.3.2.0-2**  (ID: `13373063`)

Decoding results
For FR1-TDD and FR1-FDD for PUCCH format1 5G-L1-UL shall report decoded UCI bits.

All necessary information to decode each signal received on PUCCH (i.e., scheduled resource, number of UCI bits, etc.) are got from the UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message ([11513990](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MIfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For each decoded data on PUCCH format1 (whatever the DTX decision: 'DTX' or 'nonDTX'), 5G-L1-UL shall provide to 5G-L2-PS the respective information in different messages described in ([11513958](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MGfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) as follows:

* The decoded UCI bits: the nANPucch number of UCI (for format1 there only HARQ-ACK ) bits shall be reported in the field uciBits of the UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs message.
* The decoded HARQ-ACK bits: 5G-L1-UL shall report the nANPucch decoded bits in the UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD message, with nANPucch standing for the number of HARQ-ACK bits which is got from message UlData\_PucchReceiveReq.
* Scheduling Request (SR) information. Format1 SR is not transmitted as a physical SR bit (meaning BPSK/QPSK modulated bit) but based on the PUCCH resource, in which the UE's transmission was received.

•    When nANPUCCH equals to 0,   
only one PUCCH resource is allocated for a UE and this resource is used for SR signaling only. In this case, successful detection (non-DTX) indicates that a UE sent SR. In addition, UE is instructed to send a bit "0" with BPSK, but the physical bit is not used for anything.  
•    When nANPUCCH > 0,   
there are two possible resources (SR + HARQ-ACK and HARQ-ACK only) for a UE to choose the transmission instant. One resource for one UE is reserved for SR + HARQ-ACK, the other resource for HARQ-ACK only. Depending on the detection decision (DTX vs non-DTX) of the two resources, the outcome is either SR + HARQ-ACK bit(s) or HARQ-ACK bit(s) only.

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

##### 5.3.5.2.9.4 DTX Detection

###### 5.3.5.2.9.4.1 General

**5.3.5.2.9.4.1.0-2**  (ID: `12723406`)

General
For FR1-TDD and FR1-FDD for PUCCH format1 5G-L1-UL shall use metric that indicates whether an PUCCH signal was transmitted and received as expected.

The ACK missed detection probability shall be lower than 1% to meet 3GPP minimum requirements in TS 38.104

The DTX detection methods, metrics and thresholds for PUCCH format1 are described in section  2.4.2.8  of the 5Gmax algorithm specification.

The two terms used for PUCCH DTX decision (i.e. the metric and the threshold in the fixed-point representation) as well as the decision (i.e. DTX or nonDTX) should then be provided to 5G-L2-PS via parameters:

* UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->dtxMetric  
  and (when value of parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources-> nANPucch > 0) via:  
  UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->dtxMetric
* UlData\_PucchReceiveRespRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->dtxThreshold  
  and (when value of parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources-> nANPucch > 0) via:  
  UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->dtxThreshold

The results of DTX detection are sent to 5G-L2-PS via parameters:

UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->dtx  
and (when value of parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources-> nANPucch > 0) via:  
UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->dtx

Note:

1. 5G-L2-PS could use the DTX indication to filter reliable measurements performed on PUCCH (e.g. TO), to handle DL retransmission, etc.
2. The false alarm is defined as the probability to detect UCI reporting whereas nothing was sent on PUCCH
3. If only SR is expected and no HARQ-AN in a given slot: DTX is computed for PRBs resources configured for SR reporting and one DTX metric is reported to 5G-L2-PS for the current UE.
4. If only HARQ-AN is reported by the UE and no SR is expected in the same slot, DTX is computed for the PRBs resource configured for HARQ-AN and one DTX metric is reported to 5G-L2-PS.
5. If HARQ-AN is reported by the UE during one SR slot, DTX is computed for the 2 below PUCCH resources. Then it shall report two DTX decisions for the current UE, one for each resource. PRBs resource configured for SR which should be used by the UE to report HARQ-AN and positive SR in the same slot. PRBs resource configured for HARQ-AN which should be used by the UE to report HARQ-AN in case of no positive SR.

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

###### 5.3.5.2.9.4.2 Threshold for DTX decision

###### 5.3.5.2.9.4.2.1 MLD Receiver

###### 5.3.5.2.9.4.2.1.1 Loki / Thor / Odin

**5.3.5.2.9.4.2.1.1.0-2**  (ID: `12982096`)

Loki / Thor / Odin
For FR1-TDD and FR1-FDD 5G-L1-UL for PUCCH format1 shall use threshold for DTX decision for MLD receiver.

Depending on whether SR is multiplexed with A/N and whether frequency hopping is activated, 5G-L1-UL shall select the appropriate threshold for DTX decision. This selection shall be performed for each NR-slot where resources are scheduled for PUCCH transmission.

5G-L1-UL shall get information about frequency hopping and number and type of UCI bits from parameters:

UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->srBitDetection

UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->nANPucch

UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->numOfBitsOfUciInformation

UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->frequencyHopping

UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->numCeAxCIndex

UlCell\_SetupReq->ulSubcellType

The corresponding values of threshold are defined internally in L1 software code as defined in section  2.4.2.8  of the 5Gmax algorithm specification for [MLD](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_ywZXQWYHEfCwWbD4x7Iu-g) receiver. This threshold is an array of length 16 such as:

- dtxThreshold#1is used for SR only and no frequency hopping with 2 Rx.

- dtxThreshold#2 is used for 1-bit HARQ ACK  and no frequency hopping with 2 Rx.

- dtxThreshold#3 is used for 2 HARQ ACK bits or multiplexing SR and 1-bit HARQ ACK and no frequency hopping for both PUCCH resources with 2 Rx.

- dtxThreshold#4 is used for multiplexing SR and 2-bit HARQ ACK and no frequency hopping for both PUCCH resources.

- dtxThreshold#5 is used for SR only with 2 Rx and frequency hopping or with 4 Rx and no frequency hopping.

- dtxThreshold#6 is used for 1-bit HARQ ACK  with 2 Rx and frequency hopping or with 4 Rx and no frequency hopping.

- dtxThreshold#7 is used for 2 HARQ ACK bits or multiplexing SR and 1-bit HARQ ACK with 2 Rx and frequency hopping or with 4 Rx and no frequency hopping.

- dtxThreshold#8 is used for multiplexing SR and 2-bit HARQ ACK with 2 Rx and frequency hopping or with 4 Rx and no frequency hopping.

- dtxThreshold#9 is used for SR only with 4 Rx and frequency hopping or with 8 Rx and no frequency hopping.

- dtxThreshold#10 is used for 1-bit HARQ ACK with 4 Rx and frequency hopping or with 8 Rx and no frequency hopping.

- dtxThreshold#11 is used for 2 HARQ ACK bits or multiplexing SR and 1-bit HARQ ACK with 4 Rx and frequency hopping or with 8 Rx and no frequency hopping.

- dtxThreshold#12 is used for multiplexing SR and 2-bit HARQ ACK with 4 Rx and frequency hopping or with 8 Rx and no frequency hopping.

- dtxThreshold#13 is used for SR only with 8 Rx and frequency hopping.

- dtxThreshold#14 is used for 1-bit HARQ ACK with 8 Rx and frequency hopping.

- dtxThreshold#15 is used for 2 HARQ ACK bits or multiplexing SR and 1-bit HARQ ACK with 8 Rx and frequency hopping.

- dtxThreshold#16 is used for multiplexing SR and 2-bit HARQ ACK with 8 Rx and frequency hopping.

Then, 5G-L1-UL shall use the DTX metric value (see [12721877](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_EujUYG2nEfCmnYHxzZN44w?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) to compare with dtxThreshold .

Note:

1. The DTX indication shall be provided to 5G-L2-PS as described in ([12721877](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_EujUYG2nEfCmnYHxzZN44w?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).
2. PUCCH format 1 is supported for 1 or 2 HARQ-ACK bits and SR and frequency hopping enabled or disabled.
3. The DTX detection thresholds for PUCCH format1 are described in section  2.4.2.8  of the 5Gmax algorithm specification.

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

###### 5.3.5.2.9.4.2.1.2 Loner

**5.3.5.2.9.4.2.1.2.0-1**  (ID: `12721883`)

Loner
For FR1-TDD and FR1-FDD 5G-L1-UL for PUCCH format1 shall use threshold for DTX decision for MLD receiver.

Depending on whether SR is multiplexed with A/N and whether frequency hopping is activated, 5G-L1-UL shall select the appropriate threshold for DTX decision. This selection shall be performed for each NR-slot where resources are scheduled for PUCCH transmission.

5G-L1-UL shall get information about frequency hopping and number and type of UCI bits from parameters:

UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->srBitDetection

UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->nANPucch

UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->numOfBitsOfUciInformation

UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->frequencyHopping

UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->numCeAxCIndex

UlCell\_SetupReq->ulSubcellType

The corresponding thresholds are given in the R&D parameters rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMld (see [11453138: rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMld](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAW4xvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) for an MLD (maximum likelihood detection) receiver. This R&D parameter is an array of length 12 such as:

- dtxThreshold = rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMld[0] is used for SR only and no frequency hopping with 2 Rx.

- dtxThreshold = rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMld[1] is used for 1-bit HARQ ACK  and no frequency hopping with 2 Rx.

- dtxThreshold = rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMld[2] is used for 2 HARQ ACK bits or multiplexing SR and 1-bit HARQ ACK and no frequency hopping for both PUCCH resources with 2 Rx.

- dtxThreshold = rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMld[3] is used for multiplexing SR and 2-bit HARQ ACK and no frequency hopping for both PUCCH resources.

- dtxThreshold = rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMld[4] is used for SR only with 2 Rx and frequency hopping or with 4 Rx and no frequency hopping.

- dtxThreshold = rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMld[5] is used for 1-bit HARQ ACK  with 2 Rx and frequency hopping or with 4 Rx and no frequency hopping.

- dtxThreshold = rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMld[6] is used for 2 HARQ ACK bits or multiplexing SR and 1-bit HARQ ACK with 2 Rx and frequency hopping or with 4 Rx and no frequency hopping.

- dtxThreshold = rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMld[7] is used for multiplexing SR and 2-bit HARQ ACK with 2 Rx and frequency hopping or with 4 Rx and no frequency hopping.

- dtxThreshold = rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMld[8] is used for SR only with 4 Rx and frequency hopping.

- dtxThreshold = rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMld[9] is used for 1-bit HARQ ACK with 4 Rx and frequency hopping.

- dtxThreshold = rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMld[10] is used for 2 HARQ ACK bits or multiplexing SR and 1-bit HARQ ACK with 4 Rx and frequency hopping.

- dtxThreshold = rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMld[11] is used for multiplexing SR and 2-bit HARQ ACK with 4 Rx and frequency hopping.

Then, 5G-L1-UL shall use the DTX metric value to compare with dtxThreshold .

Note:

1. The DTX indication shall be provided to 5G-L2-PS as described in ([12721877](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_EujUYG2nEfCmnYHxzZN44w?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).
2. PUCCH format 1 is supported for 1 or 2 HARQ-ACK bits and SR and frequency hopping enabled or disabled.
3. The DTX detection thresholds for PUCCH format1 are described in section  2.4.2.8  of the 5Gmax algorithm specification.

[CNI-108168-I] The requirement was refined under CNI-108168  [End CNI-108168-I]

---

###### 5.3.5.2.9.4.3 Frozen Requirement

###### 5.3.5.2.9.4.3.1 FR1-TDD

**5.3.5.2.9.4.3.1.0-1**  (ID: `11457250`)

FR1-TDD
TDD FR1 L1 Loner/Loki [RP003187-F], Thor [End RP003187-F] : Depending on whether SR is multiplexed with A/N and whether frequency hopping is activated, 5G-L1-UL shall select the appropriate threshold for DTX decision. This selection shall be performed for each NR-slot where resources are scheduled for PUCCH transmission.

5G-L1-UL gets the parameters numOfBitsOfUciInformation and numOfSymbols from the UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message.

PUCCH format 1 is supported for 1 or 2 HARQ-ACK bits and SR.

The corresponding thresholds are given in the R&D parameters rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMrc(see 5G\_L1\_8805\_replaced([11453146](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAW4x_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for an MRC (maximum ratio combining ) receiver with 2 Rx antennas. This R&D parameter is an array of length 5 such that

- dtxThreshold = rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMrc[0] is used for SR only or A/N only and no frequency hopping;

- dtxThreshold = rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMrc[1] is used for SR only or A/N only with frequency hopping;

- dtxThreshold = rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMrc[2] is used for multiplexing SR and A/N and no frequency hopping for both PUCCH resources;

- dtxThreshold = rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMrc[3] is used  for multiplexing SR and A/N and no frequency hopping for one of the PUCCH resources (the other PUCCH resource using frequency hopping);

- dtxThreshold = rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMrc[4] is used  for multiplexing SR and A/N with frequency hopping for both PUCCH resources.

For 4 Rx antennas the thresholds are obtained by the below formula:

dtxThreshold4Rx= 0.7071*dtxThreshold + 126.53*Nhop

Nhop is 2 when frequencyHopping in UlData\_PucchReceiveReq is set to "enabled". Otherwise, it is set to 1

The corresponding thresholds are given in the R&D parameters rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMld (see 5G\_L1\_3361) for an MLD (maximum likelihood detection) receiver. This R&D parameter is an array of length 12 such that

- dtxThreshold = rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMld[0] is used for SR only and no frequency hopping with 2 Rx.

- dtxThreshold = rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMld[1] is used for 1-bit HARQ ACK  and no frequency hopping with 2 Rx.

- dtxThreshold = rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMld[2] is used for 2 HARQ ACK bits or multiplexing SR and 1-bit HARQ ACK and no frequency hopping for both PUCCH resources with 2 Rx.

- dtxThreshold = rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMld[3] is used for multiplexing SR and 2-bit HARQ ACK and no frequency hopping for both PUCCH resources.

- dtxThreshold = rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMld[4] is used for SR only with 2 Rx and frequency hopping or with 4 Rx and no frequency hopping.

- dtxThreshold = rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMld[5] is used for 1-bit HARQ ACK  with 2 Rx and frequency hopping or with 4 Rx and no frequency hopping.

- dtxThreshold = rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMld[6] is used for 2 HARQ ACK bits or multiplexing SR and 1-bit HARQ ACK with 2 Rx and frequency hopping or with 4 Rx and no frequency hopping.

- dtxThreshold = rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMld[7] is used for multiplexing SR and 2-bit HARQ ACK with 2 Rx and frequency hopping or with 4 Rx and no frequency hopping.

- dtxThreshold = rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMld[8] is used for SR only with 4 Rx and frequency hopping.

- dtxThreshold = rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMld[9] is used for 1-bit HARQ ACK with 4 Rx and frequency hopping.

- dtxThreshold = rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMld[10] is used for 2 HARQ ACK bits or multiplexing SR and 1-bit HARQ ACK with 4 Rx and frequency hopping.

- dtxThreshold = rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMld[11] is used for multiplexing SR and 2-bit HARQ ACK with 4 Rx and frequency hopping.

MLD method is chosen for implementation. However if a MRC receiver is used, MRC metric should be used.

Then, 5G-L1-UL shall use the DTX metric value (see 5G\_L1\_8355\_replaced([11457966](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAuFJvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to compare with dtxThreshold . The DTX indication shall be provided to 5G-L2-PS as described in 5G\_L1\_8356\_replaced([11458713](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAxIefvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

HW-Technology Map:

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Technology / HW | Loner | Loki | Thor |
| FR1-TDD-CPRI | Supported | Supported | [CB010575-A] Supported [End CB010575-A] |
| FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI | Supported | Supported | Supported |
| FR1-TDD-7-2e-eCPRI | NA | NA | [CB009514-F] Supported [End CB009514-F] |

[RP003187-F] The requirement is also applicable for L1 Thor for FR1-TDD-eCPRI. [End RP003187-F]

---

###### 5.3.5.2.9.4.3.2 FR1-FDD

**5.3.5.2.9.4.3.2.0-1**  (ID: `11457269`)

FR1-FDD
FDD FR1 L1 Loner : Depending on whether SR is multiplexed with A/N and whether frequency hopping is activated, 5G-L1-UL shall select the appropriate threshold for DTX decision. This selection shall be performed for each NR-slot where resources are scheduled for PUCCH transmission.

5G-L1-UL gets the parameters numOfBitsOfUciInformation and numOfSymbols from the UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message.

PUCCH format 1 is supported for 1 or 2 HARQ-ACK bits and SR.

The corresponding thresholds are given in the R&D parameters rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMrc(see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_1472 5G\_L1\_3360 5G\_L1\_8805\_replaced([11453146](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAW4x_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for an MRC (maximum ratio combining ) receiver with 2 Rx antennas. This R&D parameter is an array of length 5 such that

- dtxThreshold = rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMrc[0] is used for SR only or A/N only and no frequency hopping;

- dtxThreshold = rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMrc[1] is used for SR only or A/N only with frequency hopping;

- dtxThreshold = rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMrc[2] is used for multiplexing SR and A/N and no frequency hopping for both PUCCH resources;

- dtxThreshold = rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMrc[3] is used  for multiplexing SR and A/N and no frequency hopping for one of the PUCCH resources (the other PUCCH resource using frequency hopping);

- dtxThreshold = rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMrc[4] is used  for multiplexing SR and A/N with frequency hopping for both PUCCH resources.

For 4 Rx antennas the thresholds are obtained by the below formula:

dtxThreshold4Rx= 0.7071*dtxThreshold + 126.53*Nhop

Nhop is 2 when frequencyHopping in UlData\_PucchReceiveReq is set to "enabled". Otherwise, it is set to 1

The corresponding thresholds are given in the R&D parameters rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMld (see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_1473 5G\_L1\_3361 5G\_L1\_8806\_replaced([11453163](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAW4yfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for an MLD (maximum likelihood detection) receiver. This R&D parameter is an array of length 12 such that

- dtxThreshold = rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMld[0] is used for SR only and no frequency hopping with 2 Rx.

- dtxThreshold = rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMld[1] is used for 1-bit HARQ ACK  and no frequency hopping with 2 Rx.

- dtxThreshold = rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMld[2] is used for 2 HARQ ACK bits or multiplexing SR and 1-bit HARQ ACK and no frequency hopping for both PUCCH resources with 2 Rx.

- dtxThreshold = rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMld[3] is used for multiplexing SR and 2-bit HARQ ACK and no frequency hopping for both PUCCH resources.

- dtxThreshold = rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMld[4] is used for SR only with 2 Rx and frequency hopping or with 4 Rx and no frequency hopping.

- dtxThreshold = rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMld[5] is used for 1-bit HARQ ACK  with 2 Rx and frequency hopping or with 4 Rx and no frequency hopping.

- dtxThreshold = rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMld[6] is used for 2 HARQ ACK bits or multiplexing SR and 1-bit HARQ ACK with 2 Rx and frequency hopping or with 4 Rx and no frequency hopping.

- dtxThreshold = rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMld[7] is used for multiplexing SR and 2-bit HARQ ACK with 2 Rx and frequency hopping or with 4 Rx and no frequency hopping.

- dtxThreshold = rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMld[8] is used for SR only with 4 Rx and frequency hopping.

- dtxThreshold = rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMld[9] is used for 1-bit HARQ ACK with 4 Rx and frequency hopping.

- dtxThreshold = rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMld[10] is used for 2 HARQ ACK bits or multiplexing SR and 1-bit HARQ ACK with 4 Rx and frequency hopping.

- dtxThreshold = rdPucchF1DtxThresholdsMld[11] is used for multiplexing SR and 2-bit HARQ ACK with 4 Rx and frequency hopping.

MLD method is chosen for implementation. However if a MRC receiver is used, MRC metric should be used.

Then, 5G-L1-UL shall use the DTX metric value (see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_1427 5G\_L1\_8355\_replaced([11457966](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAuFJvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to compare with dtxThreshold . The DTX indication shall be provided to 5G-L2-PS as described in 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_1427 5G\_L1\_8356\_replaced([11458713](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAxIefvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[5GC002481-AA] For FDD, the above procedure shall be supported in L1 Loki HW. [End 5GC002481-AA]

[RP003187-M] The requirement is also applicable for L1 Thor for FR1-FDD-CPRI. [End RP003187-M]

[Before-CNI-122313-A]

[CB009444-I] This requirement is applicable in RINLINE1 HW for FR1-FDD-eCPRI. [End CB009444-I]

[CNI-122313-A]

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

[End CNI-122313-A]

---

#### 5.3.5.2.10 Receive Response and HARQ report preparation

##### 5.3.5.2.10.1 UCI and measurements report

**5.3.5.2.10.1.0-2**  (ID: `12729732`)

UCI and measurements report
For FR1-TDD and FR1-FDD for PUCCH format1 for each scheduled resource after decoding control data received on PUCCH and estimating measurements 5G-L1-UL shall returns the UCI bits and a set of measurement metrics to the L2-PS via the message UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs.

Following L1L2 [IF](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_eam28HJJEfCRE7eh4Ndkrw) parameters 5G-L1-UL shall use to report UCI bits, measurements, DTX state, DTX metrics, DTX thresholds and CRC state:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs |  |
| Report / Measurement | L1L2 IF Parameter |
| UCI bits | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->uciBits |
| SR bit | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->srBit |
| DTX state | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->dtx |
| DTX metric | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->dtxMetric |
| DTX threshold | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->dtxThreshold |
| CRC state(4) | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->crc |
| Noise Power per PRB(5) | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->noisePerPrb |
| ST TA metric(4) | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->shortTermTaMetric |
| ST TA peak amplitude(4) | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->shortTermTaPeakAmp |
| Noise Power | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->noisePower |
| Received Power | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->rxPower |
| RSSI | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->rssi |
| SINR | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->sinr |
| ST FO metric(4) | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->shortTermCfoMetric |
| antenna-wise  ST FO(4) | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->extendedParameters->shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt |

Note:

1. For detailed L1L2 IF specification please find: ([11513962](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MGvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) and ([11514171](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR1aQ_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))
2. The endpoint address for UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs is defined via parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->addrPucchReceiveRespPs
3. In specific configuration parameters in above table 5G-L1-UL shall set to "invalid values". For details see: ([11454049](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAbxQPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) and ([11514171](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR1aQ_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))
4. Measurements not estimated for PUCCH format1 (related to measurements parameters values are meaningless).

5. For Loner this parameter is not estimated. For details see ([11514171](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR1aQ_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

##### 5.3.5.2.10.2 HARQ report

###### 5.3.5.2.10.2.1 Loki / Thor / Odin

**5.3.5.2.10.2.1.0-2**  (ID: `12729729`)

Loki / Thor / Odin
For FR1-TDD and FR1-FDD for PUCCH format1 when parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->nANPucch is not equal "0", 5G-L1-UL shall send HARQ feedback, SR bit status and set of DTX data (DTX state, DTX metric and its threshold) to the 5G-L2-PS via the message UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD.

Following L1L2 [IF](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_eam28HJJEfCRE7eh4Ndkrw) parameters 5G-L1-UL shall use to report HARQ feedback, SR bit status, DTX state, DTX metric and its threshold:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD |  |
| Report / Measurement | L1L2 IF Parameter |
| AN bits | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->ackNack |
| DTX decision | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->dtx |
| DTX metric | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->dtxMetric |
| DTX threshold | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->dtxThreshold |
| SR bit(5) | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->srBit |
| CRC state(4) | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->crc |

Note:

1. For detailed L1L2 IF specification please find: ([11513962](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MGvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) and ([11514243](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BT_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))
2. The endpoint address for UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs is defined via parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->addrPucchReceiveRespHarqD
3. In specific configuration parameters in above table 5G-L1-UL shall set to "invalid values". For details see: ([11454049](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAbxQPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) and ([11514243](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BT_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))
4. Measurements not estimated for PUCCH format1 (related to measurements parameters values are meaningless).
5. For specification of setting of parameter srBit see: ([11453947: Parameter srBit](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAbKM_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

### 5.3.5.3 PUCCH Format 2

**5.3.5.3.1.1.1.0-1**  (ID: `13256102`)

MMSE Receiver
Below references illustrates the Signal Processing for PUCCH format2 with MMSE receiver.

##### 5.3.5.3.1.2 Receiver modes

###### 5.3.5.3.1.2.1 FR1-TDD

###### 5.3.5.3.1.2.1.1 FR1-TDD CPRI

**5.3.5.3.1.2.1.1.0-1**  (ID: `13256545`)

FR1-TDD CPRI
For FR1-TDD CPRI, for PUCCH format2, 5G-L1-UL shall use receivers with 2 and 4 antenna streams as below table.

Use of 2Rx or 4Rx is configurable per cell during cell setup phase (with parameter UlCell\_SetupReq->ulSubcellType).

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | mode | 2Rx MMSE MRC\* | 4Rx MMSE MRC | First Feature |
|  | ulSubcellType | C2 | C4 |  |
| L1 HW | Loner | supported | supported | legacy |
| Loki | supported | supported | legacy |  |

Notes:

References for signal processing path diagram for PUCCH format2 MMSE receiver: [11104931: PUCCH Format 2 Receiver](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koDnTvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

For supported types of subcell please refer: [11381236](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uero9fvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

Abbreviations:

\*MMSE: Minimum Mean Square Error,  MRC: Maximum Ratio Combining
