\*MMSE: Minimum Mean Square Error,  MRC: Maximum Ratio Combining

---

###### 5.3.5.3.1.2.2.2 FR2-TDD eCPRI 7.2a

**5.3.5.3.1.2.2.2.0-1**  (ID: `13256212`)

FR2-TDD eCPRI 7.2a
For FR2-TDD eCPRI-7.2a, for PUCCH format2, 5G-L1-UL shall use receivers with 2 antenna streams as below table.

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | mode | 2Rx MMSE MRC\* | First Feature |
|  | ulSubcellType | D2 |  |
| L1 HW | Loner | supported | legacy |
| Loki | supported | CB007596 |  |
| Thor | supported | CB010576 |  |
| Odin |  |  |  |

Notes:

References for signal processing path diagram for PUCCH format2 MMSE receiver: [11104931: PUCCH Format 2 Receiver](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koDnTvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

For supported types of subcell please refer: [11381236](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uero9fvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

Abbreviations:

\*MMSE: Minimum Mean Square Error,  MRC: Maximum Ratio Combining

---

###### 5.3.5.3.1.2.3 FR1-FDD

###### 5.3.5.3.1.2.3.1 FR1-FDD CPRI

**5.3.5.3.1.2.3.1.0-1**  (ID: `13256554`)

FR1-FDD CPRI
For FR1-FDD CPRI, for PUCCH format2, 5G-L1-UL shall use receivers with 2 and 4 antenna streams as below table.

Use of 2Rx or 4Rx is configurable per cell during cell setup phase (with parameter UlCell\_SetupReq->ulSubcellType).

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | mode | 2Rx MMSE MRC\* | 4Rx MMSE MRC | First Feature |
|  | ulSubcellType | A2 | A4 |  |
| L1 HW | Loner | supported | supported | legacy |

Notes:

References for signal processing path diagram for PUCCH format2 MMSE receiver: [11104931: PUCCH Format 2 Receiver](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koDnTvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

For supported types of subcell please refer: [11381236](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uero9fvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

Abbreviations:

\*MMSE: Minimum Mean Square Error,  MRC: Maximum Ratio Combining

---

###### 5.3.5.3.1.2.4 Frozen Requirements

###### 5.3.5.3.1.2.4.1 FR1-TDD

**5.3.5.3.1.2.4.1.0-1**  (ID: `11456409`)

FR1-TDD
Receivers with 4 and 2 antenna streams are supported. For PUCCH format 0 and 2, 4 Rx MLSE and MMSE algorithm shall be supported, respectively.  Use of 2Rx or 4Rx is configurable per cell during cell setup phase by using IE ulSubcellType.

Refer to 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_151 5G\_L1\_IF\_152\_replaced([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for configured ulSubcellType.

Refer to 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_919 5G\_L1\_2797\_replaced([11481465](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fDeeOPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for mapping of ulSubcellType to number of Rx antennas.

[5GC001868-A] 5G-L1-UL shall also support PUCCH reception with 2 antenna streams in Loki L1 HW, using MLSE and MMSE algorithms for format0 and format 2 respectively [End 5GC001868-A]

[5GC002056-AA] 5G-L1-UL shall also support PUCCH reception with 4 antenna streams in Loki L1 HW, using MLSE and MMSE algorithms for format0 and format 2 respectively [End 5GC002056-AA]

[RP003187-A] For PUCCH in L1 Thor following algorithms shall be supported: format 1:  2Rx MLD MRC, format 3: 2Rx MMSE MRC [End RP003187-A]

[RP003187-B] For PUCCH in L1 Thor following algorithms shall be supported: format 1: 4Rx MLD MRC, format 3: 4Rx MMSE MRC [End RP003187-B]

---

###### 5.3.5.3.1.2.4.2 FR1-FDD

**5.3.5.3.1.2.4.2.0-1**  (ID: `11456400`)

FR1-FDD
Receiver with 2 antenna streams is supported. For PUCCH format 2, MMSE algorithm is used.

[5GC000836-P]Receiver with 4 antenna streams is additionally supported. For PUCCH format 0 and 2, 4 Rx MLSE and MMSE algorithm shall be supported, respectively. Use of 2Rx or 4Rx is configurable per cell during cell setup phase by using IE ulSubcellType.

Refer to 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_151 5G\_L1\_IF\_152\_replaced([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for configured ulSubcellType.

Refer to 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_919 5G\_L1\_2797\_replaced([11481465](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fDeeOPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for mapping of ulSubcellType to number of Rx antennas.

Note: The corresponding AxC mapping can be found in 5G\_UP\_2501.

[5GC001868-D] 5G-L1-UL shall also support PUCCH reception with 4 antenna streams in Loki L1 HW, using MMSE algorithm [End 5GC001868-D]

[5GC001972-A]  5G-L1-UL shall also support PUCCH reception with 2 antenna streams in vDU L1 HW. [End 5GC001972-A]

[5GC001972-B]  In addition, 5G-L1-UL shall also support PUCCH reception with 4 antenna streams in vDU L1 HW. [End 5GC001972-B]

[RP003187-H] For PUCCH in L1 Thor following algorithms shall be supported: format 1:  2Rx MLD MRC, format 3: 2Rx MMSE MRC [End RP003187-H]

[RP003187-I] For PUCCH in L1 Thor following algorithms shall be supported: format 1: 4RX MLD MRC, format 3: 4RX MMSE MRC [End RP003187-I]

---

#### 5.3.5.3.2 Demapping

**5.3.5.3.2.0-1**  (ID: `13256769`)

Demapping
For PUCCH format2 5G-L1-UL shall pack frequency domain IQ samples from PRBs allocated to PUCCH resource in the buffer. According to list of PUCCH resources, received in the receive request, FD IQ samples from symbols carrying PUCCH are written in buffer.

For more details, please find sections 2.1 and 2.4.3 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification.

Note:

Demapping is a part of common Front-End operations.

---

#### 5.3.5.3.3 Time offset compensation

**5.3.5.3.3.0-2**  (ID: `13256955`)

Time offset compensation
For PUCCH format2 5G-L1-UL shall support Time Offset Compensation ([TOC](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_FykXkGXPEfCwWbD4x7Iu-g)).

TOC is performed before raw channel estimation as specified in section 2.4.3.2 of the 5GMax algorithm specification.

TOC is applied to all received PUCCH format2 DMRS and data symbols.

Note:

The estimated target time offset (TOe) is used in TOC.

The TOC is a part of common Front-End operations.

[CNI-108168-J] The requirement was refined under CNI-108168  [End CNI-108168-J]

---

##### 5.3.5.3.4 Data/DMRS extraction

###### 5.3.5.3.4.0-1 Data/DMRS extraction For PUCCH format2 5G-L1-UL shall separate DMRS and DATA IQ samples for next processing. For more details, please find 3GPP TS 38.211 (v17.3.0): ch. 6.3.2.6.5, 6.4.1.3.3.2 . (ID: 13256972)

#### 5.3.5.3.5 Parameter estimation and measurement

##### 5.3.5.3.5.1 Raw channel estimation

**5.3.5.3.5.1.0-1**  (ID: `13256994`)

Raw channel estimation
For PUCCH format2 5G-L1-UL DMRS shall perform DMRS based raw channel estimation.

For 1 and 2 OFDM symbols configurations (with and without FH), linear interpolation algorithm is applied per OFDM symbol as specified in section 2.4.3.1.5 of the 5GMax algorithm specification.

Raw channel estimation is specified in section 2.4.3.1.1 and 2.4.3.1.2 of the 5GMax algorithm specification.

---

##### 5.3.5.3.5.2 DMRS Parameter Estimation

###### 5.3.5.3.5.2.1 Time offset estimation

###### 5.3.5.3.5.2.1.1 General

**5.3.5.3.5.2.1.1.0-1**  (ID: `13258026`)

General
For PUCCH format2 5G-L1-UL shall perform Time Offset Estimation ([TOE](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_jHPVsGWGEfCtwYrh0KQ_DA)). TO is estimated per Rx spatial stream (antenna-wise).

TOE is specified in section 2.4.3.4 of the 5GMax algorithm specification.

Note:

TOE reliability depends on the number of PRBs.

The IFFT size is fixed to 64-point in PUCCH .

For PUCCH format 2, the search window for time offset estimation is symmetric.

---

###### 5.3.5.3.5.2.1.2 Time Offset Measurements

**5.3.5.3.5.2.1.2.0-1**  (ID: `13258036`)

Time Offset Measurements
For PUCCH format2 5G-L1-UL shall estimates Short Term ([ST](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_8sZYsGWLEfCtwYrh0KQ_DA)) Time Offset ([TO](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_A8Ba0GWMEfCtwYrh0KQ_DA)) on PUCCH and reports the TO estimate (TOE) to 5G-L2-PS for update the Timing Advance ([TA](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_FB5EAGWMEfCtwYrh0KQ_DA)) measurement.

5G-L1-UL shall report a following measurements via L1-L2 IF parameters:

* Short Term Timing Advance Metric: UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->shortTermTaMetric
* Short Term Timing Advance Peak Amplitude: UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->shortTermTaPeakAmp

TOE measurements are specified in section 2.8.6 of the 5GMax algorithm specification.

Supported measurements for TOE for following L1 variants:

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | Measurement | ST TA Metric | ST TA Peak Amplitude | First Feature |
| L1 HW | Loner | supported | supported | Legacy |
| Loki | supported | supported | Legacy |  |
| Thor | supported | supported | CB010576 |  |
| Odin |  |  |  |  |

Note:

1. 5G-L1-UL shall report both measurements (ST TA Metric and ST TA Peak Amplitude)  across all the RX antennas (shall be combined before report to 5G-L2-PS).
2. The unit of ST TA Metric reported to 5G-L2-PS is equal to Tsμ where Tsμ = (1/2μ) \* Ts, where

Ts is defined in:[11491325](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tRtPzPv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ) , and μ  is defined in: [11491448](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tRt23vv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)

1. ST TOE on PUCCH is performed only when a PUCCH format2 is scheduled over 3 RBs or more. For Format2 with 1 or 2 PRBs  the reported measurements are invalid for ST TA Metric and ST TA Peak Amplitude.
2. The number of configured RX antenna is derived according to [12576677](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wsVMkDA3EfCRMdP0Nuo3Hg?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) .
3. For invalid values for ST TO measurements please find: [12709927](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_pqASwGXAEfCwWbD4x7Iu-g?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

---

###### 5.3.5.3.5.2.1.3 Power Delay Profile

**5.3.5.3.5.2.1.3.0-1**  (ID: `13335856`)

Power Delay Profile
For PUCCH format2 5G-L1-UL shall estimate Power Delay Profile (PDP).

PDP estimation is performed per Rx stream and per DMRS symbol.

Estimated PDP is used for MMSE smoothing operation.

For more details, please find section 2.4.3.4.4  of the 5Gmax algorithm specification.

[CNI-108168-J] The requirement was refined under CNI-108168  [End CNI-108168-J]

---

###### 5.3.5.3.5.2.1.4 Frozen Requirements

**5.3.5.3.5.2.1.4.0-1**  (ID: `11457379`)

Frozen Requirements
[CNI-108168]

For common requirements (for different formats) for Time offet estimation please find chapter 5G\_L1\_17428\_replaced([11458028](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAuFLfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) in chapter "PUCCH processing\ Format 3"

[END CNI-108168]

---

###### 5.3.5.3.5.2.1.4.1 FFT size

**5.3.5.3.5.2.1.4.1.0-1**  (ID: `11457411`)

FFT size
[Before 5GC001981-A] For PUCCH format 2, the IFFT size used in time offset estimation (TOE) is minimum of 512 and “FFT size/2”, the FFT size is dependent on configuration of ulBandwidth and Scs which are derived from UlCell\_SetupReq message (5G\_L1\_5G21A\_151 5G\_L1\_IF\_152\_replaced([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). [End 5GC001981-A]

[5GC001981-A] [CB007403-C]  [CB007403-E] The IFFT size is fixed to 64 in PUCCH Format 2 TO estimation, as described in section "2.4.3.9.1 TO Estimation in Time Domain" of 5GMax New Radio Algorithm Specefication document (5G\_L1\_5G21A\_916 5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). [End 5GC001981-A] [End CB007403-C] [End CB007403-E]

[Before 5GC002006-A] For PUCCH format 2, the search window length for time offset estimation (TOE) is equal to CP length. [End 5GC002006-A]

[5GC002006-A, CB007326-A] [CB007403-C] [CB007403-E]For PUCCH format 2, the search window length for time offset estimation is changed to 2/3 CP length, and the search window range is also changed to be symmetric. [End 5GC002006-A, CB007326-A] [End CB007403-C] [End CB007403-E]

[5GC001868-A] 5G-L1-UL shall also support the above algorithm(same as 5GC002006-A) in Loki L1 HW [End 5GC001868-A]

[Before-CNI-122313-A]

[CB009881-A, CB009881-CG] This requirement shall be supported in RINLINE1 HW for FR1-TDD-eCPRI.[End CB009881-A, CB009881-CG]

[CNI-122313-A]

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

[End CNI-122313-A]

---

###### 5.3.5.3.5.2.1.4.2 Power Delay Profile

**5.3.5.3.5.2.1.4.2.0-1**  (ID: `11457395`)

Power Delay Profile
[Before 5GC001981-B] Adaptive average PDP (Power Delay Profile) length determination is supported for PUCCH Format 2, as described in section 2.4.3.8.4 of 5GMax New Radio Algorithm Specefication document (5G\_L1\_5G21A\_916 5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[5GC001981-B] [CB007403-C] [CB007403-E]

{

Adaptive per RX PDP (Power Delay Profile) length determination is supported for PUCCH Format 2, as described in section 2.4.3.8.4 of 5GMax New Radio Algorithm Specefication document (5G\_L1\_5G21A\_916 5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The per Rx PDP length selection has same performance compare to combined PDP length, with the benefit of less complexity.

The simulation report is available at "[Performance comparison between combined and per Rx smoother indicator.pptx](https://nokia.sharepoint.com/sites/5Gdoc/AS_Tech_Spec/CFAMs/5GC1800-5GC1999/5GC001981%20-%20L1%20algorithm%20changes%20-%205G19B/Simulation%20Reports/Performance%20comparison%20between%20combined%20and%20per%20Rx%20smoother%20indicator.pptx)"

}

[5GC001981-B] [End CB007403-C] [End CB007403-E]

[5GC001868-A] 5G-L1-UL shall also support the adaptive per RX PDP for PUCCH F2 as described above in Loki L1 HW [End 5GC001868-A]

---

###### 5.3.5.3.5.2.2 Noise power

###### 5.3.5.3.5.2.2.1 General

**5.3.5.3.5.2.2.1.0-2**  (ID: `13258073`)

General
For PUCCH format2 5G-L1-UL shall perform the Noise Power Estimation ([NPE](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_hle2YGenEfCk8v_SG2h2xg)) per symbol. Noise Power is estimated per Rx spatial stream.

NPE is specified in section 2.4.3.1.3 of the 5GMax algorithm specification.

[CNI-108168-J] The requirement was refined under CNI-108168  [End CNI-108168-J]

---

###### 5.3.5.3.5.2.2.2 Noise Power Estimation measurement

**5.3.5.3.5.2.2.2.0-1**  (ID: `13258090`)

Noise Power Estimation measurement
For PUCCH format2 for each scheduled resource 5G-L1-UL shall calculate the noise power (interference + thermal noise) and reports this estimate to 5G-L2-PS.

This estimate is derived while considering only the allocated PRBs for a given resource. This estimate is normalized to one PRB and aggregating over all receiving antennas. The unit of this estimate is dBm.

5G-L1-UL shall report estimate via L1-L2 IF parameters: UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->noisePower

Noise Power estimation algorithm is specified in section 2.8.3.3 and 2.4.3.1.3 of the 5GMax algorithm specification.

Noise Power measurement for PUCCH format2 is supported for following L1 variants:

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | Technology | FR1-TDD (CPRI/ eCPRI-7.2a/) | FR2-TDD (CPRI/ eCPRI-7.2a) | FR1-FDD (CPRI) | First Feature |
| L1 HW | Loner | supported | supported for CPRI | supported | Legacy |
| Loki | supported | supported for eCPRI-7.2a | - | Legacy |  |
| Thor | - | supported for eCPRI-7.2a | - | CB010576 |  |
| Odin |  |  |  |  |  |

1. For invalid values for Noise Power measurements please find: ([12733068](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_mMhiRXRFEfCRE7eh4Ndkrw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

---

###### 5.3.5.3.5.2.2.3 Noise Power per PRB measurement

**5.3.5.3.5.2.2.3.0-1**  (ID: `12714976`)

Noise Power per PRB measurement
For all PUCCH transmission for each configured subcell for each slot 5G-L1-UL shall calculate the noise power per PRB estimation (interference + thermal noise) and reports this estimation to 5G-L2-PS.

There are following computations in 2 steps:

Step 1: 5G-L1-UL shall compute noise estimate per PUCCH format and per PRB, while considering all the PUCCH resources scheduled within the same PUCCH format and in the same PRB in the slot.

For PUCCH format2 transmission 5G-L1-UL shall estimate noise power on DMRS as described in section 2.4.3.1.3 of the 5Gmax algorithm specifications.

Then calculated noise power 5G-L1-UL shall average over all resources in slot for different PUCCH format2 transmission.

Then, 5G-L1-UL shall average estimates over all the receiving antennas (spatial streams).

In case of frequency hopping 5G-L1-UL shall estimate noise power as first part-hop and the second part-hop separately as two PUCCH transmissions with the same format with less symbol's quantity for each part.

Step 2: In case of more than one PUCCH transmission in PRB (also in case of different formats) 5G-L1-UL shall compute one noise estimate per PRB averaged over all PUCCH transmission in the same PRB in the slot.

5G-L1-UL shall convert these estimated noise values to logarithmic scale in dBm unit. Power scaling and conversion to dBm unit shall be done as specified in  [11458486](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAv6WPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) for Loki and [11458486](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAv6WPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) for Thor-BB.

5G-L1-UL shall report noise power per PRB measurement via L1-L2 IF parameter: UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->noisePerPrb . Type of parameter is array of float32, where array indices are selected according to PRB positions.

Noise Power per PRB estimation algorithm is specified in section 2.8.3.4 of the 5GMax algorithm specification.

Noise Power per PRB measurement for PUCCH format2 is supported for following L1 variants:

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | Technology | FR1-TDD (CPRI/ eCPRI-7.2a/) | FR2-TDD (CPRI/ eCPRI-7.2a) | FR1-FDD (CPRI) | First Feature |
| L1 HW | Loner | not supported | not supported | not supported | - |
| Loki | supported | supported for eCPRI-7.2a | - | CB008021 |  |
| Thor | - | supported for eCPRI-7.2a | - | CB009027 |  |
| Odin |  |  |  |  |  |

Note:

1. When only zero-valued samples are got from the radio module or (e)CPRI interface for all the receiving antennas (spatial streams) (e.g. broken antenna scenario or protection switching in TSN), in case of noisy measurement, or for non-scheduled PRBs, 5G-L1-UL shall report INVALID value.
2. For invalid values for Noise Power per PRB measurements please find details in: [12714973](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_lIqIEGjtEfC_xcanjXaboQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

---

11457474: Simplified algorithm for noise power estimation 11457474: Simplified algorithm for noise power estimation 11457474: Simplified algorithm for noise power estimation 11457474: Simplified algorithm for noise power estimation 11457474: Simplified algorithm for noise power estimation Simplification of the noise power estimation algorithm for PUCCH Format 2 is introduced by substituting weighting Matrix S with alternative matrix M. Matrix M is derived from LDL decomposition of S, i.e., [image-0][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in dark text on a white background. The equation is: S = V · E · VH = (VE1/2) · (VE1/2)H = MMH The equation appears to be related to matrix operations, where 'V' and 'E' are likely matrices, and 'H' denotes the conjugate transpose (Hermitian transpose). 'S' and 'M' are also likely matrices. The term E1/2 suggests a matrix square root.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_pukkola_5G_L1_Entity_Level_file_6539.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] Matrix M is precomputed and stored in memory. No performance loss expected and, due to M having reduced column dimension, less DSP operations are required. The simplified noise power estimate (per chunk block i, antenna port p and spatial stream ant)  is: [image-1][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is: $\hat{\sigma} {noise,i,p,ant}^2 = (\hat{H} {p,sep}^{pilot})^H MM^H \hat{H} {p,sep}^{pilot} = (M^H \hat{H} {p,sep}^{pilot})^H (M^H \hat{H} {p,sep}^{pilot}) = \sum {k=1}^{R} |[M^H \hat{H} {p,sep}] {k}|^2$[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_pukkola_5G_L1_Entity_Level_file_6539.002.png[/image_path][/image-1] Full description of the simplification and notation in section "2.4.3.1.3" of 5Gmax algorithm specification (5G_L1_7703_replaced( 11396538 )). (ID: 11457474)

###### 5.3.5.3.5.2.2.5 Frozen Requirement

**5.3.5.3.5.2.2.5.0-1**  (ID: `11457425`)

Frozen Requirement
**[CNI-108168]**

For common frozen requirements (for different formats) for Noise Power measurement please find  chapter 5G\_L1\_17243\_replaced([11458250](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAvTSfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) in chapter "PUCCH processing**\ Format 3"**

**[END CNI-108168]**

---

###### 5.3.5.3.5.2.3 Signal power

###### 5.3.5.3.5.2.3.1 General

###### 5.3.5.3.5.2.3.1.0-1 General For PUCCH format2 5G-L1-UL shall estimate Signal Power symbol per Rx antenna (spatial stream) base on raw channel estimation. Signal Power estimation is specified in section 2.4.3.1.4 of the 5GMax algorithm specification. (ID: 13258135)

###### 5.3.5.3.5.2.3.2 Received power

###### 5.3.5.3.5.2.3.2-1 Received power

**5.3.5.3.5.2.3.2.0-1**  (ID: `13258143`)

Received power
For PUCCH format2 for each scheduled resource 5G-L1-UL shall estimate one measurement for the UL received power and report it to 5G-L2-PS.

5G-L1-UL shall perform received power measurement on DMRS associated with PUCCH.

Each UL received power measurement shall be averaged over all the allocated REs for DMRSs and aggregated over all the receiving antennas. Then, one measurement normalized to one PRB shall be reported to L2 .

The scaling factor applied at the radio module to reach a target noise bitwidth shall be compensated at 5G-L1-UL for all the UL power measurements using the IE  UlCell\_SetupReq->rxScalingFactor  (for details see: [11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ), [11418478](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-ZJ5_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).

5G-L1-UL shall report estimation via L1-L2 IF parameter: UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->rxPower .

The rxPower parameter is defined in dBm unit as illustrated in [11514200](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BRfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

The UL received power estimation algorithm on PUCCH is described in section 2.8.4.2 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification: [11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) .

Note:

1. rxScalingFactor value is set as described in [11288559](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tp7ttPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)
2. When only zero-valued samples are received from the radio module or (e)CPRI interface for all the receiving antennas (eg. broken antenna scenario), 5G-L1-UL shall set the rxPower parameter sent in UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs message to invalid value  (-140dBm).
3. For invalid values for Received Power measurements please find: [12717252](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_AV0d4GmnEfC_xcanjXaboQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)
4. The measurement for the UL received power can be used as a level indicator for the UL power control.

---

[END CNI-108168]

---

##### 5.3.5.3.5.4 DTX Metric

**5.3.5.3.5.4.0-1**  (ID: `13258151`)

DTX Metric
For PUCCH format2 5G-L1-UL shall estimate metrics which are used to indicate whether a PUCCH signal was transmitted and received as expected.

DTX metrics depends on the number of UCI bits. When the number of UCI bits exceed 19, CRC is considered for DTX detection.

Depending on code type (Reed-Muller or Polar) two metrics are estimated.

The DTX detection and DTX metrics for PUCCH format2 are described in section  2.4.3.10  of the 5Gmax algorithm specification.

For more information about decoding please find sections 2.4.3.8 and 2.4.3.9 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification.

For DTX detection for PUCCH format2 details see: ( [11457648: DTX Detection](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAsP_fvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

---

##### 5.3.5.3.5.5 Power Adjustment and Scaling

**5.3.5.3.5.5.0-1**  (ID: `11457554`)

Power Adjustment and Scaling
[CNI-108168]

Requirements defining power scaling are stored in chapter 6 (see 5G\_L1\_4204\_replaced([11421346](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-hFsvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for Loki and 5G\_L1\_8907\_replaced([11422159](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-hswfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for Thor)

[END CNI-108168]

---

##### 5.3.5.3.5.6 Post Processing

###### 5.3.5.3.5.6.1 Channel Smoothing

###### 5.3.5.3.5.6.1.0-1 Channel Smoothing For PUCCH format2 5G-L1-UL shall apply MMSE smoothing to raw channel estimation in frequency-domain of each DMRS symbol. For more details, please find sections  2.4.3.1.2, 2.4.3.1.3 and 2.4.3.4.4 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification. (ID: 13282200)

##### 5.3.5.3.5.7 Frequency Domain Interpolation

###### 5.3.5.3.5.7.0-1 Frequency Domain Interpolation For PUCCH format2 5G-L1-UL shall perform linear interpolation to extend channel estimates of DMRS position to data position per OFDM symbol. For more details, please find section  2.4.3.1.5 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification. (ID: 13335860)

#### 5.3.5.3.6 Detection

##### 5.3.5.3.6.1 Rdd processing

**5.3.5.3.6.1.0-1**  (ID: `13333425`)

Rdd processing
For PUCCH format2 for MMSE MRC receiver 5G-L1-UL shall calculate inverted Rdd matrix.

For MMSE-MRC equalizer, it’s assumed that there is no Rx stream correlated interference. Thus, Rdd matrix is a diagonal matrix with estimated noise power as diagonal elements.

Supported receiver modes are specified in: ([12576674: F2 Receiver modes](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ammEgTA3EfCRMdP0Nuo3Hg?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).

For more details, please find sections  2.4.3.5 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification.

---

##### 5.3.5.3.6.2 Equalization

**5.3.5.3.6.2.0-1**  (ID: `13282304`)

Equalization
5G-L1-UL shall support MMSE MRC equalization algorithm for PUCCH format2.

Supported receiver modes are specified in:    [12576674: Receiver modes](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ammEgTA3EfCRMdP0Nuo3Hg?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

For more details, please find section 2.4.3.5  of the 5Gmax algorithm specification.

---

##### 5.3.5.3.6.3 Demodulation Scaler

###### 5.3.5.3.6.3.0-1 Demodulation Scaler For PUCCH format2 5G-L1-UL shall calculate the Equalizer Scaler for demodulation. For more details, please find section 2.4.3.6 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification. (ID: 13337262)

##### 5.3.5.3.6.4 Demodulation

**5.3.5.3.6.4.0-1**  (ID: `13282309`)

Demodulation
For PUCCH format2 5G-L1-UL shall execute soft demodulation to calculate the LLR of each coded bit.

The parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->modulationType is used for demodulation.

For PUCCH format2 only QPSK demodulation is used.

For more details, please find section  2.4.3.6 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification and 3GPP TS 38.211 (v17.3.0): chapters 6.3.2.5.2

---

##### 5.3.5.3.6.5 Descrambling

**5.3.5.3.6.5.0-1**  (ID: `13282311`)

Descrambling
For PUCCH format2 5G-L1-UL shall execute de-scrambling of bit sequence to recover the original coded bits.

There are 2 parameters  used for de-scrambling: UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->rnti and UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->dataScramblingInt.

For more details, please find section 2.4.3.7 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification and 3GPP TS 38.211 (v17.3.0): chapters 6.3.2.5.1

Also please find: ([11456360: Group and sequence hopping](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAmJU_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

---

#### 5.3.5.3.7 Decoding

##### 5.3.5.3.7.1 Overview

**5.3.5.3.7.1.0-1**  (ID: `13282411`)

Overview
For PUCCH format2 for each scheduled resource 5G-L1-UL shall decode UCI bits.

Upon reception of message UlData\_PucchReceiveReq ( [11513979: PUCCH Receive Request message](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MHvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)), when the parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->numOfBitsOfUciInformation > 0, 5G-L1-UL shall decode UCI bits in the indicated NR-slot and sent to 5G-L2-PS through UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs message.

The appropriate channel decoding method for each PUCCH signal shall depend on the field numOfBitsOfUciInformation as described in 38.212 §6.3.1.3, with numOfBitsOfUciInformation standing for the "Number of bits".

The UCI bits decoding for PUCCH format2 is described in section  2.4.3.8 and 2.4.3.9  of the 5Gmax algorithm specification.

---

##### 5.3.5.3.7.2 Reed-Muller Decoding

**5.3.5.3.7.2.0-1**  (ID: `13282417`)

Reed-Muller Decoding
For PUCCH format2 if there are less than 12 bits of uplink control information to be transferred (parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->numOfBitsOfUciInformation < 12) 5G-L1-UL shall use Reed-Muller code (channel coding for small blocks lengths) for decode.

The de-rate matching is applied before decoding.

No Cyclic Redundancy Check (CRC) bits are transmitted with data bits.

For more details, please find 3GPP TS 38.212 (v17.3.0): chapters 6.3.1.3, 6.3.1.4, 5.3, 5.4 and section  2.4.3.8  of the 5Gmax algorithm specification.

---

##### 5.3.5.3.7.3 Polar Decoding

**5.3.5.3.7.3.0-1**  (ID: `13282419`)

Polar Decoding
For PUCCH format2 if there are more than 11 bits of uplink control information to be transferred (parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->numOfBitsOfUciInformation > 11) 5G-L1-UL shall use Polar code for decoding.

Before decoding the de-rate matching is applied.

If there are between 12 and 19 bits of uplink control information, then 6 Cyclic Redundancy Check (CRC) bits are extracted.

If there are more than 19 bits of uplink control information, then 11 Cyclic Redundancy Check (CRC) bits are extracted.

For more details, please find 3GPP TS 38.212 (v17.3.0): chapters 6.3.1.3, 6.3.1.4, 5.3, 5.4 and section  2.4.3.3  of the 5Gmax algorithm specification.

---

##### 5.3.5.3.7.4 Cyclic Redundancy Check

**5.3.5.3.7.4.0-1**  (ID: `13282448`)

Cyclic Redundancy Check
For PUCCH format2 for each control data received on PUCCH, when the parameter  UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->numOfBitsOfUciInformation ≥ 12 bits, 5G-L1-UL shall performed error detection using Cyclic Redundancy Check ([CRC](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_LDSGd3IIEfCRE7eh4Ndkrw)) bits.

The CRC sequence is transmitted with UCI payload and its bitwidth is 6 bits for UCI payload in range [12..19] bits and it is 11 bits for UCI payload >19 bits.

For each control data received on PUCCH,

* when UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->numOfBitsOfUciInformation ≥ 12 bits, 5G-L1-UL shall report CRC to 5G-L2-PS within parameters: UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->crc  and UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->crc
* when UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->numOfBitsOfUciInformation ≤11 bits, the default value 0(OK) is filled in the parameters UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->crc  and UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->crc but it would be ignored by L2-PS.

Note:

1. For reference for L1L2 PUCCH messages see: ([11453583](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAZVA_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))
2. CRC bits and UCI payload bits are together coded with Polar code.

---

##### 5.3.5.3.7.5 Decoding results

**5.3.5.3.7.5.0-1**  (ID: `13282445`)

Decoding results
For PUCCH format2 5G-L1-UL shall report decoded UCI bits.

All necessary information to decode each signal received on PUCCH format2 (i.e., scheduled resource, number of UCI bits, etc.) are got from the UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message ([11513990](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MIfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For each decoded data on PUCCH (whatever the DTX decision: 'DTX' or 'nonDTX'), 5G-L1-UL shall provide to 5G-L2-PS the respective information in different messages described in ([11513958](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MGfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) as follows:

* The decoded UCI bits: the numOfBitsOfUciInformation UCI bits shall be reported in the field uciBits of the UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs message.
* The decoded HARQ-ACK bits: 5G-L1-UL shall report the first nANPucch decoded bits (among all the decoded UCI bits) in the UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD message, with nANPucch standing for the number of HARQ-ACK bits which is got from message UlData\_PucchReceiveReq. Note that the first HARQ-ACK bit corresponds to the MSB of the decoded sequence of bits.
* The decoded SR bit: SR bit is multiplexed with the CSI report bits and/or HARQ-ACK bits. 5G-L1-UL decodes the numOfBitsOfUciInformation number of UCI bits and passes them transparently as bit string to L2-PS in UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs . Whether SR is transmitted via  PUCCH format3 or not is transparent to 5G-L1-UL.

---

#### 5.3.5.3.8 DTX Detection

##### 5.3.5.3.8.1 General

**5.3.5.3.8.1.0-1**  (ID: `13282444`)

General
For PUCCH format2 5G-L1-UL shall use DTX metric to indicate whether a PUCCH signal was transmitted and received as expected.

The ACK missed detection probability is set to 0.5% in threshold derivation of PUCCH DTX detection by adding some margin to ensure meeting 3GPP minimum requirement in TS 38.104.

The DTX detection methods, metrics and thresholds for PUCCH format2 are described in section  2.4.3.10  of the 5Gmax algorithm specification.

The two terms used for PUCCH DTX decision (i.e. the metric and the threshold in the fixed-point representation) as well as the decision (i.e. DTX or nonDTX) should then be provided to 5G-L2-PS via parameters:

* UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->dtxMetric  
  and (when value of parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources-> nANPucch > 0) via:  
  UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->dtxMetric
* UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->dtxThreshold  
  and (when value of parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources-> nANPucch > 0) via:  
  UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->dtxThreshold

The results of DTX detection are sent to 5G-L2-PS via parameters:

* UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->dtx  
  and (when value of parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources-> nANPucch > 0) via:  
  UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->dtx
* UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->crc  
  and (when value of parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources-> nANPucch > 0) via:  
  UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->crc

Note:

1. 5G-L2-PS could use the DTX indication to filter reliable measurements performed on PUCCH (e.g. TO), to handle DL retransmission, etc.
2. The false alarm is defined as the probability to detect UCI reporting whereas nothing was sent on PUCCH

---

##### 5.3.5.3.8.2 DTX Detection algorithm

**5.3.5.3.8.2.0-1**  (ID: `13339959`)

DTX Detection algorithm
For PUCCH format2, 5G-L1-UL shall evaluate the final DTX decision based on:

* CRC
* metric and thresholds for Polar coding related to time domain SNR (IFFT based)
* metric and thresholds for Reed Muller coding  (RM based)

The DTX detection follows below procedures:

If 3 bits <= numOfBitsOfciInformation <=11 bits

metric and thresholds for Reed Muller coding are compared

Else if 12 bits <= numOfBitsOfciInformation =< 19 bits

metric and thresholds for Polar coding are compared

Else if 20 bits <= numOfBitsOfciInformation

If CRC is OK

DTX = 0

Else if CRC is NOK

metric and thresholds for Polar coding are compared

Note:

1. numOfBitsOfciInformation is given in UlData\_PucchReceiveReq. See 5G\_L1\_IF\_219\_replaced([11514147](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR1aPvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
2. Refer to 5GMax algorithm specification chapter 2.4.3.10 for details.

---

##### 5.3.5.3.8.3 Threshold for DTX decision

###### 5.3.5.3.8.3.1 Loki / Thor

**5.3.5.3.8.3.1.0-1**  (ID: `13310631`)

Loki / Thor
For PUCCH format2 5G-L1-UL shall use threshold for DTX decision.

This selection shall be performed for each NR-slot where resources are scheduled for PUCCH transmission.

1. For number of UCI bits from range [3, 11], based on the number of UCI bits, number of PRBs and number of symbols 5G-L1-UL shall select the appropriate threshold for Reed Muller coding (RM based) for DTX decision.

Thresholds for Reed Muller coding in 5GMAX algorithm document are specified for 2Rx spatial stream configuration.  
For 4Rx stream configuration 5G-L1-UL shall multiply threshold of 2Rx by 1.15 .   
For 1Rx stream configuration 5G-L1-UL shall multiply threshold of 2Rx by 0.85 .

2. For number of UCI bits bigger than 11 bits, based on number of PRBs and number of symbols 5G-L1-UL shall select the appropriate threshold for Polar coding (IFFT based) for DTX decision.

Thresholds for Polar coding in 5GMAX algorithm document are specified for 2Rx spatial stream configuration.  
For 4Rx stream configuration 5G-L1-UL shall multiply threshold of 2Rx by 1.7071 .   
For 1Rx stream configuration 5G-L1-UL shall multiply threshold of 2Rx by 0.6036 .

The corresponding values of threshold are defined internally in L1 software code in form of tables.

5G-L1-UL shall get needed information from parameters:

UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->numOfBitsOfUciInformation

UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->numOfSymbols

UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->numOfPrb

UlCell\_SetupReq->ulSubcellType

The thresholds and formulas for DTX decision are specified in  5GMAX algorithm spec chapter 2.4.3.10.

For DTX metric evaluation please find: ([13258150: DTX Metric](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ZUh8hMoCEfCYBIz6acpPHw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

Note:

1. The DTX indication shall be provided to 5G-L2-PS as described in ([12721868](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_mXk1EW2JEfCmnYHxzZN44w?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).

---

###### 5.3.5.3.8.3.2 Loner

**5.3.5.3.8.3.2.0-1**  (ID: `13339973`)

Loner
For PUCCH format2 5G-L1-UL shall use threshold for DTX decision.

This selection shall be performed for each NR-slot where resources are scheduled for PUCCH transmission.

1. For number of UCI bits from range [3, 11], based on the number of UCI bits, number of PRBs and number of symbols 5G-L1-UL shall select the appropriate threshold for Reed Muller coding (RM based) for DTX decision.

Thresholds for Reed Muller coding in 5GMAX algorithm document are specified for 2Rx spatial stream configuration.  
For 4Rx stream configuration 5G-L1-UL shall multiply threshold of 2Rx by 1.15 .   
For 1Rx stream configuration 5G-L1-UL shall multiply threshold of 2Rx by 0.85 .

2. For number of UCI bits bigger than 11 bits, based on number of PRBs and number of symbols 5G-L1-UL shall select the appropriate threshold for Polar coding (IFFT based) for DTX decision.

Thresholds for Polar coding in 5GMAX algorithm document are specified for 2Rx spatial stream configuration.  
For 4Rx stream configuration 5G-L1-UL shall multiply threshold of 2Rx by 1.7071 .   
For 1Rx stream configuration 5G-L1-UL shall multiply threshold of 2Rx by 0.6036 .

The corresponding values of threshold are delivered from RAD parameters. For details please see: ([11453048: RAD parameters for Loner](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAW4wfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).

5G-L1-UL shall get needed information from parameters:

UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->numOfBitsOfUciInformation

UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->numOfSymbols

UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->numOfPrb

UlCell\_SetupReq->ulSubcellType

The thresholds and formulas for DTX decision are specified in  5GMAX algorithm spec chapter 2.4.3.10.

For DTX metric evaluation please find: ([13258150: DTX Metric](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ZUh8hMoCEfCYBIz6acpPHw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

Note:

1. The DTX indication shall be provided to 5G-L2-PS as described in ([12721868](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_mXk1EW2JEfCmnYHxzZN44w?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).

---

###### 5.3.5.3.8.4 Thresholds modification (Loner / Loki / Thor)

**5.3.5.3.8.4.0-2**  (ID: `13339982`)

Thresholds modification (Loner / Loki / Thor)
For PUCCH format2 5G-L1-UL shall use RAD parameters (Pucch F2 Dtx Threshold Adjust Factors) to modify DTX thresholds.

These parameters are used to control the amplitude of DTX thresholds per coding scheme (either Reed-Muller code or Polar code).

The default value equals to 1 for number of PRBs (numOfPrb) equal to 1,  otherwise equals to 1.3 for number PRBs (numOfPrb) greater than 1.

The range is [1,5], the step equals 0.005.

The following table illustrates these parameters:

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Parameter Name |  | Case |  |  |
| pucchF2DtxThrFactorMultiPrbPolar |  | Polar code, numOfPrb > 1 |  |  |
| pucchF2DtxThrFactorMultiPrbRM |  | Reed-Muller code, numOfPrb > 1 |  |  |
| pucchF2DtxThrFactorOnePrbPolar |  | Polar code, numOfPrb = 1 |  |  |
| pucchF2DtxThrFactorOnePrbRM |  | Reed-Muller code, numOfPrb = 1 |  |  |

For details please see: ([11452715: RAD parameters](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAVDl_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).

Note:

1. Used coding depends on number of UCI bits (numOfBitsOfciInformation)

2. numOfPrb and numOfBitsOfciInformation are given in UlData\_PucchReceiveReq. See 5G\_L1\_IF\_219\_replaced([11514147](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR1aPvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CNI-108168-I] The requirement was refined under CNI-108168  [End CNI-108168-I]

---

#### 5.3.5.3.9 Receive Response and HARQ report preparation

##### 5.3.5.3.9.1 UCI and measurements report

**5.3.5.3.9.1.0-1**  (ID: `13258171`)

UCI and measurements report
For PUCCH format2 for each scheduled resource after decoding control data received on PUCCH and estimating measurements 5G-L1-UL shall returns the UCI bits and a set of measurement metrics to the L2-PS via the message UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs.

Following L1L2 [IF](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_eam28HJJEfCRE7eh4Ndkrw) parameters 5G-L1-UL shall use to report UCI bits, measurements, DTX state, DTX metrics, DTX thresholds and CRC state:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs |  |
| Report / Measurement | L1L2 IF Parameter |
| UCI bits | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->uciBits |
| SR bit | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->srBit |
| DTX state | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->dtx |
| DTX metric | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->dtxMetric |
| DTX threshold | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->dtxThreshold |
| CRC state | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->crc |
| Noise Power per PRB(4) | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->noisePerPrb |
| ST TA metric | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->shortTermTaMetric |
| ST TA peak amplitude | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->shortTermTaPeakAmp |
| Noise Power | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->noisePower |
| Received Power | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->rxPower |
| RSSI | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->rssi |
| SINR | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->sinr |
| ST FO metric(5) | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->shortTermCfoMetric |
| antenna-wise  ST FO(5) | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->extendedParameters->shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt |

Note:

1. For detailed L1L2 IF specification please find: ([11513962](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MGvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) and ([11514171](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR1aQ_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))
2. The endpoint address for UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs is defined via parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->addrPucchReceiveRespPs
3. In specific configuration parameters in above table 5G-L1-UL shall set to "invalid values". For details see: ([11454049](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAbxQPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) and ([11514171](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR1aQ_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))
4. For Loner this parameter are not estimated. For details see ([11514171](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR1aQ_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

5.For PUCCH format2 these parameters are not estimated.

---

##### 5.3.5.3.9.2 HARQ report

###### 5.3.5.3.9.2.1 Loki / Thor

**5.3.5.3.9.2.1.0-1**  (ID: `13258174`)

Loki / Thor
For PUCCH format2 when parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->nANPucch is not equal "0", 5G-L1-UL shall send HARQ feedback and set of DTX data (DTX state, CRC state, DTX metric and its threshold) to the 5G-L2-PS via the message UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD.

Following L1L2 [IF](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_eam28HJJEfCRE7eh4Ndkrw) parameters 5G-L1-UL shall use to report HARQ feedback, CRC state, DTX state, DTX metric and its threshold:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD |  |
| Report / Measurement | L1L2 IF Parameter |
| AN bits | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->ackNack |
| DTX decision | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->dtx |
| DTX metric | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->dtxMetric |
| DTX threshold | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->dtxThreshold |
| SR bit(4) | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->srBit |
| CRC state | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->crc |

Note:

1. For detailed L1L2 IF specification please find: ([11513962](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MGvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) and ([11514243](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BT_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))
2. The endpoint address for UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs is defined via parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->addrPucchReceiveRespHarqD
3. In specific configuration parameters in above table 5G-L1-UL shall be set to "invalid values". For details see: ([11454049](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAbxQPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) and ([11514243](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BT_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

[PR864105, CB013151-A]

1. For specification of setting of parameter srBit see: ([11453947: Parameter srBit](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAbKM_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

Added parameter srBit to message UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqDL1sw.

[End PR864105, CB013151-A]

[CNI-108168-I] The requirement was refined under CNI-108168  [End CNI-108168-I]

###### 5.3.5.3.9.2.2 Loner

Loner

##### 5.3.5.4.1.2 Receiver modes

###### 5.3.5.4.1.2.1 FR1-TDD

###### 5.3.5.4.1.2.1.1 FR1-TDD CPRI

**5.3.5.4.1.2.1.1.0-1**  (ID: `13241425`)

FR1-TDD CPRI
For FR1-TDD CPRI, for PUCCH format3, 5G-L1-UL shall use receivers with 2 and 4 antenna streams as below table.

Use of 2Rx or 4Rx is configurable per cell during cell setup phase (with parameter UlCell\_SetupReq->ulSubcellType).

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | mode | 2Rx MMSE MRC\* | 4Rx MMSE MRC | First Feature |
|  | ulSubcellType | C2 | C4 |  |
| L1 HW | Loner | supported | supported | CB006064 |
| Loki | supported | supported | CB007950 |  |
| Thor | supported | supported | CB007487 |  |
| Odin |  |  |  |  |

Notes:

References for signal processing path diagram for PUCCH format3 MMSE receiver: [12576693](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_plYS0DBJEfCRMdP0Nuo3Hg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

Abbreviations:

\*MMSE: Minimum Mean Square Error,  MRC: Maximum Ratio Combining

###### 5.3.5.4.1.2.1.2 FR1-TDD eCPRI 7.2a

**5.3.5.4.1.2.1.2.0-2**  (ID: `12723045`)

FR1-TDD eCPRI 7.2a

| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | mode | 2Rx MMSE MRC\* | 4Rx MMSE MRC | 4Rx MMSE MRC | 8Rx MMSE IRC\*\* | First Feature |
|  | ulSubcellType | C2 | C4 | C8 | C8 |  |
| L1 HW | Loner | supported | supported | - | - | CB006064 |
| Loki | supported | supported | - | - | CB007950 |  |
| Thor | supported | supported | supported\*\* | supported \*\* | CB007487 |  |
| Odin | [CB012115-IA] Supported [End CB012115-IA] | [CB012115-IA] Supported [End CB012115-IA] |  |  | CB012115 |  |

Notes:

\*\*For C8 for Thor receiver mode could be 4Rx or 8Rx and it is indicated by UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->numCeAxCIndex

###### 5.3.5.4.1.2.2 FR1-FDD

###### 5.3.5.4.1.2.2.1 FR1-FDD CPRI / OBSAI

**5.3.5.4.1.2.2.1.0-2**  (ID: `13391525`)

FR1-FDD CPRI / OBSAI
For FR1-FDD CPRI, for PUCCH format3, 5G-L1-UL shall use receivers with 2 and 4 antenna streams as below table.

Use of 2Rx or 4Rx is configurable per cell during cell setup phase (with parameter UlCell\_SetupReq->ulSubcellType).

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | mode | 2Rx MMSE MRC\* | 4Rx MMSE MRC | First Feature |
|  | ulSubcellType | A2 | A4 |  |
| L1 HW | Loner (CPRI) | supported | supported | legacy |
| Loki (CPRI / OBSAI) | supported | supported | legacy |  |
| Thor (CPRI / OBSAI) | supported | supported | CB007487-D |  |
| Odin (CPRI) | [CB012115-JA] Supported [End CB012115-JA] | [CB012115-JA] Supported [End CB012115-JA] | CB012115 |  |

References for signal processing path diagram for PUCCH format3 MMSE receiver: [12576693](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_plYS0DBJEfCRMdP0Nuo3Hg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

For Loki and Thor L1 HWs in configuration of FDD supercell, for non-serving subcell (UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->isServingSubcell = False) 5G-L1-UL shall perform PUCCH Format3 measurement only (please refer to [11454763](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAfboPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

References for signal processing path diagram for PUCCH format3 MMSE receiver for non-serving subcell: [12649426](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_QKWpo0U0EfCam_3F6qrTdA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

Note:

\*MMSE: Minimum Mean Square Error,  MRC: Maximum Ratio Combining

For supported types of subcell please refer: [11381236](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uero9fvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

---

###### 5.3.5.4.1.2.2.2 FR1-FDD eCPRI 7.2a

**5.3.5.4.1.2.2.2.0-2**  (ID: `13391529`)

FR1-FDD eCPRI 7.2a
For FR1-FDD eCPRI 7.2a, for PUCCH format3, 5G-L1-UL shall use receivers with 2,4 [CB013442-D] and 8 [End CB013442-D] antenna streams as below table.

Use of 2Rx or 4Rx [CB013442-D] or 8Rx [End CB013442-D] is configurable per cell during cell setup phase (with parameter UlCell\_SetupReq->ulSubcellType).

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | mode | 2Rx MMSE MRC\* | 4Rx MMSE MRC | 8Rx MMSE IRC\* | First Feature |
|  | ulSubcellType | A2 | A4 | A8 |  |
| L1 HW | Loki | supported | supported |  |  |
| Thor | supported | supported | supported | CB007487-D |  |
| Odin | [CB012115-LA] Supported [End CB012115-LA] | [CB012115-LA] Supported [End CB012115-LA] |  | CB012115 |  |

References for signal processing path diagram for PUCCH format3 MMSE receiver: [12576693](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_plYS0DBJEfCRMdP0Nuo3Hg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

References for signal processing path diagram for PUCCH format3 MMSE receiver with IRC: [12576694](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_O3HD8DBKEfCRMdP0Nuo3Hg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

For Loki and Thor L1 HWs in configuration of FDD supercell, for non-serving subcell (UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->isServingSubcell = False) 5G-L1-UL shall perform PUCCH Format3 measurement only (please refer to [11454763](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAfboPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

References for signal processing path diagram for PUCCH format3 MMSE receiver for non-serving subcell: [12649426](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_QKWpo0U0EfCam_3F6qrTdA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

Note:

\*MMSE: Minimum Mean Square Error,  MRC: Maximum Ratio Combining

\*\*IRC: Interference Rejection Combining

For supported types of subcell please refer: [11381236](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uero9fvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

##### 5.3.5.4.1.3 Frozen Requirements

**5.3.5.4.1.3.0-1**  (ID: `11456418`)

Frozen Requirements
Content of this requirement is frozen and valid until 26R1 release, For later releases please refer to the objects below in chapters : [12576671](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_QfMWsDA3EfCRMdP0Nuo3Hg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9),  [12576664](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_0LHvADA0EfCRMdP0Nuo3Hg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) , [12576674:](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ammEgTA3EfCRMdP0Nuo3Hg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9), [12576674](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ammEgTA3EfCRMdP0Nuo3Hg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

Receivers with 4 and 2 **[CB009363-B]and 8** [End CB009363-B]antenna streams are supported.\*\*\*\*

For PUCCH format 0 and 2, 4 Rx MLSE *and MMSE*\* algorithm shall be supported, respectively.

**[CB009363-B]**

For PUCCH format 1, 8 Rx MLD ***with pre-Whitening***\* (interference rejection) shall be supported.

For PUCCH format 3, 8 Rx MMSE IRC**\***  shall be supported.

For L1 Thor HW, shrinkage solution shall be supported, refer to “5GMax-5G New Radio Algorithm Specification” section#2.3.6.2 for MMSE-IRC shrinkage algorithm specification.

**[End CB009363-B]**

Use of 2Rx or 4Rx **[CB009363-B]or 8Rx** [End CB009363-B]is configurable per cell during cell setup phase by using IE ulSubcellType.\*\*\*\*

\*MLSE Maximum Likelihood Cyclic Shift Based Detection

\*\*MMSE: Minimum Mean Square Error

\*\*\*MLD: Maximum Likelihood Detection

\*\*\*\*pre-whitening is as a method to remove the antenna correlation of interference/noise. It can improve the performance of BER/BLER, miss detection and false alarm for colour noise/interference cases. refer to '5GMax-5G New Radio Algorithm Specification' section 2.4.2.9 for algorithm implementation steps.(<https://nokia.sharepoint.com/sites/ATFL1Spec/Controlled%20Documents/Forms/AllItems.aspx?id=%2Fsites%2FATFL1Spec%2FControlled%20Documents%2FArchitecture%20Documents&viewid=3f46fe9f%2De8dc%2D4d3a%2D8bf3%2D40d24786af68>)

**\***IRC: Interference Rejection Combining

Refer to 5G\_L1\_IF\_152\_replaced([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for configured ulSubcellType.

Refer to 5G\_L1\_2797\_replaced([11481465](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fDeeOPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for mapping of ulSubcellType to number of Rx antennas.

Refer to 5G\_UP\_17919 for MLD.

Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_17920\_replaced([11105044](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koFcc_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for MMSE IRC.

**[CB010575-A] The requirement is also applicable for L1** Thor for FR1-TDD-CPRI, but only in case of 2Rx and 4Rx receiver **[End CB010575-A]**\*\*\*\*

**[CB007595-B] The requirement is also applicable for L1** Thor for FR1-TDD-7-2e-eCPRI **[End CB007595-B]**\*\*\*\*

**[CB010970-B] The requirement is also applicable for L1** Thor (BB) for FR1-FDD-OBSAI (in case of 2Rx or 4Rx receiver). ***\*[End CB010970-B]*****\***

---

#### 5.3.5.4.2 Demapping

**5.3.5.4.2.0-2**  (ID: `13373066`)

Demapping
For PUCCH format3 5G-L1-UL shall pack frequency domain IQ samples from PRBs allocated to PUCCH resource in the buffer. According to list of PUCCH resources, received in the receive request, FD IQ samples from symbols carrying PUCCH are written in buffer.

For more details, please find sections 2.1 and 2.4.4 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification.

Note:

Demapping is a part of common Front-End operations.

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

#### 5.3.5.4.3 Time offset compensation

##### 5.3.5.4.3.1 General

**5.3.5.4.3.1.0-2**  (ID: `12723092`)

General
For FR1-TDD and FR1-FDD for PUCCH format3 5G-L1-UL shall support Time Offset Compensation ([TOC](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_FykXkGXPEfCwWbD4x7Iu-g)).

TOC is performed before channel estimation as specified in section 2.4.4.4 of the 5GMax algorithm specification.

TOC is applied to all received PUCCH format3 DMRS and data symbols.

Note:

The estimated target time offset (TOe) is used in TOC.

The TOC is a part of common Front-End operations.

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

##### 5.3.5.4.3.2 Frozen Requirement

###### 5.3.5.4.3.2.1 Overview

**5.3.5.4.3.2.1.0-1**  (ID: `11457749`)

Overview
PUCCH short format 0:

* Timing offset compensation: timing offset introduces a rotation of the channel in the frequency domain.
* Target time offset is used in PUCCH TO compensation.
* The timing offset compensation algorithm on PUCCH short format 0 is described in section 2.4.1.3 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification (see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_916 5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[5GC000885-A] FDD FR1 L1 Loner: PUCCH long format 1:

* Target time offset is used in PUCCH TO compensation.
* The timing offset compensation algorithm on PUCCH long format 1 is described in section 2.4.2.2 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification (see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_916 5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). [End 5GC000885-A]

[CB006064-A] TDD  FR1 L1 Loner/Loki: PUCCH long format 1:

* Target time offset is used in PUCCH TO compensation.

- The timing offset compensation algorithm on PUCCH long format 1 is described in section 2.4.2.2 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification (see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_916 5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). [End CB006064-A]

[5GC000580-F] PUCCH short format 2:

* [Before 5GC002006-A][5GC000580-F] The timing offset compensation algorithm on PUCCH format 2 is described in section "2.4.3.9.2 TO Phase Rotation" of the 5Gmax algorithm specification.
* [5GC002006-A] [CB007403-C]  [CB007403-E]The timing offset compensation algorithm on PUCCH format 2 is described in section "2.4.3.7 Time Offset Compensation" of the 5Gmax algorithm specification. [End 5GC002006-A] [End CB007403-C] [End CB007403-E]

[5GC000885-A] FDD FR1 L1 Loner: PUCCH long format 3:

* The estimated target time offset (TOe) is obtained, as described in section 2.4.4.3 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification (see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_916 5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
* TOe is used for timing offset compensation algorithm on PUCCH long format 3, as described in section 2.4.4.4 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification (see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_916 5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). [End 5GC000885-A]

[CB006064-A] TDD  FR1 L1 Loner/Loki: PUCCH long format 3:

* The estimated target time offset (TOe) is obtained, as described in section 2.4.4.3 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification (see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_916 5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

- TOe is used for timing offset compensation algorithm on PUCCH long format 3, as described in section 2.4.4.4 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification (see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_916 5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). [End CB006064-A]

HW-Technology Map:

PUCCH short format (F0, F2):

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Technology / HW | Loner | Loki | Thor |
| FR1-FDD-CPRI | Supported | Not supported | Not supported |
| FR1-FDD-7-2a-eCPRI | NA | Not supported | NA |
| FR1-TDD-CPRI | Supported | Supported | Not supported |
| FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI | Supported | Supported | Not supported |
| FR2-TDD-CPRI | Supported | NA | NA |
| FR2-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI | Supported | Supported | NA |

PUCCH Long format (F1, F3):

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Technology / HW | Loner | Loki | Thor |
| FR1-FDD-CPRI | Supported | Supported | Supported |
| FR1-FDD-OBSAI |  |  | [CB010969-SR-CB] Supported [End CB010969-SR-CB] |
| FR1-FDD-7-2a-eCPRI | NA | Supported | NA |
| FR1-TDD-CPRI | Supported | Supported | [CB010575-A] Supported [End CB010575-A] |
| FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI | Supported | Supported | Supported |
| FR1-TDD-7-2e-eCPRI | NA | NA | [CB007595-B] Supported [End CB007595-B] |
| FR2-TDD-CPRI | Not supported | NA | NA |
| FR2-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI | Not supported | Not supported | NA |

[5GC001868-A] 5G-L1-UL shall also support timing offset compensation for PUCCH F0 and F2 as described above (same as 5GC002006-A) in Loki L1 HW [End 5GC001868-A]

[5GC002481-AA]For FDD and in Loki L1 HW,  5G-L1-UL shall also support timing offset compensation for PUCCH F1 and F3 as described above.[End 5GC002481-AA]

[RP003187-K] L1 Thor shall also support timing offset compensation for PUCCH F1 and F3 as described above in FDD-FR1-CPRI case [End RP003187-K]

[RP003187-D] L1 Thor shall also support timing offset compensation for PUCCH F1 and F3 as described above in TDD-FR1-eCPRI case [End RP003187-D]

[CB008205-B] 5G-L1-UL shall also support timing offset compensation for PUCCH F1 and F3 in ABIO for O-RAN compliant FR1 FDD eCPRI. [End CB008205-B]

[Before-CNI-122313-A]

[CB009443-C] This requirement for format 1 and 3 shall be supported in RINLINE1 HW for FR1-TDD-eCPRI.[End CB009443-C]

[CB009444-G] This requirement  for format 1 and 3 is applicable for RINLINE1 for FR1-FDD-eCPRI. [End CB009444-G]

[CNI-122313-A]

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

[End CNI-122313-A]

###### 5.3.5.4.3.2.2 TO phase rotation

###### 5.3.5.4.3.2.2.0-1 TO phase rotation Loner and Loki (ID: 11457769)

**5.3.5.4.3.2.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11457778`)

TO phase rotation
The Demapper shall now perform the Time offset compensation (TOC), also named TO phase rotation, prior to the Raw channel estimation in front end. TO phase rotation and de-rotation (TO phase de-rotation rotates back TO so that phase rotation caused by TO is the same for PUSCH/PUCCH DMRS and data symbols) in parameter estimation module is removed.

[CB007814-G] This requirement also applies to ABIO FR1-FDD-eCPRI. [End CB007814-G]

[Before-CNI-122313-A]

[CB009443-C] This requirement shall be supported in RINLINE1 HW for FR1-TDD-eCPRI.[End CB009443-C]

[CNI-122313-A]

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

[End CNI-122313-A]

---

###### 5.3.5.4.3.2.2.0-2 TO phase rotation For Thor (ID: 11457786)

**5.3.5.4.3.2.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11457794`)

TO phase rotation
The Demapper shall now perform the Time offset compensation (TOC), also named TO phase rotation, prior to the Raw channel estimation in front end. TO phase rotation and de-rotation (TO phase de-rotation rotates back TO so that phase rotation caused by TO is the same for PUSCH/PUCCH DMRS and data symbols) in parameter estimation module is removed.

[RP003187-D] L1 Thor FR1-TDD-eCPRI shall also perform TOC prior to the raw channel estimation. [End RP003187-D]

[RP003187-K] L1 Thor FR1-FDD-CPRI shall also perform TOC prior to the raw channel estimation. [End RP003187-K]

[CB010575-A] The requirement is also applicable for L1 Thor for FR1-TDD-CPRI [End CB010575-A]

[CB011178-A] L1 shall also support this requirement in Thor for FR1-FDD-7-2a-eCPRI [End CB011178-A]
