#### 5.3.5.4.4 Frequency Offset Compensation

##### 5.3.5.4.4.1 General

###### 5.3.5.4.4.1.0-1 General FR1 TDD (ID: 11457819)

**5.3.5.4.4.1.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `12704078`)

General
For FR1-TDD for PUCCH format3 5G-L1-UL shall support frequency offset compensation (FOC).

For each Rx antenna stream 5G-L1-UL shall perform compensation of the Frequency Offset (FO) for Intra-symbol and Inter-symbol DMRS and DATA symbols.

For FOC 5G-L1-UL shall use Long Term Carrier Frequency Offset metric which 5G-L1-UL received via parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->longTermCfoMetricOfBeam .

FOC is performed before channel estimation. The FOC algorithm is specified in section 2.4.4.1 and 2.3.3.6 of the 5GMax algorithm specification.

FOC is supported in following HWs:

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | Technology | FR1-TDD-CPRI | FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a | FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e | First Feature |
| L1 HW | Loner | not supported |  | - | Legacy |
| Loki | supported |  | - | CB007449 |  |
| Thor | supported |  |  | CB007487 |  |
| Odin |  | [CB012115-IA]  Supported [End CB012115-IA] | [CB012115-GA] Supported [End CB012115-GA] | CB012115 |  |

The mapping between LT FOC and spatial stream is defined in [11457915](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAuFIPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

For supported FOC filter length see: [11457890](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAteG_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

For supported FOC optimization method see: [12700653](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_RUAzcF1pEfCPFofqMEsORA?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

Note:

1. 5G-L1-UL use LT CFO for FOC only when parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->foeValid equals 1='true'.
2. The parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->foeValid usage and related with it case of use ST FOE metric for FOC is described in: [11457873](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAteGfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)
3. Before FOC 5G-L1-UL shall perform “LT CFO validation for value 0” for each Rx antenna stream, see [12580643](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_qjrkQDGgEfCRMdP0Nuo3Hg?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) for details. 5G-L1-UL shall assume frequency offset equals 0Hz (no compensation) if LT CFO == 0+j0 is received.

---

###### 5.3.5.4.4.1.0-2 General FR1 FDD (ID: 11457835)

**5.3.5.4.4.1.0-2.0-5**  (ID: `13391530`)

General
For FR1-FDD for PUCCH format3 5G-L1-UL shall support frequency offset compensation (FOC).

For each Rx antenna stream 5G-L1-UL shall perform compensation of the Frequency Offset (FO) for Intra-symbol and Inter-symbol DMRS and DATA symbols.

For FOC 5G-L1-UL shall use Long Term Carrier Frequency Offset metric which 5G-L1-UL received via parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->longTermCfoMetricOfBeam .

FOC is performed before channel estimation. The FOC algorithm is specified in section 2.4.4.1 and 2.3.3.6 of the 5GMax algorithm specification.

FOC is supported in following HWs:

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | Technology | FR1-FDD-OBSAI | FR1-FDD-CPRI | FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a | First Feature |
| L1 HW | Loner | - | supported(2) | - | CB009107 |
| Loki | supported |  |  | CB007449 |  |
| Thor | supported |  |  | CB007487 |  |
| Odin |  | [CB012115-JA] Supported [End CB012115-JA] | [CB012115-LA] Supported [End CB012115-LA] |  |  |

The mapping between LT FOC and spatial stream is defined in [11457915](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAuFIPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

For supported FOC filter length see: [11457890](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAteG_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

For supported FOC optimization method see: [12700653](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_RUAzcF1pEfCPFofqMEsORA?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

Note:

1.  For Loki, Thor 5G-L1-UL use LT CFO for FOC only when parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->foeValid equals 1='true'.

1. From E2E for Loner, FOC is supported when NRBTS.NRCELL.actSupercellSingleSSB = True

3. For Loner the parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->foeValid is meaningless.

1. The parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->foeValid usage and related with it case of use ST FOE metric for FOC is described in: [11457873](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAteGfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)
2. Before FOC 5G-L1-UL shall perform “LT CFO validation for value 0” for each Rx antenna stream, see [12580643](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_qjrkQDGgEfCRMdP0Nuo3Hg?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) for details. 5G-L1-UL shall assume frequency offset equals 0Hz (no compensation) if LT CFO == 0+j0 is received.

---

##### 5.3.5.4.4.2 Supported FOC Filter length for PUCCH Format3

**5.3.5.4.4.2.0-2**  (ID: `12723131`)

Supported FOC Filter length for PUCCH Format3
For FR1-TDD and FR1-FDD for PUCCH format3 for intra-symbol FOC 5G-L1-UL shall use FOC filter with length values as follow:

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | Technology | FR1-TDD (CPRI/ eCPRI-7.2a/ eCPRI-7.2e) | FR1-FDD (OBSAI/ CPRI/ eCPRI-7.2a) | First Feature |
| L1 HW | Loner | - | 5 | CB009107 |
| Loki | 5, 11(1) | 5, 11(1) | CB007449 |  |
| Thor | 5, 11(1) | 5, 11(1) | CB007487 |  |
| Odin | [CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]  5 for FR1-TDD eCPRI-7.2a / FR1-TDD eCPRI-7.2e  [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] | [CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]  5 for FR1-FDD CPRI / FR1-FDD eCPRI-7.2a  [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] | CB012115 |  |

Note:

(1) For High Speed subcell when parameter UlCell\_SetupReq->actHighSpeedCell equals 1="true" .

1. Filter length refers to the total number of samples that the filter uses to calculate the output. For an FIR (Finite Impulse Response) filter, which is used for FOC, filter length is equivalent to the number of Taps. Number of Taps refers to the number of filter coefficients used in the filter's calculation.

---

##### 5.3.5.4.4.3 Supported FOC Optimization Method for PUCCH Format3

**5.3.5.4.4.3.0-2**  (ID: `12723145`)

Supported FOC Optimization Method for PUCCH Format3
For FR1-TDD and FR1-FDD for PUCCH format3 for intra-symbol FOC 5G-L1-UL shall use optimization for FOC filter coefficients. The following modes of this optimization are used according to the value of internal parameter FdFocOpt:

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | Technology | FR1-TDD (CPRI/ eCPRI-7.2a/ eCPRI-7.2e) | FR1-FDD (OBSAI/ CPRI/ eCPRI-7.2a) | First Feature |
| L1 HW | Loner | - | OFF | CB009107 |
| Loki | OFF, ON(1) | OFF, ON(1) | CB007449 |  |
| Thor | REAL, ON(1) | REAL, ON(1) | CB007487 |  |
| Odin | [CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]  REAL for FR1-TDD eCPRI-7.2a / FR1-TDD eCPRI-7.2e  [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] | [CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]  REAL for FR1-FDD CPRI / FR1-FDD eCPRI-7.2a  [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] | CB012115 |  |

Note:

(1) For High Speed subcell when parameter UlCell\_SetupReq->actHighSpeedCell equals 1="true" .

1. Parameter FdFOcOpt is described in section 2.3.3.6 of the 5GMax algorithm specification.

---

##### 5.3.5.4.4.4 Frequency Offset Compensation based on Short Term FOE

**5.3.5.4.4.4.0-2**  (ID: `12521453`)

Frequency Offset Compensation based on Short Term FOE
For PUCCH F3, if foeValid (refer to 5G\_L1\_IF\_216\_replaced([11513990](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MIfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is set to false and additionalDmrs (refer to 5G\_L1\_IF\_217\_replaced([11514084](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0zMvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is enabled, the 5G-L1-UL shall ignore the long term CFO metrics (longTermCfoMetric and longTermCfoMetricOfBeam in 5G\_L1\_IF\_216\_replaced([11513990](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MIfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and perform inter-symbol frequency offset compensation for the DMRS and data symbols by using the short term FOEs derived from the F3.

The intra-symbol FOC is skipped. If if foeValid is set to false and additionalDmrs is disabled, 5G-L1-UL shall skip the FOC (both inter and intra symbol FOC).  If foeValid is set to true, 5G-L1-UL shall use the long term CFO metrics (longTermCfoMetric and longTermCfoMetricOfBeam in 5G\_L1\_IF\_216\_replaced([11513990](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MIfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for intra and inter symbol frequency offset compensation.

[CB014106-SR-A] This requirement shall be supported in Thor FR1-TDD-7-2e-eCPRI. [End CB014106-SR-A]

---

##### 5.3.5.4.4.5 Long Term CFO mapping to spatial streams

**5.3.5.4.4.5.0-4**  (ID: `12723156`)

Long Term CFO mapping to spatial streams
5G-L1-UL shall perform antenna-wise FOC using antenna-wise LT-FOE longTermCfoMetricOfBeam received in the UlData\_PucchReceiveReq for PUCCH fomat3 as described in section 2.4.2.1 of the 5GMax New Radio Algorithm Specification document. Where mapping between LT FOE and spatial stream is defined as follows:

A2 or C2:

-longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[0]: (ce)AxC [0]

-longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[1]: (ce)AxC [1]

A4 or C4:

-longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[0]: (ce)AxC [0]

-longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[1]: (ce)AxC [1]

-longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[2]: (ce)AxC [2]

-longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[3]: (ce)AxC [3]

C8 or C8'2 or C8'4 or C8'8 or A8 :

-longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[0]: ceAxC [0]

-longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[0]: ceAxC [1]

-longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[1]: ceAxC [2]

-longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[1]: ceAxC [3]

-longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[2]: ceAxC [4]

-longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[2]: ceAxC [5]

-longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[3]: ceAxC [6]

-longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[3]: ceAxC [7]

Note:

1. For C8, C8'2, C8'4, C8'8 and A8 each element of longTermCfoMetricOfBeam corresponds to two continuous ceAxC streams. 5G\_L1\_UL shall duplicate longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[i] for ceAxC [2i+1] where i = 0,1,2,3.

2. For C8, C8'2, C8'4, C8'8  if 4Rx receiver is configured, only the first two elements of longTermCfoMetricOfBeam are valid and they correspond to ceAxC[0-3]. 5G-L1-UL shall expect the last two elements as invalid value.

1. For C2, C4, A2, A4 Long term CFO metric is sent for each Rx stream. Each value corresponds to one Rx antenna stream.

4. For eCPRI case, the order eAxC spatial stream values of the LT-FOE (longTermCfoMetricOfBeam) in the array and their mapping to beam patternId shall follow the same mapping order of EcpriConfig struct in 5G\_L1\_IF\_15453\_replaced([11514119](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR1aN_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).

1. The parameter longTermCfoMetricOfAnt is changed to longTermCfoMetricOfBeam in MULTI and L1SW in 23R4, refer to 5G\_L1\_13041\_replaced([11396378](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8r5xPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

##### 5.3.5.4.4.6 Frozen Requirement

**5.3.5.4.4.6.0-1**  (ID: `11457825`)

Frozen Requirement
TDD: CFO Compensation

[Before 5GC002244-D] TDD FR1 L1 Loner/Loki: L1-UL shall use longTermCfoMetric (included in the 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_215) to perform frequency offset compensation (FOC) on PUCCH F1 and F3 as described in section 2.4.2.1 of the 5GMax New Radio Algorithm Specification document.

[5GC002244-D]

TDD FR1 L1 Loki: 5G-L1-UL shall use longTermCfoMetric (included in the 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_215) to perform frequency offset compensation (FOC) on PUCCH F1 and F3 as described in section 2.4.2.1 of the 5GMax New Radio Algorithm Specification document (no change).

[CB006064-A]

For TDD FR1 L1 Loner/Loki , 5G- L1-UL shall ignore longTermCfoMetric (included in the 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_215 5G\_L1\_IF\_216\_replaced([11513990](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MIfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to perform frequency offset compensation (FOC) on PUCCH F1 and F3 as described in section 2.4.2.1 of the 5GMax New Radio Algorithm Specification document.

[End CB006064-A]

[5GC002244-D]TDD FR1 L1 Loner/[5GC001294-B] L1 Loki [End 5GC001294-B]: 5G-L1-UL shall use ignore longTermCfoMetricOfAnt (included in the  5G\_L1\_5G21A\_215 5G\_L1\_IF\_216\_replaced([11513990](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MIfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and shall not to perform frequency offset compensation (FOC) on PUCCH F1 and F3 for each data received in the respective spatial. as described in section 2.4.XX of the 5GMax New Radio Algorithm Specification document. The mapping between the antenna-wise LT FOE and spatial streams is provided in 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_1183.

[End 5GC002244-D]

[RP003187-B] The requirement above is applicable for L1 Thor [End RP003187-B]

[CB007449-D]

For TDD FR1 on  Loki HW:

 Frequency offset compensation (FOC) is supported based on the Long term CFO metric computed at 5G-L2-PS for each Rx antenna stream for a given UE (see 5G\_L2\_947)

* For each Rx antenna stream, 5G-L1-UL shall carry out a CFO compensation in frequency domain (post-FFT) for both data and DMRS as specified in section 2.4.2.1 of the 5GMax algorithm specification (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_695\_replaced([11101310](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_knWcovvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Note:

 CFO compensation depends on the setting of the L2 R&D parameter rdLongPucchFocEnable(see 5G\_L2\_1493).

[End CB007449-D]

[CB007487-B] L1 Thor shall support Frequency offset compensation (FOC) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI case as described above with CB007449-D feature. [End CB007487-B]

[Before-CNI-122313-A]

[CB009443-C] This requirement shall be supported in RINLINE1 HW for FR1-TDD-eCPRI case as described above with CB007449-D feature.[End CB009443-C]

[CNI-122313-A]

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

[End CNI-122313-A]

[CB008325-5G-AA]

For TDD FR1 on Thor HW:

     L1 Thor shall support FOC filter length equal to 11 taps.

FOC optimization method is aligned with PUSCH is configured to 'Real' for DMRS symbols and 'On' for Data symbols for Thor HW

[End CB008325-5G-AA]

[CB008792-A/D]

When actHighSpeedCell is enabled, the FOC filter length is set to 11 taps for all UE in the cell , otherwise, all the UE set to 5 taps by default.

[End CB008792-A/D]

[CB008792-D]

For Loki L1 HWs:

* FOE based on PUCCH DMRS is supported when F3 additional DMRS is configured with intra-slot FH.
* Additionally, Itv =4  is used by L1 for adjusting the time interval for short term correlation calculation between different DMRS symbols.
* See also section 2.4.4.1 of the 5GMax algorithm specification (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_695\_replaced([11101310](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_knWcovvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

[End CB008792-D] (See 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1380\_replaced([11105355](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koJt6_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

[CB008827-5G-A] Parity from CB008792:

When actHighSpeedCell is enabled, the FOC filter length is set to 11 taps for all UE in the cell , otherwise, all the UE set to 5 taps by default.

For Thor L1 HWs:

* FOE based on PUCCH DMRS is supported when F3 additional DMRS is configured with intra-slot FH.
* Additionally, Itv =4  is used by L1 for adjusting the time interval for short term correlation calculation between different DMRS symbols.

See also section 2.4.4.1 of the 5GMax algorithm specification (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_695\_replaced([11101310](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_knWcovvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

[End CB008827-5G-A]

[CB007595-B] The requirement is also applicable for L1 Thor for FR1-TDD-7-2e-eCPRI [End CB007595-B]

##### 5.3.5.4.5 Data/DMRS extraction

**5.3.5.4.5.0-2**  (ID: `13373080`)

Data/DMRS extraction
For PUCCH format3 5G-L1-UL shall separate DMRS and DATA IQ samples for next processing.

For more details, please find 3GPP TS 38.211 (v17.3.0): chapter 6.3.2.6.5, 6.4.1.3.3.2 .

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

#### 5.3.5.4.6 Parameter estimation and measurement

##### 5.3.5.4.6.1 Raw channel estimation

###### 5.3.5.4.6.1.1 Raw Channel estimation for DMRS Sequence Type 1

**5.3.5.4.6.1.1.0-2**  (ID: `12723168`)

Raw Channel estimation for DMRS Sequence Type 1
For FR1-TDD and FR1-FDD for PUCCH format3 5G-L1-UL shall perform channel estimation.

There is removed from DMRS symbols ZC sequence by multiply received DMRS by conjugation of reference DMRS sequence (ZC sequence).

Channel estimation is specified in section 2.4.4.7 and 2.4.4.2 of the 5GMax algorithm specification.

Note:

For PUCCH format3 5G-L1-UL generates DMRS Type1 pilot sequence according to 3GPP 38.211 5.2.2 and 6.4.1.3.3

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

###### 5.3.5.4.6.1.2 Raw Channel estimation for DMRS Sequence Type 2

**5.3.5.4.6.1.2.0-1**  (ID: `12979127`)

Raw Channel estimation for DMRS Sequence Type 2
For FR1-TDD and FR1-FDD for PUCCH format3 5G-L1-UL shall perform channel estimation.

There is removed from DMRS symbols ZC sequence by multiply received DMRS by conjugation of reference DMRS sequence (ZC sequence).

Channel estimation is specified in section 2.4.4.7 and 2.4.4.2 of the 5GMax algorithm specification.

Note:

1.For PUCCH format3 5G-L1-UL generates DMRS Type2 pilot sequence according to 3GPP 38.211 5.2.3 and 6.4.1.3.3

1. For DMRS Type2 pilot 5G-L1-UL apply optimization for raw channel estimation (similar as for PUSCH) as described in 2.3.1.1 of the 5GMax algorithm specification.
2. For impact of using Low-PAPR DMRS Type2 (Release16) on channel estimation please find: [11361085](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucyymvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) , [11105217](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koH4tvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

##### 5.3.5.4.6.2 Time Offset Estimation

###### 5.3.5.4.6.2.1 General

**5.3.5.4.6.2.1.0-2**  (ID: `12723187`)

General
For FR1-TDD and FR1-FDD for PUCCH format3 5G-L1-UL shall perform Time Offset Estimation ([TOE](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_jHPVsGWGEfCtwYrh0KQ_DA)). TO is estimated per Rx spatial stream (antenna-wise).

TOE is specified in section 2.4.4.3 of the 5GMax algorithm specification.

Note:

TOE reliability depends on the number of PRBs.

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

###### 5.3.5.4.6.2.2 Time Offset Measurements

**5.3.5.4.6.2.2.0-2**  (ID: `12723174`)

Time Offset Measurements
For FR1-TDD and FR1-FDD for PUCCH format3 5G-L1-UL shall estimates Short Term ([ST](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_8sZYsGWLEfCtwYrh0KQ_DA)) Time Offset ([TO](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_A8Ba0GWMEfCtwYrh0KQ_DA)) on PUCCH and reports the TO estimate (TOE) to 5G-L2-PS for update the Timing Advance ([TA](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_FB5EAGWMEfCtwYrh0KQ_DA)) measurement.

5G-L1-UL shall report a following measurements via L1-L2 IF parameters:

* Short Term Timing Advance Metric: UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->shortTermTaMetric
* Short Term Timing Advance Peak Amplitude: UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->shortTermTaPeakAmp

TOE measurements are specified in section 2.8.6 of the 5GMax algorithm specification.

Supported measurements for TOE for following L1 variants:

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | Measurement | ST TA Metric | ST TA Peak Amplitude | First Feature |
| L1 HW | Loner | supported | supported | Legacy |
| Loki | supported | supported | Legacy |  |
| Thor | supported | supported | CB007487 |  |
| Odin | [CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] Supported for  FR1-TDD eCPRI-7.2a / FR1-TDD eCPRI-7.2e [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] [CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] FR1-FDD CPRI / FR1-FDD eCPRI-7.2a [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] | [CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] Supported for  FR1-TDD eCPRI-7.2a / FR1-TDD eCPRI-7.2e [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] [CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] FR1-FDD CPRI / FR1-FDD eCPRI-7.2a [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] | CB012115 |  |

Note:

1. 5G-L1-UL shall report both measurements (ST TA Metric and ST TA Peak Amplitude)  across all the RX antennas (shall be combined before report to 5G-L2-PS).
2. The unit of ST TA Metric reported to 5G-L2-PS is equal to Tsμ where Tsμ = (1/2μ) \* Ts, where

Ts is defined in:[11491325](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tRtPzPv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ) , and μ  is defined in: [11491448](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tRt23vv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)

1. ST TOE on PUCCH is performed only when a PUCCH format 3 is scheduled with 1 and 2 DMRS on all RBs. For Format3, it is assumed that all the supported configurations always fulfill the minimum requirement to provide a valid ST TOE.
2. The number of configured RX antenna is derived according to [12576677](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wsVMkDA3EfCRMdP0Nuo3Hg?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) .
3. For invalid values for ST TO measurements please find: [12709927](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_pqASwGXAEfCwWbD4x7Iu-g?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)
4. For PUCCH format3 this requirement is not applicable when parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq-> PucchResourceAllocationConfig-> isServingSubcell IE is set to false (configuration for non-serving subcell for FDD supercell), refer to ([11453916](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAajLvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

###### 5.3.5.4.6.2.3 Power Delay Profile

**5.3.5.4.6.2.3.0-2**  (ID: `13373081`)

Power Delay Profile
For FR1-TDD and FR1-FDD for PUCCH format3 5G-L1-UL shall estimate Power Delay Profile (PDP).

PDP estimation is performed per Rx stream and per DMRS symbol.

Estimated PDP is used for MMSE smoothing operation.

For more details, please find section 2.4.4.3  of the 5Gmax algorithm specification.

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

**5.3.5.4.6.2.4.1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11458052`)

General
[CNI-59405] CP2 moved

FDD FR1 L1 Loner: TO is estimated for PUCCH F3 as described in section 2.4.4.3 of 5GMax New Radio Algorithm Specification document. PUCCH F1 is not used for TO estimation because it has 1 PRB only.

[5GC002481-AA][CB007271-C] For FDD and in Loki L1 HW, the above algorithm shall also be supported. [End 5GC002481-AA][End CB007271-C]

[RP003187-K] L1 Thor shall also support this requirement for FDD-FR1-CPRI [End RP003187-K]

[CB010969-SR-CB] This requirement shall be supported by L1 Thor in FR1-FDD-OBSAI. [End CB010969-SR-CB]

[End CNI-59405]

###### 5.3.5.4.6.2.4.2 Short Term Time Offset Measurement

###### 5.3.5.4.6.2.4.2.0-1 Short Term Time Offset Measurement Loner, Loki (ID: 11458086)

**5.3.5.4.6.2.4.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11458096`)

Short Term Time Offset Measurement
In addition to the TO estimation performed on PUSCH, if:

- a PUCCH format 2 is scheduled over 3 RBs or more,

- FDD FR1 **Loner: for a PUCCH format 3 with 1 and 2 DMRS on all RBs.**

- **[CB006064-A] TDD FR1** ~~Loki~~**/Loner: for a PUCCH format 3 with 1 and 2 DMRS on all RBs.** [End CB006064-A]***\****\*

1- 5G-L1-UL estimates a short term (ST) timing offset (TO) on PUCCH and reports it to 5G-L2-PS within the *UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs message, which could use it to update the TA measurement.*

2- A single correlation peak should be reported to 5G-L2-PS in TO parameters *shortTermTaMetric and* shortTermTaPeakAmp sent in *UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs message.*\*\*

The search window length for time offset estimation is changed for PUCCH format 2 and the *shortTermTaMetric shall be adjusted with the new search window range (see ~~5G\_L1\_5G21A\_1166~~ 5G\_L1\_4468\_replaced([11457411](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fArB2_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).*

The timing offset estimation algorithm on:

- PUCCH format 2 is described in section 2.4.3.8

- FDD FR1 **Loner: : PUCCH format 3 is described in section 2.4.4.3**

- **[CB006064-A] TDD FR1** ~~Loki~~**/Loner: PUCCH format 3 is described in section 2.4.4.3.** [End CB006064-A]***\****\*

of the 5Gmax algorithm specifications (see ~~5G\_L1\_5G21A\_916~~ 5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

5G-L1-UL shall also perform TO estimation on PUCCH format2 and provide this estimate to 5G-L2-PS as explained above in **Loki L1 HW.**

---

###### 5.3.5.4.6.2.4.2.0-2 Short Term Time Offset Measurement Thor (ID: 12708629)

**5.3.5.4.6.2.4.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11458111`)

Short Term Time Offset Measurement
In addition to the TO estimation performed on PUSCH,  for TDD FR1 for PUCCH format 3 with 1 and 2 DMRS on all RBs.

1- 5G-L1-UL estimates a short term (ST) timing offset (TO) on PUCCH and reports it to 5G-L2-PS within the UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs message, which could use it to update the TA measurement.

2- A single correlation peak should be reported to 5G-L2-PS in TO parameters shortTermTaMetric and shortTermTaPeakAmp sent in UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs message.

The timing offset estimation algorithm on: TDD FR1 PUCCH format 3 is described in section 2.4.4.3. of the 5Gmax algorithm specifications (see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_916 5G\_L1\_7703).

**[RP003187-F] In terms of TDD FR1 PUCCH format 3 the requirement is also applicable for L1** Thor for FR1-TDD-eCPRI.\*\*\*\*

L1 Thor does not support short PUCCH formats. **[End RP003187-F]**

**[CB010575-D] The requirement is also applicable for L1** Thor for FR1-TDD-CPRI **[End CB010575-D]**\*\*\*\*

**[CB009514-F] The requirement is also applicable for Thor(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e** [End CB009514-F]\*\*\*\*

---

###### 5.3.5.4.6.2.4.3 Invalid values for TOE parameters

**5.3.5.4.6.2.4.3.0-1**  (ID: `11458128`)

Invalid values for TOE parameters
Timing offset estimation for PUCCH are performed in 5G-L1-UL per RX antenna and shall be combined before report to 5G-L2-PS.

The number of configured RX antenna is derived according to 5G\_L1\_2797.

The timing offset combining algorithm is described in section 2.7.6 of the 5Gmax algorithm specifications (see 5G\_L1\_7703).

5G-L1-UL shall perform TO estimation as explained above in Loki L1 HW.

[5GC002244-A]

Invalid value of shortTermTaMetric and shortTermTaMetricOfAnt shall be set to −32768.

Invalid value of shortTermTaPeakAmp and shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt shall be set to −1.

[End 5GC002244-A]

**[RP003187-F] The requirement is also applicable for** L1 Thor for FR1-TDD-eCPRI**. [End RP003187-F]**\*\*\*\*

**[RP003187-M] The requirement is also applicable for** L1 Thor for FR1-FDD-CPRI. **[End RP003187-M]**\*\*\*\*

**[CB010575-D] The requirement is also applicable for L1** Thor for FR1-TDD-CPRI **[End CB010575-D]**\*\*\*\*

**[CB009514-F] The requirement is also applicable for Thor(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e** [End CB009514-F]\*\*\*\*

---

##### 5.3.5.4.6.3 Carrier frequency offset estimation

###### 5.3.5.4.6.3.1 General

**5.3.5.4.6.3.1.0-3**  (ID: `12711523`)

General
For FR1-TDD and FR1-FDD for PUCCH format3 5G-L1-UL shall perform Frequency Offset Estimation ([FOE](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_z_SHQWPNEfCtwYrh0KQ_DA)) based on PUCCH DMRS when additional DMRS is configured with intra-slot frequency hopping (when there are more than one DMRS symbol per hop).

Frequency Offset is estimated per Rx spatial stream.

5G-L1-UL shall use Itv =4 to adjust the time interval for short term correlation calculation between different DMRS symbols.

FOE is specified in section 2.4.4.1 of the 5GMax algorithm specification.

FOE is supported for following L1 variants:

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | Technology | FR1-TDD (CPRI/ eCPRI-7.2a/ eCPRI-7.2e) | FR1-FDD (OBSAI/ CPRI/ eCPRI-7.2a) | First Feature |
| L1 HW | Loner | not supported | not supported | - |
| Loki | supported | supported | CB008792 |  |
| Thor | supported | supported | CB008827 |  |
| Odin |  |  |  |  |

Note:

1. When the number of PUCCH symbols is lower than 10 (i.e. UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->numOfSymbols value < 10), 5G-L1-UL shall not perform FOE on PUCCH F3 and it shall report invalid FOE result (i.e. 0+j0, see [11109788](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ko8YFfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for Carrier Frequency Offset Handling ([11150515](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksT1LvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
2. For PUCCH format3 this requirement is not applicable when parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq-> PucchResourceAllocationConfig-> isServingSubcell IE is set to false (configuration for non-serving subcell for FDD supercell), refer to ([11453916](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAajLvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[CNI-108168-J] The requirement was refined under CNI-108168  [End CNI-108168-J]

---

###### 5.3.5.4.6.3.2 Short Term Frequency Offset Measurement

**5.3.5.4.6.3.2.0-1**  (ID: `12711555`)

Short Term Frequency Offset Measurement
For FR1-TDD and FR1-FDD for PUCCH format3 5G-L1-UL shall calculate Short Term ([ST](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_8sZYsGWLEfCtwYrh0KQ_DA)) Frequency Offset metric on PUCCH when additional DMRS is configured and reports this metric to 5G-L2-PS.

5G-L1-UL shall report a ST FO metric via L1-L2 IF parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->shortTermCfoMetric

ST FO metric measurement is supported for following L1 variants:

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | Technology | FR1-TDD (CPRI/ eCPRI-7.2a/ eCPRI-7.2e) | FR1-FDD (OBSAI/ CPRI/ eCPRI-7.2a) | First Feature |
| L1 HW | Loner | not supported | not supported | - |
| Loki | supported | supported | CB008792 |  |
| Thor | supported | supported | CB008827 |  |
| Odin |  |  |  |  |

Note:

1. 5G-L1-UL shall report Short Term ([ST](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_8sZYsGWLEfCtwYrh0KQ_DA)) Frequency Offset metric across all the RX antennas (shall be combined before report to 5G-L2-PS).
2. For invalid values for ST FO measurement please find:[11454096](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAbxTPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)
3. For PUCCH format3 this requirement is not applicable when parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq-> PucchResourceAllocationConfig-> isServingSubcell IE is set to false (configuration for non-serving subcell for FDD supercell), refer to ([11453916](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAajLvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

###### 5.3.5.4.6.3.3 Antenna-wise Short Term Frequency Offset Measurement

**5.3.5.4.6.3.3.0-1**  (ID: `12711574`)

Antenna-wise Short Term Frequency Offset Measurement
For FR1-TDD and FR1-FDD for PUCCH format3 5G-L1-UL shall calculate antenna-wise ("spatial-stream-wise") Short Term ([ST](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_8sZYsGWLEfCtwYrh0KQ_DA)) Frequency Offset metrics on PUCCH when additional DMRS is configured and reports this metrics to 5G-L2-PS.

The metrics are calculated separately for each RX antenna (spatial stream).

5G-L1-UL shall report the antenna-wise ST FO metrics via L1-L2 IF parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->extendedParameters->shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt

Antenna-wise ST FO metrics measurement is supported for following L1 variants:

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | Technology | FR1-TDD (CPRI/ eCPRI-7.2a/ eCPRI-7.2e) | FR1-FDD (OBSAI/ CPRI/ eCPRI-7.2a) | First Feature |
| L1 HW | Loner | not supported | not supported | - |
| Loki | supported | supported | CB008792 |  |
| Thor | supported | supported | CB008827 |  |
| Odin |  |  |  |  |

Note:

1. Mapping between antenna-wise ST FO and the spatial stream is given in [12696416](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_v6JTYFu1EfCVVMis1D3_Nw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)
2. The number of configured RX antenna is derived according to [12576677](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wsVMkDA3EfCRMdP0Nuo3Hg?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) .
3. For invalid values for antenna-wise ST TO measurements please find:[11454096](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAbxTPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)
4. For PUCCH format3 this requirement is not applicable when parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq-> PucchResourceAllocationConfig-> isServingSubcell IE is set to false (configuration for non-serving subcell for FDD supercell), refer to ([11453916](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAajLvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

###### 5.3.5.4.6.3.4 Mapping between antenna-wise ST FOE and spatial streams

**5.3.5.4.6.3.4.0-1**  (ID: `12696435`)

Mapping between antenna-wise ST FOE and spatial streams
For antenna-wise ST FOE for PUCCH format3 5G-L1-UL shall use mapping between ST FOE and spatial stream defined as follows:

A2 or C2:

-shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt[0]: (ce)AxC [0]

-shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt[1]: (ce)AxC [1]

A4 or C4:

-shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt[0]: (ce)AxC [0]

-shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt[1]: (ce)AxC [1]

-shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt[2]: (ce)AxC [2]

-shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt[3]: (ce)AxC [3]

C8 or C8'2 or C8'4 or C8'8 [CB013442-D] or A8 [End CB013442-D] :

-shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt[0]: ceAxC [0]

-shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt[1]: ceAxC [1]

-shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt[2]: ceAxC [2]

-shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt[3]: ceAxC [3]

-shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt[4]: ceAxC [4]

-shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt[5]: ceAxC [5]

-shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt[6]: ceAxC [6]

-shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt[7]: ceAxC [7]

Note:

1. ST FOE estimates are sent to L2 via parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveResp->Subcells->PucchResources->extendedParameters->shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt . This parameter is a dynamic array with size based on subcell type. Refer to 5G\_L1\_IF\_221\_replaced([11514182](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BQvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

2. For eCPRI case, the order eAxC spatial stream values of the ST-FOE (shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt) in the array shall follow the same mapping order of EcpriConfig struct in 5G\_L1\_IF\_15453\_replaced([11514119](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR1aN_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).

---

###### 5.3.5.4.6.3.5 ST CFO Protection

**5.3.5.4.6.3.5.0-4**  (ID: `12521455`)

ST CFO Protection
For PUCCH F3, 5G-L1-UL shall validate short-term FOE results (both shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt in 5G\_L1\_IF\_221\_replaced([11514182](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BQvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and shortTermCfoMetric in 5G\_L1\_IF\_222\_replaced([11514207](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BR_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and adjust its range if necessary. See 5G\_L1\_10507\_replaced([11401361](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e9DGF_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for PUSCH FOE protection as reference.

Note: Detailed procedures can be found in 5gmax specification document chapter 2.3.3.3.

The FOE protection (range adjustment) shall be supported in FDD Loki and Thor and in TDD FR1 Loki and Thor.

[CB014106-SR-A] This requirement shall be supported in Thor FR1-TDD-7-2e-eCPRI. [End CB014106-SR-A]

---

###### 5.3.5.4.6.3.6 Frozen Requirements

**5.3.5.4.6.3.6.0-1**  (ID: `11480933`)

Frozen Requirements
Content of this requirement is frozen and valid until 26R1 release, For later releases please refer to the objects below in chapters: [12696416](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_v6JTYFu1EfCVVMis1D3_Nw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

For Thor:

For PUCCH F1 and F3, 5G-L1-UL expects to get antenna-wise LT-FOE from 5G-L2-PS and perform antenna-wise FOC. The mapping between each element of the IE longTermCfoMetricOfAnt and the spatial stream depends on CPRI/eCPRI configuration as below.

 eCPRI configuration

For eCPRI case, the order eAxC spatial stream values of the antennas-wise ST-FOE (shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt) in 5G\_L1\_IF\_201\_replaced([11513837](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRzlAfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and LT-FOE (**[Before CB009363-D]longTermCfoMetricOfAnt** [CB009363-D] longTermCfoMetricOfBeam **[End CB009363-D]) in the array in 5G\_L1\_IF\_216\_replaced([11513990](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MIfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and their mapping to beam patternId shall follow the same mapping order of *EcpriConfig struct in ~~5G\_L1\_5G21A\_263~~ 5G\_L1\_IF\_266\_replaced([11514653](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR4dkfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).***\*\*\*\*

 CPRI configuration

For CPRI case, table below is used for the order of AxC spatial stream values.

**Mapping between antenna-wise ST FOE/LT FOE and spatial stream for (e)CPRI**

**[Before CB009363-D]**

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Subcell Type | ST FOE for antenna i | LT FOE for antenna i | (e)CPRI spatial stream | **First feature** |
| A2 or C2 | shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt[0] | longTermCfoMetricOfAnt[0] | (ce)AxC0 |  |
| shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt[1] | longTermCfoMetricOfAnt[1] | (ce)AxC1 |  |  |
| A4 or C4 | shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt[0] | longTermCfoMetricOfAnt[0] | (ce)AxC0 |  |
| shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt[1] | longTermCfoMetricOfAnt[1] | (ce)AxC1 |  |  |
| shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt[2] | longTermCfoMetricOfAnt[2] | (ce)AxC2 |  |  |
| shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt[3] | longTermCfoMetricOfAnt[3] | (ce)AxC3 |  |  |
| C8 | shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt[0] | longTermCfoMetricOfAnt[0] | ceAxC0 | **CB009363-B** |
| shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt[1] | longTermCfoMetricOfAnt[1] | ceAxC1 |  |  |
| … | … | … |  |  |
| shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt[i] | longTermCfoMetricOfAnt[i] | ceAxCi |  |  |
| … | … | … |  |  |
| shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt[7] | longTermCfoMetricOfAnt[7] | ceAxC7 |  |  |

**[CB009363-D]**

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Subcell Type | ST FOE for antenna i | LT FOE for antenna j | (e)CPRI spatial stream i | **First feature** |
| A2 or C2 | shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt[0] | longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[0] | (ce)AxC0 | **CB009363-D** |
| shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt[1] | longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[1] | (ce)AxC1 |  |  |
| A4 or C4 | shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt[0] | longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[0] | (ce)AxC0 | **CB009363-D** |
| shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt[1] | longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[1] | (ce)AxC1 |  |  |
| shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt[2] | longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[2] | (ce)AxC2 |  |  |
| shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt[3] | longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[3] | (ce)AxC3 |  |  |
| C8 | shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt [0] | longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[0] | ceAxC0 | **CB009363-D** |
| shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt[1] | longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[0] | ceAxC1 |  |  |
| shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt[2] | longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[1] | ceAxC2 |  |  |
| shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt[3] | longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[1] | ceAxC3 |  |  |
| shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt[4] | longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[2] | ceAxC4 |  |  |
| shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt[5] | longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[2] | ceAxC5 |  |  |
| shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt[6] | longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[3] | ceAxC6 |  |  |
| shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt[7] | longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[3] | ceAxC7 |  |  |

**[End CB009363-D]**

Refer to "**5GMax-5G New Radio Algorithm Specification" Section 2.3.3 for algorithm implementation steps.(<https://nokia.sharepoint.com/sites/ATFL1Spec/Controlled%20Documents/Forms/AllItems.aspx?id=%2Fsites%2FATFL1Spec%2FControlled%20Documents%2FArchitecture%20Documents&viewid=3f46fe9f%2De8dc%2D4d3a%2D8bf3%2D40d24786af68)>**

Note 1: CPRI FR1 TDD 4Rx beamforming is not supported. Thus antenna-wise ST-FOE and FOC for PUSCH is not designed to support CPRI FR1 TDD 4Rx beamforming. Reason behind is that, in CPRI 4Rx beamforming cells, beam pattern Id mapping to AxC Id is not specified. 5G-L2-PS doesn’t know beam pattern Id’s mapping to AxC stream, and thus can’t perform beam specific FO handling.

Note 2: although antenna-wise ST-FOE and FOC is introduced for FR1 TDD Rx beamforming cells with eCPRI RU, L1's behavior is the same among:

- CPRI or eCPRI FR1 TDD 2RX beamforming

- CPRI or eCPRI FR1 TDD 2RX non beamforming

- CPRI FR1 TDD 4Rx non beamforming

- CPRI FR1 FDD 2RX non beamforming

- CPRI FR1 FDD 4Rx non beamforming

- FR2 TDD 2Rx

-  ***\*[CB009363-B] For Thor L1 HW eCPRI FR1 TDD 8RX beamforming* \*[End CB009363-B]**\*\*\*\*

**[CB009363-D]**

The parameter shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt in **UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs message is changed to dynamic array based on subcell type. Refer to 5G\_L1\_IF\_221\_replaced([11514182](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BQvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

The parameter longTermCfoMetricOfAnt is changed to longTermCfoMetricOfBeam in MULTI and L1SW in 23R4. Refer to 5G\_L1\_13041\_replaced([11396378](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8r5xPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**[End CB009363-D]**

**[CB010575-D] The requirement is also applicable for L1** Thor for FR1-TDD-CPRI, but only for up to 4 spatial streams (uplink subcell type C2 and C4). ***\*[End CB010575-D]*****\***

**[CB007595-B] The requirement is also applicable for L1** Thor for FR1-TDD-7-2e-eCPRI **[End CB007595-B]**\*\*\*\*

|  |  |
| --- | --- |

##### 5.3.5.4.6.4 Noise power

###### 5.3.5.4.6.4.1 General

**5.3.5.4.6.4.1.0-2**  (ID: `12723225`)

General
For FR1-TDD and FR1-FDD for PUCCH format3 5G-L1-UL shall perform the Noise Power Estimation ([NPE](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_hle2YGenEfCk8v_SG2h2xg)). Noise Power is estimated per Rx spatial stream.

NPE is specified in section 2.4.4.5 of the 5GMax algorithm specification.

Note:

1. For impact of using Low-PAPR DMRS Type2 (Release16) on NPE measurements please find: [11361085](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucyymvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) , [11105258](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koIfx_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

###### 5.3.5.4.6.4.2 Noise Power measurement

**5.3.5.4.6.4.2.0-2**  (ID: `12723228`)

Noise Power measurement
For FR1-TDD and FR1-FDD for PUCCH format3 for each scheduled resource 5G-L1-UL shall calculate the noise power (interference + thermal noise) and reports this estimate to 5G-L2-PS.

This estimate is derived while considering only the allocated PRBs for a given resource. This estimate is normalized to one PRB and aggregating over all receiving antennas. The unit of this estimate is dBm.

5G-L1-UL shall report estimate via L1-L2 IF parameters: UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->noisePower

Noise Power estimation algorithm is specified in section 2.8.3.3 and 2.4.4.5 of the 5GMax algorithm specification.

Noise Power measurement for PUCCH format3 is supported for following L1 variants:

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | Technology | FR1-TDD (CPRI/ eCPRI-7.2a/ eCPRI-7.2e) | FR1-FDD (OBSAI/ CPRI/ eCPRI-7.2a) | First Feature |
| L1 HW | Loner | supported | supported | Legacy |
| Loki | supported | supported | Legacy |  |
| Thor | supported | supported | CB007487 |  |
| Odin | [CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] Supported for  FR1-TDD eCPRI-7.2a / FR1-TDD eCPRI-7.2e [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] | [CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] Supported for FR1-FDD CPRI / FR1-FDD eCPRI-7.2a [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] |  |  |

1. For invalid values for Noise Power measurements please find: ([12733068](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_mMhiRXRFEfCRE7eh4Ndkrw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

---

###### 5.3.5.4.6.4.3 Noise Power per PRB measurement

**5.3.5.4.6.4.3.0-2**  (ID: `12723229`)

Noise Power per PRB measurement
For all PUCCH transmission for each configured subcell for each slot 5G-L1-UL shall calculate the noise power per PRB estimation (interference + thermal noise) and reports this estimation to 5G-L2-PS.

There are following computations in 2 steps:

Step 1: 5G-L1-UL shall compute noise estimate per PUCCH format and per PRB, while considering all the PUCCH resources scheduled within the same PUCCH format and in the same PRB in the slot.

For PUCCH format3 transmission 5G-L1-UL shall estimate noise power on DMRS as described in section 2.4.4.5 of the 5Gmax algorithm specifications.

5G-L1-UL shall average estimates over all the receiving antennas (spatial streams).

In case of frequency hopping 5G-L1-UL shall estimate noise power as first part-hop and the second part-hop separately as two PUCCH transmissions with the same format with less symbol's quantity for each part.

Step 2: In case of more than one PUCCH transmission in PRB (also in case of different formats) 5G-L1-UL shall compute one noise estimate per PRB averaged over all PUCCH transmission in the same PRB in the slot.

5G-L1-UL shall convert these estimated noise values to logarithmic scale in dBm unit. Power scaling and conversion to dBm unit shall be done as specified in  [11458486](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAv6WPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) for Loki and [11458486](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAv6WPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) for Thor-BB.

5G-L1-UL shall report noise power per PRB measurement via L1-L2 IF parameter: UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->noisePerPrb . Type of parameter is array of float32, where array indices are selected according to PRB positions.

Noise Power per PRB estimation algorithm is specified in section 2.8.3.4 of the 5GMax algorithm specification.

Noise Power per PRB measurement for PUCCH format3 is supported for following L1 variants:

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | Technology | FR1-TDD (CPRI/ eCPRI-7.2a/ eCPRI-7.2e) | FR1-FDD (OBSAI/ CPRI/ eCPRI-7.2a) | First Feature |
| L1 HW | Loner | not supported | not supported | - |
| Loki | supported | supported | CB008021 |  |
| Thor | supported | supported | CB009027 |  |
| Odin | [CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] Supported for  FR1-TDD eCPRI-7.2a / FR1-TDD eCPRI-7.2e [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] | [CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] Supported for FR1-FDD CPRI / FR1-FDD eCPRI-7.2a [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] |  |  |

Note:

1. When only zero-valued samples are got from the radio module or (e)CPRI interface for all the receiving antennas (spatial streams) (e.g. broken antenna scenario or protection switching in TSN), in case of noisy measurement, or for nonscheduled PRBs, 5G-L1-UL shall report INVALID value.
2. For invalid values for Noise Power per PRB measurements please find details in: [12714973](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_lIqIEGjtEfC_xcanjXaboQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)
3. For PUCCH format3 this requirement is not applicable when parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq-> PucchResourceAllocationConfig-> isServingSubcell IE is set to false (configuration for non-serving subcell for FDD supercell), refer to ([11453916](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAajLvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

###### 5.3.5.4.6.4.4 Simplified algorithm for noise power estimation

###### 5.3.5.4.6.4.4.1 Activation of algorithm

**5.3.5.4.6.4.4.1.0-1**  (ID: `11458302`)

Activation of algorithm
5G-L1-UL shall support the simplified noise power estimation algorithm for PUCCH Format 2 and Format 3 as respectively described in 5G\_L1\_10010\_replaced([11457474](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAro5fvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L1\_10011\_replaced([11458327](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAv6U_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) when RAD parameter rdPucchNPESimplified  (see 5G\_L1\_10013\_replaced([11453022](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAWRvfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is activated. Activation of the simplified method is done using a pre-processor directive (before compilation).

HW-Technology Map:

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Technology / HW | Loki | Thor |
| FR1-FDD-CPRI | Supported for F3 | Supported for F3 |
| FR1-FDD-7-2a-eCPRI | Supported for F3 | NA |
| FR1-TDD-CPRI | Supported for F2, F3 | [CB010575-D] Supported for F3 [End CB010575-D] |
| FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI | Supported for F2, F3 | Supported for F3 |
| FR1-TDD-7-2e-eCPRI | NA | [CB009514-F] Supported for F3 [End CB009514-F] |
| FR2-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI | Supported for F2 | NA |

11458327:
Algorithm description
Simplification of the noise power estimation algorithm for PUCCH Format 3 is introduced by substituting weighting Matrix S with alternative matrix M. Matrix M is derived from LDL decomposition of S, i.e.,
[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in dark text on a white background. The equation is:
S = V · E · VH = (VE1/2) · (VE1/2)H = MMH
The equation appears to be related to matrix operations, where 'V' and 'E' are likely matrices, and 'H' denotes the conjugate transpose (Hermitian transpose). 'S' and 'M' are also likely matrices. The term E1/2 suggests a matrix square root.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_6641.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
Matrix M is precomputed and stored in memory. No performance loss expected and, due to M having reduced column dimension, less DSP operations are required. The simplified noise power estimate (per chunk block i, antenna port p and spatial stream ant)  is:
[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$\hat{\sigma}*{noise,i,p,ant}^2 = (\hat{H}*{p,sep}^{pilot})^H MM^H \hat{H}*{p,sep}^{pilot} = (M^H \hat{H}*{p,sep}^{pilot})^H (M^H \hat{H}*{p,sep}^{pilot}) = \sum*{k=1}^{R} |[M^H \hat{H}*{p,sep}]*{k}|^2$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_6641.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]
 
Full description of the simplification and notation in section "2.4.4.5" of 5Gmax algorithm specification (5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
 
[CB007595-B] The requirement is also applicable for L1 Thor for FR1-TDD-7-2e-eCPRI [End CB007595-B]
 
HW-Technology Map:

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Technology / HW | Loki | Thor |
| FR1-FDD-CPRI | Supported | Supported |
| FR1-FDD-OBSAI |  | [CB010969-SR-CB] Supported [End CB010969-SR-CB] |
| FR1-FDD-7-2a-eCPRI | Supported | NA |
| FR1-TDD-CPRI | Supported | [CB010575-D] Supported [End CB010575-D] |
| FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI | Supported | Supported |
| FR1-TDD-7-2e-eCPRI | NA | Supported |

General
PUCCH Format 3

###### 5.3.5.4.6.4.5.2 Noise Power measurement

###### 5.3.5.4.6.4.5.2.0-1 Noise Power measurement Loner and Loki (ID: 11458266)

**5.3.5.4.6.4.5.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11458272`)

Noise Power measurement
For each configured subcell, 5GNB 5G-L1-UL shall estimate the noise (interference + thermal noise) power using the DMRS associated to PUCCH. This estimate is derived while considering only the allocated PRBs. Then, 5G-L1-UL reports the estimated value (after normalizing to one PRB, averaging over all the layers and aggregating over all receiving antennas) to 5G-L2-PS within the parameter noisePower in UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs message.

The noise estimation algorithm on PUCCH is described in section 2.6.2.2 "2.7.3.2 PUCCH" of the 5Gmax algorithm specification (see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_916 5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

NOTE: The noise estimate on non-allocated PRBs for the PUCCH symbol is not required.

For details please also see 5G\_L1\_4462\_replaced([11454566](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAeNhvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

PUCCH Format0 is supported. Since there is no DMRS associated to PUCCH Format0, the noise estimation will be performed based on PUCCH data signals, as defined in section 2.4.3.1.1 "2.4.1.1.3 Noise Power Estimation" of the 5Gmax algorithm specification v5.3 (see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_916 5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

PUCCH format 2 is also supported. Noise estimation is performed based on PUCCH format 2 DMRS.

FDD FR1 L1 Loner: PUCCH formats 1 and 3 are also supported. Noise estimation is performed based on PUCCH format 1 DMRS and PUCCH format 3 DMRS, respectively.

[CB006064-A] TDD FR1 L1 Loner/Loki: PUCCH formats 1 and 3 are also supported. Noise estimation is performed based on PUCCH format 1 DMRS and PUCCH format 3 DMRS, respectively.[End CB006064-A]

5G-L1-UL shall also perform noise power estimation on PUCCH format0 and format2 as explained above in Loki L1 HW.

[5GC002481-AA] For FDD and Loki L1 HW, the noise power estimation on PUCCH format1 and format3 as explained above shall be also supported. [End 5GC002481-AA]

[Before-CNI-122313-A]

[CB009443-C] This requirement for PUCCH format 1 and 3 shall be supported in RINLINE1 HW for FR1-TDD-eCPRI. [End CB009443-C]

[CB009444-I] This requirement for PUCCH format 1 and 3 shall be supported in RINLINE1 HW for FR1-FDD-eCPRI. [End CB009444-I]

[CNI-122313-A]

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

[End CNI-122313-A]

###### 5.3.5.4.6.4.5.2.0-2 Noise Power measurement Thor (ID: 11458279)

**5.3.5.4.6.4.5.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11458286`)

Noise Power measurement
For Thor

For each configured subcell, 5GNB 5G-L1-UL shall estimate the noise (interference + thermal noise) power using the DMRS associated to PUCCH. This estimate is derived while considering only the allocated PRBs. Then, 5G-L1-UL reports the estimated value (after normalizing to one PRB, averaging over all the layers and aggregating over all receiving antennas) to 5G-L2-PS within the parameter noisePower in UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs message.

The noise estimation algorithm on PUCCH is described in section "2.7.3.2 PUCCH" of the 5Gmax algorithm specification (see 5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

NOTE: The noise estimate on non-allocated PRBs for the PUCCH symbol is not required.

FDD FR1 L1 : PUCCH formats 1 and 3 are also supported. Noise estimation is performed based on PUCCH format 1 DMRS and PUCCH format 3 DMRS, respectively.

TDD FR1 L1 : PUCCH formats 1 and 3 are also supported. Noise estimation is performed based on PUCCH format 1 DMRS and PUCCH format 3 DMRS, respectively.

NOTE: For details please also see, format 1 : 5G\_L1\_14217\_replaced([11454886](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAgCsfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),  format 3 : 5G\_L1\_14219\_replaced([11454795](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAfbpPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[RP003187-F] In terms of PUCCH formats 1 and 3 the requirement is also applicable for L1 Thor for FR1-TDD-eCPRI; L1 Thor does not support short PUCCH formats. See also 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1656\_replaced([11108410](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koqrRPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End RP003187-F]

[RP003187-M] In terms of PUCCH formats 1 and 3 the requirement is also applicable for L1 Thor for FR1-FDD-CPRI; L1 Thor does not support short PUCCH formats. See also 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1656\_replaced([11108410](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koqrRPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End RP003187-M]

[CB010575-D] The requirement is also applicable for L1 Thor for FR1-TDD-CPRI [End CB010575-D]

11458486:
Noise Power per PRB measurement
11458486:
Noise Power per PRB measurement
Noise power estimation per PRB for each format is performed as follow.

Format 0:

The noise power estimation is performed based on PUCCH data signals as described in section 2.4.1.1.3 “Noise Power Estimation" of the 5Gmax algorithm specifications (see 5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) per symbol.

All calculated power noise for each symbol per PRB are averaged for a given PRB if many PUCCH transmission in the same PRBs are multiplexed.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$P\_{N,PRB,r} = \frac{1}{N\_{pucch}} \sum\_{l=0}^{N\_{pucch}-1} P\_{N,l,r}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_6646.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a close-up of the text "P N,I" in a sans-serif font. The letters are slightly blurred and have a gradient of colors, appearing to be orange, yellow, and blue. The text is set against a white background, with a black border on the right and bottom edges of the visible portion.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_6646.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]: noise calculated in 2.4.1.1.3 Noise power estimation[image-2][image\_desc]The image contains a blurry, pixelated graphic with the letters "P" and "N" in a stylized font. The "P" is in a darker color, possibly blue or purple, with a lighter outline. The "N" is in a lighter color, possibly yellow or orange, also with a lighter outline. The letters are positioned next to each other, with the "P" slightly to the left and above the "N". The background is black.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_6646.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2].

[image-3][image\_desc]The image is a close-up, abstract, and blurry depiction of a stylized letter "L" or a similar geometric shape. The shape is rendered with a gradient of colors, transitioning from a warm yellow and orange on the left to cool blues and purples in the center, and then to white and a faint gray on the right. [image-4][image\_desc]The image is too blurry and unclear to provide a detailed description.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_6646.005.png[/image\_path][/image-4] : antenna index

[image-5][image\_desc]The image contains the text "N puceh" in a blurry, stylized font. The text is white with a subtle gradient effect, and it appears to be on a white background. The bottom portion of the image is black.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_6646.006.png[/image\_path][/image-5]: used symbols for PUCCH format 0 transmission.

In case of of frequency hopping where 2 PRBs are used for a PUCCH transmission we shall average noise power separately for each PRB.

Then, calculated noise power shall be averaged over all the receiving antennas (spatial streams) for each PRB.

Format 1:

Noise power [image-6][image\_desc]The image contains the text "P\_noise,m'". The text is written in a dark blue color with a slight blur. The letter "P" is capitalized and is larger than the other letters. The letters "noise" are in lowercase and are followed by a comma. The letter "m" is in lowercase and is followed by a prime symbol.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_6646.007.png[/image\_path][/image-6]shall be estimated as described in section 2.4.2.5 “Noise power and signal power estimation" of the 5Gmax algorithm specifications (see 5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Then, calculated noise power shall be averaged over all the receiving antennas (spatial streams).

This shall be done for each PRB for the PUCCH format 1 transmission, because if inter slot hopping is enabled PUCCH format 1 transmission could occupy 2 PRBs.

[image-7][image\_desc]The image contains the text "m" followed by a prime symbol. The letters are rendered in a stylized font with a gradient effect, transitioning from yellow to blue and then to purple. The prime symbol is yellow. The text is set against a white background.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_6646.008.png[/image\_path][/image-7] - hop index - determines PRB index. For one PRB [image-8][image\_desc]The image contains the mathematical expression "m' = 0". The text is in a sans-serif font and appears to be in a light blue color with some white highlights. The background is white.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_6646.009.png[/image\_path][/image-8] and noise power [image-9][image\_desc]The image contains the text "P noise,0". The text is in a dark color against a white background. The letter "P" is larger than the other letters and is positioned to the left. The word "noise" is written in lowercase letters and is positioned to the right of "P". The number "0" is written to the right of "noise" and is slightly smaller than the letters.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_6646.010.png[/image\_path][/image-9] and for other [image-10][image\_desc]The image contains the mathematical expression "m' = 1". The text is rendered in a stylized font with a gradient effect, giving it a slightly blurred appearance. The characters are white with a subtle blue and pink hue. The background is white, and the entire image is framed by a black border.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_6646.011.png[/image\_path][/image-10] and noise power [image-11][image\_desc]The image contains the text "P\_noise,1". The text is in a dark color against a white background. The letters are slightly blurred, and there are some colorful artifacts around the edges of the letters, particularly on the left side of the "P". The text is positioned in the center of the image.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_6646.012.png[/image\_path][/image-11], if there is no hopping then [image-12][image\_desc]The image contains the text "m" followed by a prime symbol. The letters are rendered in a stylized font with a gradient effect, transitioning from yellow to blue and then to purple. The prime symbol is yellow. The text is set against a white background.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_6646.013.png[/image\_path][/image-12]= 0 only.

PUCCH F1 noise power estimation must be achieved separately for PUCCH resources with different symbol length multiplexed in same PRB.

For details please also see, format 1 : 5G\_L1\_14217\_replaced([11454886](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAgCsfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Format 2:

Noise power shall be estimated estimated on PUCCH format 2 DMRS as described in section "2.4.3.1.3 Noise Power Estimation" of the 5Gmax algorithm specifications (see 5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Then calculated noise power is averaged over all resources in slot for different PUCCH format 2 transmission.

Then, calculated noise power shall be averaged over all the receiving antennas (spatial streams).

Format 3:

At first noise power shall be estimated on PUCCH format 3 DMRS as described in section 2.4.4.5 “Noise power and signal power estimation" of the 5Gmax algorithm specifications (see 5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Then, calculated power noise per PRB is averaged over all the receiving antennas (spatial streams).

NOTE: For details please also see,  format 3 : 5G\_L1\_14219\_replaced([11454795](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAfbpPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

In case of frequency hopping for format 2 or 3, noise power shall be estimated as first part and the second part separately as two PUCCH with the same format with less symbols quantity for each part.

In case of many PUCCH transmission in the same PRB we shall average all of them.

[Before CNI-126050-A]

These estimated values are converted in W (Watt). The reported value is in aW (10-18 Watt) units.

[CNI-126050-A]

L1 shall convert these estimated noise values to logarithmic scale in dBm unit. Power scaling and conversion to dBm unit shall be done as specified in 5G\_L1\_4204\_replaced([11421346](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-hFsvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for Loki and 5G\_L1\_8907\_replaced([11422159](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-hswfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for Thor-BB.

[End CNI-126050-A]

L1 shall send estimated values to L2-PS using noisePerPrb IE in UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs message. Array indices shall be selected according to PRB positions

Unallocated PUCCH resources are set to INVALID value.

This requirement is applied to ABIP as well.

Averaging over spatial streams also applies to Thor HW for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-TDD-eCPRI.

HW-Technology Map:

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Technology / HW | Loki | Thor |
| FR1-FDD-CPRI | Supported for F1, F3 | Supported for F1, F3 |
| FR1-FDD-OBSAI |  | Supported for F1, F3 |
| FR1-FDD-7-2a-eCPRI | Supported for F1, F3 | Supported for F1, F3 |
| FR1-TDD-CPRI | Supported for F0, F1, F2, F3 | Supported for F1, F3 |
| FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI | Supported for F0, F1, F2, F3 | Supported for F1, F3 |
| FR1-TDD-7-2e-eCPRI | NA | Supported for F1, F3 |
| FR2-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI | Supported for F0, F2 | Supported for F0, F2 |

---

##### 5.3.5.4.6.5 Signal Power

###### 5.3.5.4.6.5.1 General

**5.3.5.4.6.5.1.0-2**  (ID: `12723230`)

General
For FR1-TDD and FR1-FDD for PUCCH format3 5G-L1-UL shall estimate Signal Power per Rx antenna (spatial stream).

Signal Power estimation is specified in section 2.4.4.5 of the 5GMax algorithm specification.

Note:

1. For impact of using Low-PAPR DMRS Type2 (Release16) on Signal Power estimation please find: [11361085](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucyymvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) , [11105288](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koJG0vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

###### 5.3.5.4.6.5.2 Received Power

**5.3.5.4.6.5.2.0-4**  (ID: `12717204`)

Received Power
For FR1-TDD and FR1-FDD for PUCCH format3 for each scheduled resource 5G-L1-UL shall estimate one measurement for the UL received power and report it to 5G-L2-PS.

5G-L1-UL shall perform received power measurement on DMRS associated with PUCCH.

Each UL received power measurement shall be averaged over all the allocated REs for DMRSs and aggregated over all the receiving antennas. Then, one measurement normalized to one PRB shall be reported to L2 .

The scaling factor applied at the radio module to reach a target noise bitwidth shall be compensated at 5G-L1-UL for all the UL power measurements using the IE  UlCell\_SetupReq->rxScalingFactor  (for details see: [11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ), [11418478](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-ZJ5_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).

5G-L1-UL shall report estimation via L1-L2 IF parameter: UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->rxPower .

The rxPower parameter is defined in dBm unit as illustrated in [11514200](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BRfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

The UL received power estimation algorithm on PUCCH is described in section 2.8.4.2 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification: [11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) .

Note:

1. rxScalingFactor value is set as described in [11288559](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tp7ttPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)
2. When only zero-valued samples are received from the radio module or (e)CPRI interface for all the receiving antennas (eg. broken antenna scenario), 5G-L1-UL shall set the rxPower parameter sent in UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs message to invalid value  (-140dBm).
3. For invalid values for Received Power measurements please find: [12717252](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_AV0d4GmnEfC_xcanjXaboQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)
4. The measurement for the UL received power can be used as a level indicator for the UL power control.

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

##### 5.3.5.4.6.6 RSSI

**5.3.5.4.6.6.0-4**  (ID: `12717277`)

RSSI
For FR1-TDD and FR1-FDD for PUCCH format3 for each scheduled resource in slot 5G-L1-UL shall estimate one [RSSI](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_CtgTJmbXEfCwWbD4x7Iu-g) and report it to 5G-L2-PS.

The RSSI measurements shall be performed for DMRS associated wth PUCCH.

For each scheduled resource 5G-L1-UL shall estimate one measurement. Each RSSI measurement shall be averaged by over all the allocated REs for UL DMRSs (demodulation reference signals) and aggregated over all the receiving antennas. Then, one measurement normalized to one PRB shall be reported to L2 for long term (LT) averaging.

The scaling factor applied at the radio module to reach a target noise bitwidth shall be compensated at 5G-L1-UL for all the RSSI measurements ([11404480](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e9UL0PvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) using the IE UlCell\_SetupReq->rxScalingFactor (see: [11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The rssi parameter is defined in dBm unit as illustrated in: [11514200](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BRfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

5G-L1-UL shall report estimation via L1-L2 IF parameter: UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->rssi

The RSSI estimation algorithm on PUCCH is described in section  "2.8.2.2 PUCCH" of the 5Gmax algorithm specification (see: [11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note:

1. rxScalingFactor value is set as described in [11288559](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tp7ttPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)
2. When only zero-valued samples are received from the radio module or (e)CPRI interface for all the receiving antennas (eg. broken antenna scenario), 5G-L1-UL shall set the rssi parameter sent in UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs message to invalid value  (-140dBm).
3. For invalid values for RSSI measurements please find: [12717253](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_MIieAGmnEfC_xcanjXaboQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)
4. The RSSI measurement can be used as a level indicator for the UL power control.

5. For PUCCH format3 estimated RSSI is not reported to 5G-L2-PS when parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq-> PucchResourceAllocationConfig-> isServingSubcell IE is set to false (configuration for non-serving subcell for FDD supercell), refer to ([11453916](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAajLvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

##### 5.3.5.4.6.7 SINR Estimation

**5.3.5.4.6.7.0-4**  (ID: `12717284`)

SINR Estimation
For FR1-TDD and FR1-FDD for PUCCH format3 for each scheduled resource 5G-L1-UL shall compute one SINR measurement.

Since only one logical antenna port is used by PUCCH format3, one estimate shall be then provided to 5G-L2-PS.

For formats3, each SINR measurement is computed at the equalizer output, averaged all the allocated REs for one NR-slot for particular resource (not normalized to one PRB). The signals received on all the active antennas are taken into account.

As a post-equalizer SINR is provided to 5G-L2-PS, its value depends on the equalizer type (e.g., MRC, IRC, etc.)

The sinr parameter is defined in dB unit as illustrated in:[11514200](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BRfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

5G-L1-UL shall report estimation via L1-L2 IF parameter: UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->sinr .

The SINR estimation algorithm on PUCCH is described in section  "2.8.5.2 PUCCH" of the 5Gmax algorithm specification (see:[11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note:

1. The thermal noise and the interference will be measured together, i.e., they won't be resolved independently.
2. Since PUCCH format3 is mapped to single logical antenna port (no layer mapping as per 38.211 section 6.3.2), 5G-L1-UL shall report invalid value for the SINR measurement associated to the layer index > 1
3. In the case of invalid measurements for SINR 5G-L1-UL shall report to 5G-L2-PS the value: -255 dB.
4. For invalid values for SINR measurements please find: [12717254](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Ow_uAGmnEfC_xcanjXaboQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)
5. The measurement for the SINR can be used as an indicator for the UL link adaptation.

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

##### 5.3.5.4.6.8 DTX Metric

**5.3.5.4.6.8.0-3**  (ID: `12819788`)

DTX Metric
For FR1-TDD and FR1-FDD for PUCCH format3 5G-L1-UL shall estimate metric that is used to indicates whether a PUCCH signal was transmitted and received as expected.

The DTX metric estimation methods for PUCCH format3 are described in section  2.4.4.13  of the 5Gmax algorithm specification.

Supported DTX estimation methods for PUCCH format3 for following L1 variants:

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | Technology | iFFTbased | DecodingBased | First Feature |
| L1 HW | Loner | supported | not supported | Legacy |
| Loki | supported | supported | CB007950 |  |
| Thor | supported | supported | CB007487 |  |
| Odin | [CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] Supported for  FR1-TDD eCPRI-7.2a / FR1-TDD eCPRI-7.2e [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] [CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] Supported for FR1-FDD CPRI / FR1-FDD eCPRI-7.2a [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] |  | CB012115 |  |

The calculation method selection algorithm is described: ( [11458733: DTX metric computation method selection algorithm](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAxIfPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

For DTX detection for PUCCH format3 details see: ([11458691: DTX Detection](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAxIdvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

Note:

1. iFFTbased DTX metric is computed according to equivalent SNR in time domain-based algorithm.

2. For PUCCH format3 this requirement is not applicable when parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq-> PucchResourceAllocationConfig-> isServingSubcell IE is set to false (configuration for non-serving subcell for FDD supercell), refer to ([11453916](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAajLvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
