##### 5.3.5.4.6.10 Post Processing

###### 5.3.5.4.6.10.1 Channel Smoothing

**5.3.5.4.6.10.1.0-2**  (ID: `13373085`)

Channel Smoothing
For PUCCH format3 5G-L1-UL shall apply MMSE smoothing to raw channel estimation in frequency-domain of each DMRS symbol.

For more details, please find sections  2.4.4.7, 2.4.4.5 and 2.4.4.1 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification.

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

##### 5.3.5.4.6.11 Disturbance Covariance matrix estimation (MMSE-IRC)

**5.3.5.4.6.11.0-2**  (ID: `13373086`)

Disturbance Covariance matrix estimation (MMSE-IRC)
For PUCCH format3 and MMSE-IRC receiver 5G-L1-UL shall estimate covariance matrix of interference and noise (Rdd) averaged over each hop.

Disturbance covariance matrix is a part of IRC receiver algorithm.

The covariance matrix of interference and noise is calculated per PRB per symbol.

Supported receiver modes are specified in:   [12576677](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wsVMkDA3EfCRMdP0Nuo3Hg)

For more details, please find section 2.4.4.8 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification.

[CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e [End CB012115-GA]

---

#### 5.3.5.4.7 Detection

##### 5.3.5.4.7.1 Rdd processing

###### 5.3.5.4.7.1.1 MMSE MRC

###### 5.3.5.4.7.1.1.1 Rdd Matrix

**5.3.5.4.7.1.1.1.0-2**  (ID: `13373087`)

Rdd Matrix
For PUCCH format3, for MMSE MRC receiver 5G-L1-UL shall calculate inverted Rdd matrix.

For MMSE-MRC equalizer, it’s assumed that there is no Rx stream correlated interference. Thus, Rdd matrix is a diagonal matrix with estimated noise power as diagonal elements.

Supported receiver modes are specified in:   [12576677](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wsVMkDA3EfCRMdP0Nuo3Hg)

For more details, please find sections  2.4.4.8 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification.

[CB012115-IA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a [End CB012115-IA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

###### 5.3.5.4.7.1.2 MMSE IRC

###### 5.3.5.4.7.1.2.1 Shrinkage procedure

**5.3.5.4.7.1.2.1.0-4**  (ID: `12723236`)

Shrinkage procedure
For FR1-TDD eCPRI-7.2a and FR1-TDD eCPRI-7.2e and FR1-FDD eCPRI-7.2a 5G-L1-UL shall support shrinkage solution for MMSE IRC receiver for PUCCH format3.

Supported receiver modes are specified in:   [12576677](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wsVMkDA3EfCRMdP0Nuo3Hg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

For more details, please find section 2.4.4.8  of the 5Gmax algorithm specification.

[CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e [End CB012115-GA]

---

###### 5.3.5.4.7.1.2.2 Cholesky Decomposition and Rdd Inversion

**5.3.5.4.7.1.2.2.0-2**  (ID: `12981406`)

Cholesky Decomposition and Rdd Inversion
For PUCCH format3, for MMSE IRC receiver 5G-L1-UL shall apply Cholesky decomposition and inversion of Rdd matrix (after shrinkage).

Supported receiver modes are specified in:   [12576677](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wsVMkDA3EfCRMdP0Nuo3Hg)

For more details, please find sections  2.4.4.8 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification.

###### 5.3.5.4.7.2.1.2 Transform Precoding for MMSE MRC

Transform Precoding for MMSE MRC

Equalization for MMSE IRC
For FR1-TDD eCPRI-7.2a and FR1-TDD eCPRI-7.2e and FR1-FDD eCPRI-7.2a 5G-L1-UL shall support MMSE IRC equalization algorithm for PUCCH format3.

##### 5.3.5.4.7.3 Demodulation

**5.3.5.4.7.3.0-2**  (ID: `13373095`)

Demodulation
For PUCCH format3 5G-L1-UL shall execute soft demodulation to calculate the LLR of each coded bit.

The parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->modulationType is used for demodulation.

For more details, please find section  2.4.4.10 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification and 3GPP TS 38.211 (v17.3.0): chapters 6.3.2.6.2

Note:

1. For PUCCH format3 this requirement is not applicable when parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq-> PucchResourceAllocationConfig-> isServingSubcell IE is set to false (configuration for non-serving subcell for FDD supercell), refer to ([11453916](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAajLvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

##### 5.3.5.4.7.4 Descrambling

**5.3.5.4.7.4.0-2**  (ID: `13373097`)

Descrambling
For PUCCH format3 5G-L1-UL shall execute de-scrambling of bit sequence to recover the original coded bits.

There are 2 parameters used for de-scrambling: UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->rnti and UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->dataScramblingInt.

For more details, please find section 2.4.4.11 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification and 3GPP TS 38.211 (v17.3.0): chapters 6.3.2.6.1

Also please find: ([11456360: Group and sequence hopping](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAmJU_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

Note:

1. For PUCCH format3 this requirement is not applicable when parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq-> PucchResourceAllocationConfig-> isServingSubcell IE is set to false (configuration for non-serving subcell for FDD supercell), refer to ([11453916](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAajLvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

#### 5.3.5.4.8 Decoding

##### 5.3.5.4.8.1 Overview

**5.3.5.4.8.1.0-3**  (ID: `12729132`)

Overview
For FR1-TDD and FR1-FDD for PUCCH format3 for each scheduled resource 5G-L1-UL shall decode UCI bits.

Upon reception of message UlData\_PucchReceiveReq ( [11513979: PUCCH Receive Request message](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MHvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)), when the parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->numOfBitsOfUciInformation > 0, 5G-L1-UL shall decode UCI bits in the indicated NR-slot and sent to 5G-L2-PS through UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs message.

The appropriate channel decoding method for each PUCCH signal shall depend on the field numOfBitsOfUciInformation as described in 38.212 §6.3.1.3, with numOfBitsOfUciInformation standing for the "Number of bits".

The UCI bits decoding for PUCCH format3 is described in section  2.4.4.12  of the 5Gmax algorithm specification.

Note:

1. For PUCCH format3 this requirement is not applicable when parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq-> PucchResourceAllocationConfig-> isServingSubcell IE is set to false (configuration for non-serving subcell for FDD supercell), refer to ([11453916](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAajLvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

##### 5.3.5.4.8.2 Reed-Muller Decoding

**5.3.5.4.8.2.0-2**  (ID: `13373099`)

Reed-Muller Decoding
For PUCCH format3 if there are less than 12 bits of uplink control information to be transferred (parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->numOfBitsOfUciInformation < 12) 5G-L1-UL shall use Reed-Muller code (channel coding for small blocks lengths) for decode.

The de-rate matching is applied before decoding.

No Cyclic Redundancy Check (CRC) bits are transmitted with data bits.

For more details, please find 3GPP TS 38.212 (v17.3.0): chapters 6.3.1.3, 6.3.1.4, 5.3, 5.4 and section  2.4.4.12  of the 5Gmax algorithm specification.

Note:

1. For PUCCH format3 this requirement is not applicable when parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq-> PucchResourceAllocationConfig-> isServingSubcell IE is set to false (configuration for non-serving subcell for FDD supercell), refer to ([11453916](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAajLvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

##### 5.3.5.4.8.3 Polar Decoding

**5.3.5.4.8.3.0-2**  (ID: `13373100`)

Polar Decoding
For PUCCH format3 if there are more than 11 bits of uplink control information to be transferred (parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->numOfBitsOfUciInformation > 11) 5G-L1-UL shall use Polar code for decoding.

Before decoding the de-rate matching is applied.

If there are between 12 and 19 bits of uplink control information, then 6 Cyclic Redundancy Check (CRC) bits are extracted.

If there are more than 19 bits of uplink control information then, 11 Cyclic Redundancy Check (CRC) bits are extracted.

For more details, please find 3GPP TS 38.212 (v17.3.0): chapters 6.3.1.3, 6.3.1.4, 5.3, 5.4 and section  2.4.4.12  of the 5Gmax algorithm specification.

Note:

1. For PUCCH format3 this requirement is not applicable when parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq-> PucchResourceAllocationConfig-> isServingSubcell IE is set to false (configuration for non-serving subcell for FDD supercell), refer to ([11453916](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAajLvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

##### 5.3.5.4.8.4 Cyclic Redundancy Check

**5.3.5.4.8.4.0-3**  (ID: `12729384`)

Cyclic Redundancy Check
For FR1-TDD and FR1-FDD for PUCCH format3 for each control data received on PUCCH, when the parameter  UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->numOfBitsOfUciInformation ≥ 12 bits, 5G-L1-UL shall perform error detection using Cyclic Redundancy Check ([CRC](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_LDSGd3IIEfCRE7eh4Ndkrw)) bits.

The CRC sequence is transmitted with UCI payload and its bitwidth is 6 bits for UCI payload in range [12 ..19] bits and it is 11 bits for UCI payload >19 bits.

For each control data received on PUCCH,

* when UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->numOfBitsOfUciInformation ≥ 12 bits, 5G-L1-UL shall report CRC to 5G-L2-PS within parameters: UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->crc  and UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->crc
* when UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->numOfBitsOfUciInformation ≤11 bits, the default value 0(OK) is filled in the parameters UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->crc  and UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->crc but it would be ignored by L2-PS.

Note:

1. For PUCCH format3 this requirement is not applicable when parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq-> PucchResourceAllocationConfig-> isServingSubcell IE is set to false (configuration for non-serving subcell for FDD supercell), refer to ([11453916](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAajLvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
2. For reference for L1L2 PUCCH messages see: ([11453583](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAZVA_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))
3. CRC bits and UCI payload bits are together coded with Polar code.

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

##### 5.3.5.4.8.5 Decoding results

**5.3.5.4.8.5.0-3**  (ID: `12729155`)

Decoding results
For FR1-TDD and FR1-FDD for PUCCH format3 5G-L1-UL shall report the decoded UCI bits.

All necessary information to decode each signal received on PUCCH (i.e., scheduled resource, number of UCI bits, etc.) are got from the UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message ([11513990](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MIfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For each decoded data on PUCCH format3 (whatever the DTX decision: 'DTX' or 'nonDTX'), 5G-L1-UL shall provide to 5G-L2-PS the respective information in different messages described in ([11513958](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MGfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) as follows:

* The decoded UCI bits: the numOfBitsOfUciInformation UCI bits shall be reported in the field uciBits of the UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs message.
* The decoded HARQ-ACK bits: 5G-L1-UL shall report the first nANPucch decoded bits (among all the decoded UCI bits) in the UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD message, with nANPucch standing for the number of HARQ-ACK bits which is got from message UlData\_PucchReceiveReq. Note that the first HARQ-ACK bit corresponds to the MSB of the decoded sequence of bits.
* The decoded SR bit: SR bit is multiplexed with the CSI report bits and/or HARQ-ACK bits. 5G-L1-UL decodes the numOfBitsOfUciInformation number of UCI bits and passes them transparently as bit string to L2-PS in UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs . Whether SR is transmitted via  PUCCH format3 or not is transparent to 5G-L1-UL.

Note:

1. For PUCCH format3 this requirement is not applicable when parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq-> PucchResourceAllocationConfig-> isServingSubcell IE is set to false (configuration for non-serving subcell for FDD supercell), refer to ([11453916](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAajLvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

#### 5.3.5.4.9 DTX Detection

##### 5.3.5.4.9.1 General

**5.3.5.4.9.1.0-3**  (ID: `12723238`)

General
For FR1-TDD and FR1-FDD for PUCCH format3 5G-L1-UL shall use DTX metric to indicate whether an PUCCH signal was transmitted and received as expected.

The UCI block error probability shall be lower than 1% to meet 3GPP minimum requirements in TS 38.104

The DTX detection methods, metrics and thresholds for PUCCH format3 are described in section  2.4.4.13  of the 5Gmax algorithm specification.

The two terms used for PUCCH DTX decision (i.e. the metric and the threshold in the fixed-point representation) as well as the decision (i.e. DTX or nonDTX) should then be provided to 5G-L2-PS via parameters:

* UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->dtxMetric  
  and (when value of parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources-> nANPucch > 0) via:  
  UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->dtxMetric
* UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->dtxThreshold  
  and (when value of parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources-> nANPucch > 0) via:  
  UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->dtxThreshold

The results of DTX detection are sent to 5G-L2-PS via parameters:

* UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->dtx  
  and (when value of parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources-> nANPucch > 0) via:  
  UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->dtx
* UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->crc  
  and (when value of parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources-> nANPucch > 0) via:  
  UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->crc

Supported DTX detection methods and thresholds for PUCCH format3 for following L1 variants:

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | Technology | iFFTbased | DecodingBased | First Feature |
| L1 HW | Loner | supported | not supported | Legacy |
| Loki | supported | supported | CB007950 |  |
| Thor | supported | supported | CB007487 |  |
| Odin | [CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] Supported for  FR1-TDD eCPRI-7.2a / FR1-TDD eCPRI-7.2e [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] [CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] FR1-FDD CPRI / FR1-FDD eCPRI-7.2a [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] |  | CB012115 |  |

Note:

1. 5G-L2-PS could use the DTX indication to filter reliable measurements performed on PUCCH (e.g. TO), to handle DL retransmission, etc.
2. The false alarm is defined as the probability to detect UCI reporting whereas nothing was sent on PUCCH

3. For PUCCH format3 this requirement is not applicable when parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq-> PucchResourceAllocationConfig-> isServingSubcell IE is set to false (configuration for non-serving subcell for FDD supercell), refer to ([11453916](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAajLvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

##### 5.3.5.4.9.2 DTX metric computation method selection algorithm

###### 5.3.5.4.9.2.0-5 DTX metric computation method selection algorithm 12723242: DTX metric computation method selection algorithm For PUCCH Format 3, the DTX detection follows below procedures: If 3 bits &lt;= numOfBitsOfciInformation &lt;=19 bits If actPucchF3MethodDtx is true 'decoding based' method is selected Else If actPucchF3MethodDtx is false 'ifftbased' method is selected Else if numOfBitsOfciInformation  &gt; 19 bits If CRC is OK DTX = 0 Else if CRC is NOK 'ifftbased' method is selected. Note: 1. numOfBitsOfciInformation is given in UlData_PucchReceiveReq. See 5G_L1_IF_219_replaced( 11514147 ). 2. actPucchF3MethodDtx is given in UlCell_SetupReq. See 5G_L1_IF_152_replaced( 11513449 ). 3. Refer to 5GMax algorithm specification chapter 2.4.4.13 for details on 'decoding based' and 'ifftbased' methods. 4. 8Rx receiver is applicable to C8, C8'2, C8'4, C8'8 and A8 subcell on Thor [CB012115-GA] and to C8'2 and C8'4 subcell on Odin [End CB012115-GA]. All receiver modes for PUCCH format3 are specified in: 12576677 5.  For 8Rx, 5G-L1-UL shall also select the DTX detection method depending on actPucchF3MethodDtx, as simulation [image-0][image_desc]The image is a blurry, low-resolution icon that appears to represent a Microsoft PowerPoint file. The icon is primarily white with an orange overlay on the left side. The orange overlay has a stylized "P" in white. To the right of the "P", there is a faint, blurry orange shape that resembles a slide or a document. The overall impression is that of a file icon, likely for a presentation.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_pukkola_5G_L1_Entity_Level_file_6684.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] performance evaluation of NR PUCCH F3 DTX detection.pptx shows that 'decoding based' method performs worse than 'ifftbased' method if PUCCH F3 additional DMRS symbol is configured. [CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA ] The requirement is also applicable for 'ifftbased' method (actPucchF3MethodDtx is false) for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a for 2RX and 4RX  [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] [CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for 'ifftbased' method (actPucchF3MethodDtx is false) for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] (ID: 12723242)

##### 5.3.5.4.9.3 DTX decoding method "ifftbased"

**5.3.5.4.9.3.0-3**  (ID: `12723250`)

DTX decoding method "ifftbased"
For FR1-TDD and FR1-FDD 5G-L1-UL for PUCCH format3 shall use threshold for DTX decision for ifftbased method.

Depending on the number of scheduled RBs and the number of OFDM symbols dedicated to DMRS, 5G-L1-UL shall select the appropriate threshold for DTX decision. This selection shall be performed for each NR-slot where resources are scheduled for PUCCH transmission.

5G-L1-UL shall infer the number of OFDM symbols dedicated to DMRS from the parameters:

UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->numOfSymbols

UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->additionalDmrs

UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->frequencyHopping

UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->numCeAxCIndex

UlCell\_SetupReq->ulSubcellType

5G-L1-UL shall get information about number of RBs from parameter:

UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->numOfPrb

The corresponding values of threshold are defined internally in L1 software code as defined in section 2.4.4.13 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification in form of table.

For more than 2Rx antenna configuration, the thresholds of 2 antennas are multiplied by related factors as specified in 5GMAX algorithm spec chapter 2.4.4.13.

Then, 5G-L1-UL shall use the DTX metric value ( [12819680: DTX Metric](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_UX7msKk0EfCrANRYxAlR5A?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) to compare with dtxThreshold .

Note:

1. The DTX indication shall be provided to 5G-L2-PS as described in ([12721868](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_mXk1EW2JEfCmnYHxzZN44w?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).

2. For PUCCH format3 this requirement is not applicable when parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq-> PucchResourceAllocationConfig-> isServingSubcell IE is set to false (configuration for non-serving subcell for FDD supercell), refer to ([11453916](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAajLvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

##### 5.3.5.4.9.4 DTX decoding method "DecodingBased"

**5.3.5.4.9.4.0-1**  (ID: `12819798`)

DTX decoding method "DecodingBased"
For FR1-TDD and FR1-FDD 5G-L1-UL for PUCCH format3 shall use threshold for DTX decision for "DecodingBased" method.

Depending on the number of UCI bits, number of softbits (LLR), number of "RX streams" and coding method (Reed-Muller, Polar), 5G-L1-UL shall select the appropriate threshold for DTX decision. This selection shall be performed for each NR-slot where resources are scheduled for PUCCH transmission.

5G-L1-UL shall get information about number of UCI bits from parameter:

UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->numOfBitsOfUciInformation

5G-L1-UL shall infer the number of softbits (LLR) bits from the parameters:

UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->numOfSymbols

UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->additionalDmrs

UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->frequencyHopping

UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->numOfPrb

UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->modulationType

UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->numCeAxCIndex

UlCell\_SetupReq->ulSubcellType

The thresholds and formulas for DTX decision are specified in  5GMAX algorithm spec chapter 2.4.4.13.

The corresponding values of threshold are defined internally in L1 software code in form of tables.

For DTX metric evaluation please find: ([12819680: DTX Metric](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_UX7msKk0EfCrANRYxAlR5A?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

Note:

1. The DTX indication shall be provided to 5G-L2-PS as described in ([12721868](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_mXk1EW2JEfCmnYHxzZN44w?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).

2. For PUCCH format3 this requirement is not applicable when parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq-> PucchResourceAllocationConfig-> isServingSubcell IE is set to false (configuration for non-serving subcell for FDD supercell), refer to ([11453916](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAajLvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

##### 5.3.5.4.9.5 DTX decoding method "PmMinBased"

**5.3.5.4.9.5.0-1**  (ID: `13478556`)

DTX decoding method "PmMinBased"
For PUCCH format3 5G-L1-UL shall use polar decoder metrics for DTX decision for  'PmiMinBased' method.

The 'PmMinBased' method does not use a thresholds. Its decision logic involves comparing path metrics from the polar decoder in conjunction with the Cyclic Redundancy Check (CRC) result.

For dtx detection, three values of two DTX metrics (PMdecoded, PMall(1) and PMall(1)) are use and compared together with CRC result:

* If CRC result is OK and PMdecoded is the only minimum value of PMall (that is when PMdecoded equals to PMall(1) and PMall(1) is unequal to PMall(2)) then decision is NON\_DTX (PUCCH transmission is detected).
* Otherwise, decision is DTX.

Here:

* PMdecoded is the path metric of the decoded codeword (one integer).
* PMall is the path metric of all the paths in the list in ascending order (list of 16 integers, as the number of path is limited to 16).
* CRC - result of Cyclic Redundancy Check (based on CRC bits transmitted with UCI  payload)

Additional used two values of metrics are send to 5G-L2-PS via parameters:

* PMdecoded via parameterUlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->dtxMetric  
  and (when value of parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources-> nANPucch > 0) via:  
  UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->dtxMetric
* PMall(1) via parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->dtxThreshold  
  and (when value of parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources-> nANPucch > 0) via:  
  UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->dtxThreshold

The "PmMinBased" algorithm, as described in section 2.4.4.13 5GMAX algorithm specification

Note:

1. This method is part of an enhanced DTX detection scheme for PUCCH format3 (for UCI payload in range [12..19] bits), which is activated when the parameter NRBTS/NRCELL/actPucchF3EnhanceDTX is set to true and additional DMRS are configured. Unlike other methods such as 'iFFTbased' or 'DecodingBased' which compare a calculated metric against a pre-defined threshold, the PmMinBased method does not use. Its decision logic involves comparing path metrics from the decoder (PMdecoded, PMall(1), PMall(2)) in conjunction with the Cyclic Redundancy Check (CRC) result. The 'PmMinBased' decision relies on determining whether the path metric of the decoded UCI is the unique minimum among all possible path metrics (PMall). The first two values in the sorted list of all path metrics are PMall(1) and PMall(2).

1. The DTX indication shall be provided to 5G-L2-PS as described in ([12721868](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_mXk1EW2JEfCmnYHxzZN44w?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).

3. For PUCCH format3 this requirement is not applicable when parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq-> PucchResourceAllocationConfig-> isServingSubcell IE is set to false (configuration for non-serving subcell for FDD supercell), refer to ([11453916](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAajLvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

##### 5.3.5.4.9.6 Frozen Requirements

###### 5.3.5.4.9.6.1 FR1-FDD

**5.3.5.4.9.6.1.0-1**  (ID: `11458787`)

FR1-FDD
FDD FR1 L1 Loner: Depending on the number of scheduled RBs and the number of OFDM symbols dedicated to DMRS, 5G-L1-UL shall select the appropriate threshold for DTX decision. This selection shall be performed for each NR-slot where resources are scheduled for PUCCH transmission.

5G-L1-UL gets the parameter numOfRBs from the UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message. The number of OFDM symbols dedicated to DMRS can be infered from the parameters numOfSymbols and  additionalDmrs from the UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message.

[5GC000885-F] FDD FR1 L1 Loner: The number of OFDM symbols dedicated to DMRS is related to frequencyHopping  of lData\_PucchReceiveReq, too.[End 5GC000885-F]

PUCCH format 3 is supported for 3 to 50 bits and a variable number if RBs in the range [1..16], excluding 7, 11, 13 and 14 RBs.

The corresponding thresholds are given in the R&D parameter rdPucchF3ThresholdsxDmrsSymb, where x can take values in {1, 2, 4} (see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_1482 5G\_L1\_3370 5G\_L1\_8525\_replaced([11452972](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAWRt_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_1483 5G\_L1\_3371 5G\_L1\_8526\_replaced([11452990](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAWRufvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_1484 5G\_L1\_3372 5G\_L1\_8527\_replaced([11453004](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAWRu_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for 2 Rx. These R&D parameters are arrays of length 12. They can be read as:

dtxThreshold = rdPucchF3ThresholdsxDmrsSymb [numOfRBs-1] for numOfRBs in [1..6]

dtxThreshold = rdPucchF3ThresholdsxDmrsSymb [numOfRBs-2] for numOfRBs in [8..10]

dtxThreshold = rdPucchF3ThresholdsxDmrsSymb [numOfRBs-3] for numOfRBs =12

dtxThreshold = rdPucchF3ThresholdsxDmrsSymb [numOfRBs-5] for numOfRBs in [15,16]

for  more than 2Rx antenna configuration, the applied dtxThreshold  values are the thresholds of 2 antennas multiplied by related factors in  5GMAX algorithm spec chapter 2.4.4.13.

Then, 5G-L1-UL shall use the DTX metric value (see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_1427 5G\_L1\_8355\_replaced([11457966](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAuFJvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to compare with dtxThreshold . The DTX indication shall be provided to 5G-L2-PS as described in 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_1427 5G\_L1\_8356\_replaced([11458713](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAxIefvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[5GC002481-AA] For FDD and L1 Loki HW, the above description shall be also supported. [End 5GC002481-AA]

[RP003187-M] The requirement is also applicable for L1 Thor for FR1-FDD-CPRI. [End RP003187-M]

[Before-CNI-122313-A]

[CB009444-I] This requirement is applicable in RINLINE1 HW for FR1-FDD-eCPRI. [End CB009444-I]

[CNI-122313-A]

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

[End CNI-122313-A]

---

###### 5.3.5.4.9.6.2 General

###### 5.3.5.4.9.6.2.0-1 General Loner and  Loki (ID: 11458706)

**5.3.5.4.9.6.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11458713`)

General
There should be a metric in 5G-L1-UL that indicates whether an PUCCH signal was transmitted and received as expected. The false alarm target for this metric is set to 1%, where the false alarm is defined as the probability to detect UCI reporting whereas nothing was sent on PUCCH. Thus, the HARQ-ACK false alarm target is 0.5%.

The two terms used for PUCCH DTX decision (i.e. the metric and the threshold in the fixed point representation) as well as the decision (i.e. DTX or nonDTX) should then be provided to 5G-L2-PS in the messages UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs and UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD.  5G-L2-PS could use the DTX indication to filter reliable measurements performed on PUCCH (e.g. TO), to handle DL retransmission, etc.

The PUCCH DTX detection algorithm is described in:

- For PUCCH Format 0: section 2.4.1.6 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification v5.3  (see 5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

- For PUCCH Format 2: section 2.4.3.10 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification (see 5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

- [5GC000885-A] FDD FR1 L1 Loner: for PUCCH Format 1:MLD detection method is chosen based on section 2.4.2.8 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification (see 5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). For PUCCH Format 3: section 2.4.4.13 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification (see 5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). [End 5GC000885-A]

- [CB006064-A] TDD FR1 L1 Loner/Loki: for PUCCH Format 1:MLD detection method is chosen based on section 2.4.2.8 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification (see 5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). For PUCCH Format 3: section 2.4.4.13 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification (see 5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).[End CB006064-A]

[5GC001868-A] 5G-L1-UL shall also compute PUCCH DTX metric for format 0 format 2 and report this metric to 5G-L2-PS as above in Loki L1 HW. [End 5GC001868-A]

---

###### 5.3.5.4.9.6.2.0-2 General Thor (ID: 11458719)

**5.3.5.4.9.6.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11458726`)

General
For Thor:

There should be a metric in 5G-L1-UL that indicates whether an PUCCH signal was transmitted and received as expected. The false alarm target for this metric is set to 1%, where the false alarm is defined as the probability to detect UCI reporting whereas nothing was sent on PUCCH. Thus, the HARQ-ACK false alarm target is 0.5%.

The two terms used for PUCCH DTX decision (i.e. the metric and the threshold in the fixed point representation) as well as the decision (i.e. DTX or nonDTX) should then be provided to 5G-L2-PS in the messages UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs and UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD.  5G-L2-PS could use the DTX indication to filter reliable measurements performed on PUCCH (e.g. TO), to handle DL retransmission, etc.

The PUCCH DTX detection algorithm is described in:

- FDD FR1 L1: for PUCCH Format 1:MLD detection method is chosen based on section 2.4.2.8 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification (see 5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). For PUCCH Format 3: section 2.4.4.13 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification (see 5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

- TDD FR1 L1: for PUCCH Format 1:MLD detection method is chosen based on section 2.4.2.8 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification (see 5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). For PUCCH Format 3: section 2.4.4.13 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification (see 5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[RP003187-F] In terms of TDD FR1 PUCCH Formats 1 and 3 the requirement is also applicable for L1 Thor for FR1-TDD-eCPRI.

L1 Thor does not support short PUCCH formats.

[End RP003187-F]

[End CNI-122313-A]

#### 5.3.5.4.10 Receive Response and HARQ report preparation

##### 5.3.5.4.10.1 UCI and measurements report

**5.3.5.4.10.1.0-2**  (ID: `13373105`)

UCI and measurements report
For FR1-TDD and FR1-FDD for PUCCH format3 for each scheduled resource after decoding control data received on PUCCH and estimating measurements 5G-L1-UL shall returns the UCI bits and a set of measurement metrics to the L2-PS via the message UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs.

Following L1L2 [IF](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_eam28HJJEfCRE7eh4Ndkrw) parameters 5G-L1-UL shall use to report UCI bits, measurements, DTX state, DTX metrics, DTX thresholds and CRC state:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs |  |
| Report / Measurement | L1L2 IF Parameter |
| UCI bits | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->uciBits |
| SR bit | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->srBit |
| DTX state | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->dtx |
| DTX metric | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->dtxMetric |
| DTX threshold | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->dtxThreshold |
| CRC state | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->crc |
| Noise Power per PRB(5) | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->noisePerPrb |
| ST TA metric | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->shortTermTaMetric |
| ST TA peak amplitude | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->shortTermTaPeakAmp |
| Noise Power | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->noisePower |
| Received Power | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->rxPower |
| RSSI | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->rssi |
| SINR | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->sinr |
| ST FO metric(5) | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->shortTermCfoMetric |
| antenna-wise  ST FO(5) | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs->Subcells->PucchResources->extendedParameters->shortTermCfoMetricOfAnt |

Note:

1. For detailed L1L2 IF specification please find: ([11513962](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MGvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) and ([11514171](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR1aQ_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))
2. The endpoint address for UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs is defined via parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->addrPucchReceiveRespPs
3. For PUCCH format3 when the parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->isServingSubcell equals "false", PUCCH processing is reduced to Noise Power, Received Power and SINR measurements. For details see: ([11454738](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAe0nPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)), ([11454248](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAcYWvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) and ([11514171](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR1aQ_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))
4. In specific configuration parameters in above table 5G-L1-UL shall set to "invalid values". For details see: ([11454049](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAbxQPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) and ([11514171](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR1aQ_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))
5. For Loner these parameters are not estimated. For details see ([11514171](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR1aQ_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

##### 5.3.5.4.10.2 HARQ report

###### 5.3.5.4.10.2.1 Loki / Thor / Odin

**5.3.5.4.10.2.1.0-2**  (ID: `12729728`)

Loki / Thor / Odin
For FR1-TDD and FR1-FDD for PUCCH format3 when parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->nANPucch is not equal "0", 5G-L1-UL shall send HARQ feedback and set of DTX data (DTX state, CRC state, DTX metric and its threshold) to the 5G-L2-PS via the message UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD.

Following L1L2 [IF](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_eam28HJJEfCRE7eh4Ndkrw) parameters 5G-L1-UL shall use to report HARQ feedback, CRC state, DTX state, DTX metric and its threshold:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD |  |
| Report / Measurement | L1L2 IF Parameter |
| AN bits | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->ackNack |
| DTX state | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->dtx |
| DTX metric | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->dtxMetric |
| DTX threshold | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->dtxThreshold |
| SR bit(5)(6) | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->srBit |
| CRC state | UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD->Subcells->PucchResources->crc |

Note:

1. For detailed L1L2 IF specification please find: ([11513962](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MGvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) and ([11514243](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BT_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))
2. The endpoint address for UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs is defined via parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->addrPucchReceiveRespHarqD
3. For PUCCH format3 when the parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->isServingSubcell equals "false", PUCCH processing is reduced to Noise Power, Received Power and SINR measurements. For details see: ([11454738](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAe0nPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)), ([11454248](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAcYWvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) and ([11514243](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BT_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))
4. In specific configuration parameters in above table 5G-L1-UL shall set to "invalid values". For details see: ([11454049](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAbxQPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) and ([11514243](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BT_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))
5. For specification of setting of parameter srBit see: ([11453947: Parameter srBit](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAbKM_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))   
   6. Parameter srBit is not supported in message UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqDLoner (for Loner).

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

Loner
For FR1-TDD and FR1-FDD for PUCCH format3 when parameter UlData\_PucchReceiveReq->Subcells->PucchResources->nANPucch is not equal "0", 5G-L1-UL shall send HARQ feedback and set of DTX data (DTX state, CRC state, DTX metric and its threshold) to the 5G-L2-PS via the message UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD.

##### 5.3.5.4.10.3 Frozen Requiremets

###### 5.3.5.4.10.3.1 Parameters for Harq and DTX feedback.

###### 5.3.5.4.10.3.1.0-1 Parameters for Harq and DTX feedback. Loner and Loki (ID: 11454305)

**5.3.5.4.10.3.1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11454311`)

Parameters for Harq and DTX feedback.
HARQ feedback and set of DTX data (DTX state, DTX metric and its threshold)are sent to the 5G-L2-PS entity to inform about the AN status reported by the UEs. The UlData\_PucchReceiveReq (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_216\_replaced([11513990](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MIfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L1\_IF\_219\_replaced([11514147](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR1aPvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), original location: 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_215) message informs (via nANPucch) the 5G-L1-UL about the presence of AN bits in the given PUCCH resource to be processed. If nANPucch is not zero the decoder/detector of 5G-L1-UL shall extract the AN bits after UCI decoding/detection  and sent the information (ackNack) to 5G-L2-PS via UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarq (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_224\_replaced([11514255](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BUvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), original location: 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_223). Due to timing constraints, UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD message is sent to 5G-L2-PS by L1-FPGA directly. The endpoint address for this message is defined in the UlData\_PucchReceiveReq (IE addrPucchReceiveRespHarqD) message.

**[Before-CNI-122313-A]**

**[CB009444-I] This requirement is applicable for RINLINE1 for FR1-FDD-eCPRI.** [End CB009444-I]\*\*\*\*

**[CNI-122313-A]**

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

**[End CNI-122313-A]**

**[CB009543-B]In case of FDD supercell this requirement is applicable only for serving subcell and PUCCH F3 resource allocation; i.e for such PUCCH resource, UlData\_PucchReceiveReq > PucchResourceAllocationConfig > isServingSubcell IE is set to true, refer to 5G\_L1\_18207\_replaced([11453923](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAbKMPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))**[End CB009543-B]\*\*\*\*

---

###### 5.3.5.4.10.3.1.0-2 Parameters for Harq and DTX feedback. For Thor (ID: 11454320)

**5.3.5.4.10.3.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11454327`)

Parameters for Harq and DTX feedback.
HARQ feedback and set of DTX data (DTX state, DTX metric and its threshold)are sent to the 5G-L2-PS entity to inform about the AN status reported by the UEs. The UlData\_PucchReceiveReq (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_216\_replaced([11513990](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MIfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L1\_IF\_219\_replaced([11514147](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR1aPvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), original location: 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_215) message informs (via nANPucch) the 5G-L1-UL about the presence of AN bits in the given PUCCH resource to be processed. If nANPucch is not zero the decoder/detector of 5G-L1-UL shall extract the AN bits after UCI decoding/detection  and sent the information (ackNack) to 5G-L2-PS via UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarq (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_224\_replaced([11514255](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BUvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), original location: 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_223). The endpoint address for this message is defined in the UlData\_PucchReceiveReq (IE addrPucchReceiveRespHarqD) message.

**[RP003187-A, RP003187-H] This requirement is supported in L1** Thor **[End RP003187-A, RP003187-H]**\*\*\*\*

**[CB010575-A] The requirement is also applicable for L1** Thor for FR1-TDD-CPRI **[End CB010575-A]**\*\*\*\*

**[CB011178-A] The requirement is also applicable for L1** Thor for FR1-FDD-7-2a-eCPRI **[End CB011178-A]**\*\*\*\*

**[CB009543-B]In case of FDD supercell this requirement is applicable only for serving subcell and PUCCH F3 resource allocation; i.e for such PUCCH resource, UlData\_PucchReceiveReq > PucchResourceAllocationConfig > isServingSubcell IE is set to true, refer to 5G\_L1\_18207\_replaced([11453923](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAbKMPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))**[End CB009543-B]\*\*\*\*

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
|  | **Thor** |
| **FR1-FDD-CPRI** | Supported |
| **FR1-FDD-7-2a-eCPRI** | **[CB011178-A] Supported** [End CB011178-A]\*\*\*\* |
| **FR1-FDD-OBSAI** | **[CB010969-SR-CB] Supported** [End CB010969-SR-CB]\*\*\*\* |
| **FR1-TDD-CPRI** | **[CB010575-A] Supported** [End CB010575-A]\*\*\*\* |

###### 5.3.5.4.10.3.2 Harq reporting

**5.3.5.4.10.3.2.0-1**  (ID: `11454287`)

Harq reporting
**AN reporting**

Upon reception of message *UlData\_PucchReceiveReq, indicating* nANPucch >0, HARQ-ACK bits shall be decoded in the indicated NR-slot and sent to 5G-L2-PS through *UlData\_ PucchReceiveRespHarqD message.*\*\*

**[Before 5GC001982-A]According the value of the IE *pucchFormat received in UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message, 5G-L1-UL shall proceed as follows:***

* If *pucchFormat equals to 0, then 5G-L1-UL shall always send the message* UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD to 5G-L2-PS whatever the value of the IE *nANPucch in UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message*\*\*
* If *pucchFormat equals to 2, then 5G-L1-UL shall send the message* UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD to 5G-L2-PS, only when the value of the IE *nANPucch > 0 in UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message* *[End 5GC001982-A]*\*\*\*\*

**[5GC001982-A] 5G-L1-UL shall send the message *UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD to 5G-L2-PS, only when the value of the IE *nANPucch > 0 in UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message.*\*[End 5GC001982-A]***\*\*\*

**[5GC001868-A] 5G-L1-UL shall also behave as above for HARQ-ACK decoding on PUCCH in Loki L1 HW** [End 5GC001868-A]\*\*\*\*

**[CB007814-G] This requirement also applies to ABIO FR1-FDD-eCPRI.** [End CB007814-G]\*\*\*\*

**[RP003187-A, RP003187-H] 5G-L1-UL shall also behave as above for HARQ-ACK decoding on PUCCH in L1** Thor **[End RP003187-A, RP003187-H]**\*\*\*\*

**[CB008205-B] 5G-L1-UL shall also support requirements above in ABIO for O-RAN compliant FR1 FDD eCPRI.**[End CB008205-B]\*\*\*\*

**[Before-CNI-122313-A]**

**[CB009443-C] This requirement shall be supported in RINLINE1 HW for FR1-TDD-eCPRI.**[End CB009443-C]\*\*\*\*

**[CNI-122313-A]**

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

**[End CNI-122313-A]**

**[CB010575-A] 5G-L1-UL shall behave as above for HARQ-ACK decoding on PUCCH in L1** Thor for **FR1 TDD CPRI** [End CB010575-A]***\****\*

**[CB007595-B] The requirement is also applicable for L1** Thor for FR1-TDD-7-2e-eCPRI **[End CB007595-B]**\*\*\*\*

**[CB010969-SR-CB] This requirement shall be supported by L1 Thor in FR1-FDD-OBSAI.** [End CB010969-SR-CB]\*\*\*\*

**[CB009543-B]In case of FDD supercell this requirement is applicable only for serving subcell and PUCCH F3 resource allocation; i.e for such PUCCH resource, UlData\_PucchReceiveReq > PucchResourceAllocationConfig > isServingSubcell IE is set to true, refer to 5G\_L1\_18207\_replaced([11453923](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAbKMPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))**[End CB009543-B]\*\*\*\*

## 5.3.6 Timing requirements

### 5.3.6.1 Timing requirements location

#### 5.3.6.1.0-1 Timing requirements location PUCCH timing requirements for L1-L2 interface are specified in the 5G L1 Interface module, chapter 3.2.6 (see: 11514719: Timing for UL L1-L2 IF ) (ID: 13358791)

## 5.3.7 PUCCH capacity

### 5.3.7.1 Overview

**5.3.7.1.0-3**  (ID: `13392353`)

Overview
In this section, PUCCH capacity stands for the maximum number of PUCCH resources which are multiplexed in either time and/or frequency domain per slot. The capacity is given for each PUCCH format, in particular format0, format1, format2 and format3.

The PUCCH capacity numbers in this section refer to real-time processing capacity. The supported configurations are given in the following.

The capacity per L1 instance and/or per L1 pool  refers to the maximum number of resources and it is shared between the different subcells associated to this L1 instance  and/or L1 pool . This capacity is independent from the number of subcells/L1 instance or L1 pool.

For definition of L1 instance please see: ([11381159](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uerB6fvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and ([11381988](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uevTXfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) .

For definition of L1 pool and number of L1 pools per L1 instance, please see: ([11382080](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uev6afvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), ([11382811](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uey9u_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), ([11384438](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ue5EWfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), ([11385930](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufAZEvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and ([11381988](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uevTXfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) .

For TDD FR1 and FDD, when BB pooling enabled, the supported PUCCH capacity for different L1 deployment variants refer to ([11374026](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueFzFPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) for the Format1 and Format3 for HARQ A/N.

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

### 5.3.7.2 PUCCH capacity numbers

#### 5.3.7.2.1 Loner

**5.3.7.2.1.0-1**  (ID: `11458968`)

Loner
For **L1 Loner HW, the PUCCH capacity numbers for each format in real-time processing are specified in the table below:**

**For TDD FR1,**

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **PUCCH****Format**\*\*\*\* | **Number of resources per L1 instance****(and per subcell, optional)****per slot*****\****\* |
| **Format 0** | Up to 16 per L1 instance. (NOTE: Distribution of UEs between subcells is specified in ([11397587](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uf3UsvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). |
| **Format 1** | **[CB006064-A]** Up to 128 per L1 Loner instance for 2 spatial streams Up to 96 per L1 Loner instance for 4 spatial streams **[End CB006064-A]** |
| **Format 2** | Up to 16 per L1 instance in the case when PUCCH is used for transmission of UCI of the length <=11 bits (coded with use of Reed-Muller code). Up to 8 per L1 instance in the case when PUCCH is used for transmission of UCI of the length >=12 bits (coded with use of  Polar code). (NOTE: Distribution of UEs between subcells is specified in ([11397587](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uf3UsvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). |
| **Format 3** | **[CB006064-A]** Up to 48 (RM or Polar) per L1 Loner instance for 2 spatial streams Up to 36 (RM or Polar) per L1 Loner instance for 4 spatial streams **[End CB006064-A]** |

**For TDD FR2,**

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **PUCCH****Format**\*\*\*\* | **Number of resources per L1 instance****(and per subcell, optional)****per slot*****\****\* |
| **Format 0** | Up to 4 per L1 instance (Up to 2 per subcell) Note: resources on different symbols |
| **Format 1** | - |
| **Format 2** | Up to 4 per L1 instance (Up to 2 per subcell) Note: resources on different symbols |
| **Format 3** | - |

**For FDD FR1,**

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **PUCCH****Format**\*\*\*\* | **Number of resources per L1 instance****(and per subcell, optional)****per slot*****\****\* |
| **Format 0** | Up to 12 per L1 instance. |
| **Format 1** | Up to 84 per L1 Loner instance   **[Before CB006667-B]** Note: from end to end perspective, up to 48 PUCCH F1 resources are supported **[End CB006667-B]** |
| **Format 2** | Up to 12 per L1 instance in the case when PUCCH is used for transmission of UCI of the length <=11 bits (coded with use of Reed-Muller code). Up to 8 per L1 instance in the case when PUCCH is used for transmission of UCI of the length >=12 bits (coded with use of  Polar code). |
| **Format 3** | Up to 44 per L1 Loner instance   **[Before CB006667-B]** Note: from end to end perspective, up to 21 PUCCH F3 resources are supported **[End CB006667-B]** |

**Note:**

The short PUCCH resources can be located either in symbol#12 and #13.

The long PUCCH and short PUCCH can’t co-exist.

The Loner hardware has a message size limit of 12800 bytes including 8 bytes EM (event machine) header and thus this places a constraint on the number of PUCCH resources that can be supported in a single UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message.

**[Before PR696174]**

In 5G21A and up to 22R3, at most 126 resources can be supported. From 22R4 to 23R1, at most 127 resources can be supported. In 23R2, at most 126 resources can be supported.

The resources can be shared freely between both formats (F1 and F3) while not exceeding the per format capacity described in the tables above.

**[PR696174]**

In 23R3, up to 131 resources are supported for F1+F3. Resources can be shared freely between the formats while not exceeding the per format capacity described in the tables above.

**[End PR696174]**

---

#### 5.3.7.2.2 Loki

##### 5.3.7.2.2.1 FR1 TDD

**5.3.7.2.2.1.0-5**  (ID: `12490749`)

FR1 TDD
For **L1 Loki HW and TDD FR1, the PUCCH capacity numbers for each format in real-time processing are specified in** 5G\_UP\_3249. Please note that **CB007950-A has introduced the long PUCCH for TDD FR1 Loki.**\*\*\*\*

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **PUCCH****Format**\*\*\*\* | **Number of resources per L1 instance****(and per subcell, optional)****per slot*****\****\* | **First Feature** |
| **Format 0** | Up to 33 PUCCH F0 resources per L1 Loki instance. **Note: From end to end and L2-PS perspectives, 18 F0 resources are needed per L1 Loki instance.** |  |
| **Format 1** | Up to [Before CB014386-A] 216 [CB014386-A] 312 [End CB014386-A] resources per L1 Loki instance :  up to 62 resources per cell per slot for the case of up to 3 cells per L1 Loki instance  When UE pooling is active(5G\_UP\_1772), up to [Before CB014386-A] 112 [CB014386-A] 136 [End CB014386-A] resources can be supported in one cell per slot.   Up to [Before CB014386-A] 72 [CB014386-A] 104 [End CB014386-A] resources per L1 Loki instance and per cell per slot in case of 6 consecutive UL slots are configured, see Note 1. | **CB007950-A** |
| **Format 2** | Up to 18 PUCCH F2 resources per L1 Loki instance (RM or Polar) for BF/non-BF case.   **Note: For UCI length <=11 bits or >= 12 bits, the Reed-Muller code or Polar code is used, respectively.** |  |
| **Format 3** | Up to **71 resources (RM or Polar)  per L1 Loki instance :**  up to 22 resources (RM or Polar)  per cell per slot for the case of up to 3 cells per L1 Loki instance when UE pooling is deactive  When UE pooling is active(5G\_UP\_1772), up to **40** resources can be supported in one cell per slot.\*\*\*\*   Up to 23 resources per L1 Loki instance and per cell per slot in case of 6 consecutive UL slots are configured, see Note 1. | **CB007950-A** |

PUCCH F3 resources are shared between HARQ-AN and pCSI per cell/slot. More details about the number of HARQ-AN resources on F1/F3 per cell/slot are in 5G\_RAN\_CP\_12356511.

**Note:**

The short PUCCH resources can be located either in symbol#12 and #13.

The long PUCCH and short PUCCH can’t co-exist.

**Note 1: When MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/tddFrameStructure.frameStructureType = tdLte and MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/tddFrameStructure.tdLteUlDlConfig = tdLteConfig0, then 6 consecutive UL slots are configured.**

In this configuration number of resources for PUCCH Format 1 and Format 3 are limited due to DU processing capability limitation.

Short PUCCH would not be applied on FDD and Loki L1 HW as NIDD parameter *pucchSelectMode is restricted to  ‘longPucch’ in this case.*

The long PUCCH and short PUCCH can’t co-exist.

**Note:**

Current Loki capacity is aligned with Loner capacity/subcell/slot (see 5G\_UP\_3263). Further updates are possible in case of any restriction in L1 to support the requested values

 up to 1500 RCU per FDD cell for the cases of 3 cells per L1 Loki instance  with  up to 12 FDM UEs on PDSCH per cell (5G\_UP\_3192 [in 22R1 version])

 up to 750 RCU per FDD cell for the cases of 6 cells per L1 Loki instance  with  up to 6 FDM UEs on PDSCH per cell (5G\_UP\_3192 [in 22R1 version])

**Note 2: see CP constraints about #SR and #pCSI resources in 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_2856 and 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_2851**

**Note 2: PUCCH capacity numbers for 2 (resp. 4) cells case are covered by and are the same than 3 (resp. 6) cells case.**

When UE pooling is enabled (5G\_UP\_1772\_replaced([11372844](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ud_scPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), refer to ([11373764](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueD98_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)), ([11613695](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FaO-4vwKEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)), ([11610921](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FZ1WR_wKEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) for the number of HARQ-AN resources on F1 and F3 per L1 pool (see 5G\_UP\_2133\_replaced([11381159](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uerB6fvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and per slot.

For the maximum number of multiplexed UEs per PRB for PUCCH format 1, please refer to 5G\_CP\_OTH\_410\_replaced([11599656](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Y3QbdvwOEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

##### 5.3.7.2.4.0-3 Odin FR2-TDD (ID: 11453671)

### 5.3.7.3 PUCCH formats interdependencies

#### 5.3.7.3.1 Short and Long PUCCH formats coexistence

**5.3.7.3.1.0-2**  (ID: `13361645`)

Short and Long PUCCH formats coexistence
Per L1 instance and/or per L1 pool 5G-L1-UL shall support either short or long PUCCH. Mix short and long PUCCH per L1 instance and/or per L1 pool is not supported

NOTE:

Short PUCCH refers to PUCCH format0 and format2

Long PUCCH refers to PUCCH format1 and format3

---

#### 5.3.7.3.2 Long PUCCH formats coexistence within same slot

**5.3.7.3.2.0-2**  (ID: `12727514`)

Long PUCCH formats coexistence within same slot
For FR1-TDD and FR1-FDD 5G-L1-UL shall handle long PUCCH resources of either:

* format1 only or
* format3 only or
* format1 and format3 (FDM).

Each PUCCH resource has its own settings (e.g. pucchFormat, numOfBitsOfUciInformation, numOfPrb, firstSymbol, nANPucch, startPrb, numOfSymbols, timeDomainOcc (format1), initialCyclicShift (format1), etc).

Allocating multiple PUCCH format1 resources in the same symbol and frequency is supported via different initial cyclic shifts.

Allocating multiple PUCCH format3 resources in the same symbol and frequency is not supported.  However long PUCCH resources can be FDMed over the same symbols but on different frequencies.

5G-L1-UL shall send format1 and format3 PUCCH resources in seperate UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD messages.

5G-L1-UL shall aggregate format1 and format3 PUCCH resources in one UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs message.

5G-L1-UL shall receive aggregated multiple UEs per subcell from one  UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message.

5G-L1-UL shall aggregate multiple UEs per subcell and send one UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs message for them.

5G-L1-UL shall aggregate multiple UEs per subcell and send one UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD message for them.

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

#### 5.3.7.3.3 Short PUCCH formats coexistence within same slot

**5.3.7.3.3.0-1**  (ID: `13361644`)

Short PUCCH formats coexistence within same slot
5G-L1-UL can handle within one symbol PUCCH resources of either:

* Format0 only or
* Format2 only or
* Format0 and Format2.

Each PUCCH resource has its own settings (e.g. pucchFormat, numOfBitsOfUciInformation, numOfPrb, firstSymbol, nANPucch, startPrb, numOfSymbols, etc)

Allocating multiple PUCCH format0 resources in the same symbol and frequency is supported via different initial cyclic shifts.

Allocating multiple PUCCH format2 resources in the same symbol and frequency is not supported.  However short PUCCH resources can be FDMed over the same symbols but on different frequencies.

5G-L1-UL shall send format0 and format2 PUCCH resources in seperate UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD messages.

5G-L1-UL shall aggregate format0 and format2 PUCCH resources in one UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs message.

5G-L1-UL shall receive aggregate multiple UEs per subcell from one  UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message.

5G-L1-UL shall aggregate multiple UEs per subcell and send one UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs message for them.

5G-L1-UL shall aggregate multiple UEs per subcell and send one UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD message for them.

---

#### 5.3.7.3.4 UCI shared between PUCCH and PUSCH

**5.3.7.3.4.0-2**  (ID: `13392456`)

UCI shared between PUCCH and PUSCH
5G-L1-UL shall support mix of PUCCH format1, PUCCH format3 and UCI on PUSCH (P-CSI) in the same slot.

[CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2a and FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e. [End CB012115-IA, CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin(BB) for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-FDD-eCPRI 7.2a. [End CB012115-JA, CB012115-LA]

---

### 5.3.7.4 Distribution of PUCCH resources over symbols for short format

**5.3.7.4.0-1**  (ID: `11458950`)

Distribution of PUCCH resources over symbols for short format
Distribution of PUCCH resources over symbols (short formats)

The PUCCH resources can be located in different way between up to 2 symbols: #12 and #13,

e.g. in the case the total number of PUCCH resources is 16 per slot per subcell or L1 instance the resources can be distributed in the following way between the symbols:

* 16 resources in #12 symbol, 0 resources in #13 symbol,
* 0 resources in #12 symbol, 16 resources in #13 symbol,
* 8 resources in #12 symbol, 8 resources in #13 symbol,
* 12 resource in #12 symbol, 4 resources in #13 symbol, etc.

---

### 5.3.7.5 PUCCH capacity with buffered UL

#### 5.3.7.5.1 Buffered UL

##### 5.3.7.5.1.0-1 Buffered UL For TDD, with Buffered UL (see 11372372: Buffered UL Concept ) the available capacity for all supported formats is doubled. If the capacity without Buffered UL is N PUCCH resources per slot, then with Buffered UL the L1 instance shall be able to process N corresponding PUCCH resources in real time and additional N in non-real-time from a buffer. (ID: 11458934)

#### 5.3.7.5.2 RT and NRT processing

**5.3.7.5.2.0-1**  (ID: `11458916`)

RT and NRT processing
RT processing capacity (see [11372372: Buffered UL Concept](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ud8pPfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) ) of all PUCCH formats shall be uniformly distributed among subcells processed in RT, and NRT processing capacity shall be uniformly distributed among subcells processed in NRT.

Example: L1 instance is able to process 2 subcells of type C2 and 16 PUCCH F0 resources in RT. This means that each of the 2 subcells is able to process 8 PUCCH F0 resources.

Note: For TDD and Loner L1 HW with Buffered UL:  
   - the supported PUCCH capacity numbers per L1 HW and per technology provided in ([13360163: PUCCH capacity numbers](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_yoZSIPI-EfC0Z6kKit-MzQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) applies for RT processing.  
   - the scheduling of NRT processing is not expecting within the timing window for UL slots (see 5G\_UP\_1731\_replaced([11372384](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ud8pRfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

---

#### 5.3.7.5.3 PUCCH resources distribution for RT and NRT mode

##### 5.3.7.5.3.0-1 PUCCH resources distribution for RT and NRT mode L1-SW shall assign resources in RT or NRT based on 5G-L2-PS selection. (ID: 11453842)

#### 5.3.7.5.4 Frequency Domain Multiplexing with other channels

##### 5.3.7.5.4.0-1 Frequency Domain Multiplexing with other channels L1-SW shall process consistently FDMd channels in the same symbol/subcell, either all RT or all NRT. (ID: 11454840)
